BoostAPR: Boosting Automated Program Repair via Execution-Grounded Reinforcement Learning with Dual Reward Models
Authors: Yuanhao Li, Hongbo Wang, Xiaotang Shang, Xunzhu Tang, Yiming Cao, Xuhong Chen
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-09T19:31:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T16:38:24+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 2 figures. Accepted at ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for program repair is hindered by sparse execution feedback and coarse sequence-level rewards that obscure which edits actually fix bugs. We present BoostAPR, a three-stage framework addressing these challenges: (1) supervised fine-tuning on execution-verified demonstrations with reasoning traces, (2) training dual reward models--a sequence-level assessor and a line-level credit allocator--from execution outcomes, and (3) PPO optimization where the line-level model redistributes rewards to critical edit regions. This line-level credit assignment operates at an intermediate granularity naturally suited to code changes. Trained on SWE-Gym and evaluated on four benchmarks, BoostAPR achieves 40.7% on SWE-bench Verified (+22.9pp over base model), 24.8% on Defects4J (Python-to-Java transfer), 84.5% on HumanEval-Java, and 95.0% on QuixBugs, achieving competitive results among open-source models with strong cross-language generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BoostAPR：通过执行驱动的强化学习与双奖励模型提升自动程序修复
强化学习在程序修复中面临执行反馈稀疏和粗粒度序列级奖励难以定位修复编辑的挑战。我们提出BoostAPR，一个三阶段框架应对这些问题：（1）基于执行验证的演示与推理轨迹进行监督微调，（2）从执行结果训练双奖励模型——序列级评估器与行级信用分配器，（3）PPO优化中行级模型将奖励重新分配至关键编辑区域。这种行级信用分配以自然适配代码变更的中间粒度运作。在SWE-Gym上训练并在四个基准上评估，BoostAPR在SWE-bench Verified上达到40.7%（较基础模型提升22.9个百分点），在Defects4J（Python到Java迁移）上达24.8%，在HumanEval-Java上达84.5%，在QuixBugs上达95.0%，在开源模型中取得具有竞争力的结果并展现强跨语言泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
Automated program repair with reinforcement learning suffers from sparse execution feedback and coarse sequence-level rewards that fail to pinpoint which edits fix bugs. To address this, BoostAPR introduces a three-stage framework: first, supervised fine-tuning on execution-verified demonstrations with reasoning traces; second, training dual reward models including a sequence-level assessor and a line-level credit allocator derived from execution outcomes; and third, PPO optimization where the line-level model redistributes rewards to critical edit regions at an intermediate granularity suited to code changes. Evaluated on SWE-bench Verified, Defects4J, HumanEval-Java, and QuixBugs, BoostAPR achieves 40.7% (+22.9pp over base model), 24.8% (Python-to-Java transfer), 84.5%, and 95.0% respectively, demonstrating competitive results among open-source models with strong cross-language generalization.
基于强化学习的程序修复面临执行反馈稀疏和序列级奖励粗粒度的问题，难以定位具体修复编辑。为此，BoostAPR提出三阶段框架：首先在含推理轨迹的执行验证演示上进行监督微调；其次训练双奖励模型，包括序列级评估器和基于执行结果的行级信用分配器；最后通过PPO优化，由行级模型将奖励重新分配到关键编辑区域，其粒度天然适配代码变更。在SWE-bench Verified、Defects4J、HumanEval-Java和QuixBugs上评估，BoostAPR分别达到40.7%（较基模型提升22.9个百分点）、24.8%（Python到Java迁移）、84.5%和95.0%，在开源模型中取得具有竞争力的结果，并展现出强大的跨语言泛化能力。
Tight Sample Complexity Bounds for Entropic Best Policy Identification
Authors: Amer Essakine, Claire Vernade
First: 2026-05-13T16:02:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T16:02:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study best-policy identification for finite-horizon risk-sensitive reinforcement learning under the entropic risk measure. Recent work established a constant gap in the exponential horizon dependence between lower and upper bounds on the number of samples required to identify an approximately optimal policy. Precisely, known lower bounds scale in $Ω(e^{|β| H})$ where $H$ is the horizon of the MDP, while the state-of-the-art upper bound achieves at best $O(e^{2|β| H})$ (arXiv:2506.00286v2) using a generative model. We show that this extra exponential factor can be traced to overly loose concentration control for exponential utilities. To close this open gap, we revisit the analysis of this problem through a forward-model based algorithm building on KL-based exploration bonuses that we adapt to the entropic criterion. The improvement we get is due to two main novel technical innovations. We leverage the smoothness properties of the exponential utility to derive sharper concentration bounds, and we propose a new stopping rule that exploits further this tightness to obtain a sample complexity that matches the lower bound.
中文标题/摘要
标题：熵最优策略识别的紧样本复杂度界
我们研究了熵风险度量下有限时域风险敏感强化学习的最优策略识别问题。近期工作揭示了在识别近似最优策略所需样本数量的下界与上界之间存在指数级时域依赖的常数差距。具体而言，已知下界以$Ω(e^{|β| H})$标度（其中$H$为MDP的时域长度），而当前最优上界在使用生成模型时仅能达到$O(e^{2|β| H})$（arXiv:2506.00286v2）。我们证明这一额外指数因子源于对指数型效用的过度宽松的集中性控制。为弥合这一开放差距，我们重新审视该问题的分析，提出一种基于前向模型的算法，该算法构建于适用于熵准则的KL探索奖励之上。我们的改进源于两项主要技术创新：利用指数型效用的光滑性导出更紧的集中性界，并提出一种新的停止规则以进一步利用这种紧性，从而获得与下界匹配的样本复杂度。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the sample complexity gap in best-policy identification for finite-horizon risk-sensitive reinforcement learning under the entropic risk measure, where existing lower bounds scale as Ω(e^{|β|H}) and upper bounds as O(e^{2|β|H}). The authors identify that the extra exponential factor arises from overly loose concentration control for exponential utilities. To close this gap, they propose a forward-model based algorithm with KL-based exploration bonuses adapted to the entropic criterion, introducing two key innovations: leveraging smoothness properties of the exponential utility for sharper concentration bounds, and a new stopping rule that exploits this tightness. The resulting sample complexity matches the lower bound, resolving the open problem.
本文研究了有限时域风险敏感强化学习在熵风险度量下的最优策略识别问题，其中现有样本复杂度下界为Ω(e^{|β|H})，上界为O(e^{2|β|H})，存在指数级差距。作者指出额外指数因子源于对指数效用函数的浓度控制过于宽松。为弥合这一差距，他们提出了一种基于前向模型的算法，结合针对熵准则调整的KL探索奖励，并引入两项创新：利用指数效用函数的平滑性推导更紧的浓度界，以及设计新的停止规则以充分利用这种紧性。最终样本复杂度与下界匹配，解决了这一开放问题。
Block-R1: Rethinking the Role of Block Size in Multi-domain Reinforcement Learning for Diffusion Large Language Models
Authors: Yan Jiang, Ruihong Qiu, Zi Huang
First: 2026-05-12T08:09:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:38:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recently, reinforcement learning (RL) has been widely applied during post-training for diffusion large language models (dLLMs) to enhance reasoning with block-wise semi-autoregressive generation. Block size has therefore become a vital factor in dLLMs, since it determines the parallel decoding granularity and affects the rollout trajectories during RL optimisation, e.g., GRPO. Instead of investigating the effect of block size during inference on individual domains, this paper studies block size from a domain conflict perspective for dLLM RL post-training in multi-domain scenarios. The main contributions are: (1) a formulation of domain block size conflict in multi-domain RL for dLLMs, which will largely affect the post-training effectiveness for rollout-based RL methods; (2) a novel dataset, Block-R1-41K is constructed with a best-improved training block size for each sample, which also induces a Block Size Conflict Score to quantitatively measure the domain conflict; (3) a new benchmark, Block-R1, for flexible RL post-training for dLLMs in both single and cross domain; and (4) a simple yet powerful cross-domain post-training method with sample-level best-improved training block sizes. Extensive experiments on 13 distinct datasets, 7 latest RL algorithms and diverse dLLM backbones are comprehensively covered in Block-R1. The benchmark is open-sourced at https://github.com/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1 with the dataset released at https://huggingface.co/datasets/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1-41K.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Block-R1：重新思考块大小在扩散大语言模型多域强化学习中的作用
近期，强化学习（RL）被广泛应用于扩散大语言模型（dLLMs）的后训练阶段，通过块级半自回归生成来增强推理能力。块大小因此成为dLLMs的关键因素，因为它决定了并行解码的粒度，并影响RL优化（如GRPO）中的展开轨迹。本文并非研究推理阶段块大小对单个领域的影响，而是从领域冲突的角度探讨dLLM RL后训练在多域场景中的块大小问题。主要贡献包括：（1）提出了dLLMs多域RL中的领域块大小冲突公式，该冲突将显著影响基于展开的RL方法的后训练效果；（2）构建了新型数据集Block-R1-41K，为每个样本提供最佳改进的训练块大小，并引入块大小冲突分数以定量衡量领域冲突；（3）提出了新基准Block-R1，支持dLLMs在单域和跨域中的灵活RL后训练；（4）提出了一种简单而强大的跨域后训练方法，采用样本级最佳改进的训练块大小。Block-R1在13个不同数据集、7种最新RL算法和多种dLLM骨干网络上进行了全面实验。该基准已在https://github.com/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1开源，数据集发布于https://huggingface.co/datasets/YanJiangJerry/Block-R1-41K。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the role of block size in reinforcement learning (RL) post-training for diffusion large language models (dLLMs) in multi-domain scenarios, motivated by the observation that block size determines parallel decoding granularity and affects rollout trajectories during RL optimization. The authors identify a domain block size conflict that undermines post-training effectiveness and propose a solution: they construct the Block-R1-41K dataset with sample-level best-improved training block sizes, introduce a Block Size Conflict Score to quantify domain conflict, and develop a cross-domain post-training method that uses these optimal block sizes. Extensive experiments across 13 datasets, 7 RL algorithms, and diverse dLLM backbones demonstrate that their approach effectively resolves domain conflicts and improves performance in both single and cross-domain settings.
本文研究了在扩散大语言模型（dLLM）的强化学习（RL）后训练中，块大小在多领域场景下的作用，其动机在于块大小决定了并行解码粒度并影响RL优化（如GRPO）中的轨迹生成。作者发现存在领域块大小冲突，这会削弱后训练效果，并提出解决方案：构建了包含样本级最佳改进训练块大小的Block-R1-41K数据集，引入块大小冲突分数以量化领域冲突，并开发了一种使用这些最优块大小的跨领域后训练方法。在13个数据集、7种最新RL算法和多种dLLM骨干网络上的大量实验表明，该方法有效解决了领域冲突，并在单领域和跨领域设置中均提升了性能。
Decoupling Exploration and Policy Optimization: Uncertainty Guided Tree Search for Hard Exploration
Authors: Zakaria Mhammedi, James Cohan
First: 2026-03-23T17:56:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:33:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The process of discovery requires active exploration -- the act of collecting new and informative data. However, efficient autonomous exploration remains a major unsolved problem. The dominant paradigm addresses this challenge by using Reinforcement Learning (RL) to train agents with intrinsic motivation, maximizing a composite objective of extrinsic and intrinsic rewards. We suggest that this approach incurs unnecessary overhead: while policy optimization is necessary for precise task execution, employing such machinery solely to expand state coverage may be inefficient. In this paper, we propose a new approach that explicitly decouples exploration from policy optimization and bypasses RL entirely during the exploration phase. Our method uses a tree-search strategy inspired by the Go-With-The-Winner algorithm, paired with a measure of uncertainty to systematically drive exploration. By removing the overhead of policy optimization, our approach explores an order of magnitude more efficiently than standard intrinsic motivation baselines on hard exploration benchmarks. Further, we demonstrate that the trajectories discovered during exploration can be distilled into deployable policies using existing supervised backward learning algorithms, achieving state-of-the-art performance by a wide margin on Montezuma's Revenge, Pitfall!, and Venture without relying on domain-specific knowledge. Finally, we demonstrate the generality of our framework in high-dimensional continuous action spaces by solving the MuJoCo Adroit dexterous manipulation and AntMaze tasks in a sparse-reward setting, directly from image observations and without expert demonstrations or offline datasets. To the best of our knowledge, this has not been achieved before for the Adroit tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解耦探索与策略优化：面向困难探索的不确定性引导树搜索
发现过程需要主动探索——即收集新颖且信息丰富的数据。然而，高效的自主探索仍是一个未解决的主要问题。主流范式通过使用强化学习训练具有内在动机的智能体来应对这一挑战，最大化外在奖励与内在奖励的复合目标。我们认为这种方法带来了不必要的开销：虽然策略优化对于精确任务执行是必要的，但仅为了扩展状态覆盖而使用此类机制可能效率低下。本文提出了一种新方法，明确将探索与策略优化解耦，并在探索阶段完全绕过强化学习。我们的方法采用受“赢家通吃”算法启发的树搜索策略，结合不确定性度量来系统性地驱动探索。通过消除策略优化的开销，我们的方法在困难探索基准测试中的探索效率比标准内在动机基线高出一个数量级。此外，我们证明探索过程中发现的轨迹可以通过现有的监督式反向学习算法蒸馏为可部署策略，在《蒙特祖玛的复仇》、《陷阱！》和《冒险》游戏中无需领域特定知识即实现了大幅领先的最优性能。最后，我们通过在高维连续动作空间中解决稀疏奖励设置下的MuJoCo Adroit灵巧操作和AntMaze任务，直接基于图像观测且无需专家演示或离线数据集，展示了框架的通用性。据我们所知，这在Adroit任务中此前尚未实现。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency of using reinforcement learning for exploration by proposing a method that decouples exploration from policy optimization. The approach employs a tree-search strategy based on the Go-With-The-Winner algorithm, guided by uncertainty measures to systematically explore without the overhead of policy optimization. Experimental results show that this method explores an order of magnitude more efficiently than intrinsic motivation baselines on hard exploration benchmarks, achieves state-of-the-art performance on Montezuma's Revenge, Pitfall!, and Venture without domain-specific knowledge, and solves MuJoCo Adroit and AntMaze tasks from image observations in sparse-reward settings, a first for Adroit tasks.
本文针对强化学习中探索效率低下的问题，提出了一种将探索与策略优化解耦的方法。该方法采用基于Go-With-The-Winner算法的树搜索策略，结合不确定性度量来系统性地驱动探索，避免了策略优化的额外开销。实验结果表明，该方法在困难探索基准上比内在动机基线方法高效一个数量级，在Montezuma's Revenge、Pitfall!和Venture上无需领域知识即达到最先进性能，并在稀疏奖励设置下从图像观测直接解决了MuJoCo Adroit和AntMaze任务，其中Adroit任务为首次实现。
Multi-Objective and Mixed-Reward Reinforcement Learning via Reward-Decorrelated Policy Optimization
Authors: Yang Bai, Kaiyuan Liu, Ziyuan Zhuang, Jiahong Zhou, Rongxiang Weng, Xin Chen, Jingang Wang, Xunliang Cai
First: 2026-05-13T15:05:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:05:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Complex reinforcement learning environments frequently employ multi-task and mixed-reward formulations. In these settings, heterogeneous reward distributions and correlated reward dimensions often destabilize the construction of scalar advantages. To address these challenges, we propose Reward-Decorrelated Policy Optimization (RDPO), a reward-processing method designed to explicitly target both failure modes. RDPO first utilizes Magnitude-Aware Quantile normalization to stabilize prompt-level advantage allocation across binary, fractional, and continuous rewards. It then applies Mahalanobis whitening within each active reward subspace to mitigate correlation redundancy prior to aggregation. When applied during the post-training of LongCat-Flash, RDPO enhances instruction following, writing quality, and robustness to hard prompts while remaining broadly competitive on reasoning and coding evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于奖励去相关的多目标与混合奖励强化学习策略优化
复杂强化学习环境常采用多任务和混合奖励设定。在此类场景中，异质奖励分布与相关奖励维度常破坏标量优势函数的稳定性。为应对这些挑战，我们提出奖励去相关策略优化（RDPO），一种专门针对这两种失效模式的奖励处理方法。RDPO首先利用幅度感知分位数归一化，在二元、分数和连续奖励中稳定提示级优势分配；随后在每个活跃奖励子空间内应用马氏白化处理，以在聚合前缓解相关性冗余。将RDPO应用于LongCat-Flash的后训练阶段后，模型在指令遵循、写作质量及困难提示鲁棒性方面得到提升，同时在推理与代码评估任务中保持广泛竞争力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the instability caused by heterogeneous reward distributions and correlated reward dimensions in multi-objective and mixed-reward reinforcement learning. The authors propose Reward-Decorrelated Policy Optimization (RDPO), which uses Magnitude-Aware Quantile normalization to stabilize advantage allocation across diverse reward types and Mahalanobis whitening to reduce correlation redundancy within reward subspaces. Applied to post-training of LongCat-Flash, RDPO improves instruction following, writing quality, and robustness to hard prompts while maintaining competitive performance on reasoning and coding tasks.
该论文针对多目标和混合奖励强化学习中因奖励分布异质和维度相关导致的训练不稳定问题，提出了奖励去相关策略优化方法。该方法通过幅度感知分位数归一化稳定不同奖励类型下的优势分配，并利用马氏白化减少奖励子空间内的相关性冗余。在LongCat-Flash模型的后训练中应用该方法，提升了指令遵循、写作质量和对困难提示的鲁棒性，同时在推理和编码任务上保持竞争力。
Achieving $ε^{-2}$ Sample Complexity for Single-Loop Actor-Critic under Minimal Assumptions
Authors: Ishaq Hamza, Zaiwei Chen
First: 2026-05-13T15:04:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:04:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we establish last-iterate convergence rates for off-policy actor--critic methods in reinforcement learning. In particular, under a single-loop, single-timescale implementation and a broad class of policy updates, including approximate policy iteration and natural policy gradient methods, we prove the first $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity guarantee for finding an $ε$-optimal policy under minimal assumptions, namely, the existence of a policy that induces an irreducible Markov chain. This stands in stark contrast to the existing literature, where an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity is achieved only through nested-loop updates and/or under strong, algorithm-dependent assumptions on the policies, such as uniform mixing and uniform exploration. Technically, to address the challenges posed by the coupled update equations arising from the single-loop implementation, as well as the potentially unbounded iterates induced by off-policy learning, our analysis is based on a coupled Lyapunov drift framework. Specifically, we establish a geometric convergence rate for the actor and an $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/T)$ convergence rate for the critic, and combine the two Lyapunov drift inequalities through a cross-domination property. We believe this analytical framework is of independent interest and may be applicable to other coupled iterative algorithms with unbounded
中文标题/摘要
标题：在最小假设下实现单循环演员-评论家的 $ε^{-2}$ 样本复杂度
本文建立了强化学习中离策略演员-评论家方法的最后迭代收敛速率。特别地，在单循环、单时间尺度实现以及包括近似策略迭代和自然策略梯度方法在内的广泛策略更新类别下，我们证明了在最小假设（即存在一个能诱导不可约马尔可夫链的策略）下，找到 $ε$-最优策略的首个 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 样本复杂度保证。这与现有文献形成鲜明对比，现有文献中 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-2})$ 样本复杂度仅通过嵌套循环更新和/或在强算法依赖假设（如均匀混合和均匀探索）下实现。技术上，为应对单循环实现带来的耦合更新方程以及离策略学习可能导致的无限迭代，我们的分析基于耦合李雅普诺夫漂移框架。具体地，我们建立了演员的几何收敛速率和评论家的 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/T)$ 收敛速率，并通过交叉支配性质结合两个李雅普诺夫漂移不等式。我们相信这一分析框架具有独立意义，并可能适用于其他具有无界迭代的耦合迭代算法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the sample complexity of off-policy actor-critic methods in reinforcement learning, motivated by the need for efficient single-loop algorithms under minimal assumptions. The authors propose a single-loop, single-timescale implementation compatible with policy updates like approximate policy iteration and natural policy gradient. They prove a sample complexity of Õ(ε⁻²) for finding an ε-optimal policy, requiring only the existence of a policy inducing an irreducible Markov chain, unlike prior work needing nested loops or strong assumptions like uniform mixing. The analysis uses a coupled Lyapunov drift framework, establishing geometric convergence for the actor and Õ(1/T) convergence for the critic, with a cross-domination property linking them. Main results show this is the first such guarantee under minimal assumptions, with the framework potentially applicable to other coupled iterative algorithms.
本文针对强化学习中离策略演员-评论家方法的样本复杂度问题，旨在在最小假设下实现高效的单循环算法。作者提出了一种单循环、单时间尺度的实现，兼容近似策略迭代和自然策略梯度等策略更新方法。他们证明了在仅需存在一个能诱导不可约马尔可夫链的策略的最小假设下，找到ε-最优策略的样本复杂度为Õ(ε⁻²)，这与现有文献中需要嵌套循环或均匀混合等强假设的方法形成鲜明对比。分析采用耦合李雅普诺夫漂移框架，建立了演员的几何收敛率和评论家的Õ(1/T)收敛率，并通过交叉支配性质将两者结合。主要结果表明这是首个在最小假设下实现该保证的方法，该分析框架可能适用于其他耦合迭代算法。
CO-MAP: A Reinforcement Learning Approach to the Qubit Allocation Problem
Authors: Ankit Kulshrestha, Xiaoyuan Liu
Venue: NeurIPS
First: 2026-05-13T15:04:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T15:04:09+00:00
Comments: Under review at NeurIPS'26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A quantum compiler is a critical piece in the quantum computing pipeline since it allows an abstract quantum circuit to be run on a physical quantum computer. One extremely important subproblem in quantum compilation is the generation of a logical to physical qubit mapping. Typically in quantum compilers this step is either implemented as a random or a heuristic based assignment that aims to minimize additional (SWAP) gate overhead in the quantum circuit. In this paper, we present an alternative approach to solving the qubit mapping problem. Specifically, we formulate the qubit mapping problem with a combinatorial optimization (CO) objective. We then present a method to find a solution to the CO problem by training a reinforcement learning (RL) policy. We also propose a local search based post-processing algorithm to further reduce the overhead. Our results show a dramatic improvement over conventional techniques in reducing the number of SWAPs. On different real world datasets like MQTBench and Queko circuits, our trained policy achieves a \textbf{65-85\%} reduction in SWAP overhead when compared to existing quantum compilers.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the qubit allocation problem in quantum compilation, which maps logical qubits to physical qubits to minimize SWAP gate overhead. The authors formulate this as a combinatorial optimization problem and propose CO-MAP, a reinforcement learning approach to learn a policy for finding optimal mappings. A local search post-processing step further reduces overhead. Experiments on MQTBench and Queko circuits show a 65-85% reduction in SWAP overhead compared to existing quantum compilers, demonstrating significant improvement over heuristic and random baselines.
该论文针对量子编译中的量子比特分配问题，旨在最小化SWAP门开销。作者将问题形式化为组合优化目标，并提出CO-MAP方法，通过训练强化学习策略来寻找最优映射，并辅以局部搜索后处理进一步降低开销。在MQTBench和Queko等真实数据集上的实验表明，与现有量子编译器相比，该方法将SWAP开销减少了65-85%，显著优于启发式和随机基线方法。
AP-BMM: Approximating Capability-Cost Pareto Sets of LLMs via Asynchronous Prior-Guided Bayesian Model Merging
Authors: Kesheng Chen, Yamin Hu, Zhenqian Zhu, Yiya Diao, Wenjian Luo
First: 2025-12-10T15:32:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T14:51:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Serving Large Language Models (LLMs) often requires choosing between stronger reasoning and lower inference cost. Model merging offers a practical way to build several models between a reasoning-oriented model and a cheaper base model, but common model-level merging methods usually control this trade-off with only one or two global knobs. We study this setting as a multi-objective optimization problem: instead of producing one merged model, the goal is to find a set of merged models that cover different accuracy--token-cost preferences. Layer-wise merging is more flexible because it can assign different merge weights to different Transformer layers. However, it introduces two practical challenges. First, the layer-wise search space is large, and existing methods often search it without using helpful signals from the source models. Second, LLM evaluations can take very different amounts of time, so synchronous batch optimization wastes GPU time while waiting for slow evaluations. We propose Asynchronous Prior-Guided Bayesian Model Merging (AP-BMM). AP-BMM uses parameter and reasoning-activation differences between the source models to suggest which layers should matter early in the search. It also uses an asynchronous Bayesian optimization loop that accounts for candidate models already being evaluated. A lightweight reranking step further spreads candidates across the accuracy--cost trade-off. Under fixed evaluation budgets, AP-BMM achieves stronger Pareto-set quality and broader trade-off coverage than synchronous layer-wise baselines and representative model-level merging baselines. Compared with the synchronous Bayesian baseline, it also reduces wall-clock time by improving GPU utilization. Code: https://github.com/MiLab-HITSZ/AP-BMM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AP-BMM：通过异步先验引导的贝叶斯模型合并近似LLM的能力-成本帕累托集
服务大型语言模型（LLM）时，通常需要在更强的推理能力和更低的推理成本之间做出选择。模型合并提供了一种实用方法，可以在面向推理的模型和更便宜的基础模型之间构建多个模型，但常见的模型级合并方法通常仅通过一两个全局旋钮来控制这种权衡。我们将此设置作为多目标优化问题进行研究：目标不是生成一个合并模型，而是找到一组覆盖不同准确率-令牌成本偏好的合并模型。逐层合并更为灵活，因为它可以为不同的Transformer层分配不同的合并权重。然而，这带来了两个实际挑战。首先，逐层搜索空间很大，现有方法在搜索时往往未利用源模型中的有用信号。其次，LLM评估所需时间差异很大，因此同步批量优化在等待慢速评估时会浪费GPU时间。我们提出了异步先验引导的贝叶斯模型合并（AP-BMM）。AP-BMM利用源模型之间的参数和推理激活差异，在搜索早期建议哪些层应被关注。它还使用异步贝叶斯优化循环，考虑已在评估中的候选模型。一个轻量级的重排序步骤进一步将候选模型分散到准确率-成本权衡曲线上。在固定评估预算下，AP-BMM相比同步逐层基线和代表性模型级合并基线，实现了更强的帕累托集质量和更广的权衡覆盖范围。与同步贝叶斯基线相比，它还通过提高GPU利用率减少了挂钟时间。 代码：https://github.com/MiLab-HITSZ/AP-BMM。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of balancing reasoning capability and inference cost in serving Large Language Models (LLMs) by framing model merging as a multi-objective optimization problem to produce a Pareto set of merged models covering various accuracy-token-cost preferences. The proposed method, Asynchronous Prior-Guided Bayesian Model Merging (AP-BMM), leverages parameter and reasoning-activation differences between source models to guide layer-wise search and employs an asynchronous Bayesian optimization loop to handle varying evaluation times, followed by a lightweight reranking step. Experimental results show that AP-BMM achieves stronger Pareto-set quality and broader trade-off coverage than synchronous layer-wise and model-level baselines under fixed evaluation budgets, while also reducing wall-clock time through improved GPU utilization.
该论文针对服务大型语言模型时推理能力与推理成本之间的权衡问题，将模型合并视为多目标优化问题，旨在生成覆盖不同准确率-令牌成本偏好的帕累托最优模型集合。提出的异步先验引导贝叶斯模型合并方法（AP-BMM）利用源模型之间的参数和推理激活差异来指导逐层搜索，并采用异步贝叶斯优化循环处理不同评估时间，最后通过轻量级重排序步骤进一步扩展权衡覆盖范围。实验结果表明，在固定评估预算下，AP-BMM在帕累托集质量和权衡覆盖广度上均优于同步逐层和模型级基线方法，同时通过提高GPU利用率减少了实际运行时间。
TiCo: Time-Controllable Spoken Dialogue Model
Authors: Kai-Wei Chang, Wei-Chih Chen, En-Pei Hu, Hung-yi Lee, James Glass
First: 2026-03-23T17:51:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T14:33:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce TiCo, a time-controllable spoken dialogue model (SDM) that follows time-constrained instructions (e.g., "Please generate a response lasting about 15 seconds") and generates spoken responses with controllable duration. This capability is valuable for real-world spoken language systems such as voice assistants and interactive agents, where controlling response duration can improve interaction quality. However, despite their strong ability to generate natural spoken responses, existing models lack time awareness and struggle to follow duration-related instructions. To systematically evaluate this, we introduce TiCo-Bench, the first benchmark for time-controllable instruction following in SDMs, on which existing open-source and commercial models frequently fail to satisfy explicit time constraints. TiCo addresses this limitation by enabling an SDM to estimate elapsed speaking time during generation through Spoken Time Markers (STM) (e.g., <10.6 seconds>). These markers help the model maintain awareness of time and adjust the remaining content to meet the target duration. TiCo is post-trained efficiently without question-answer paired data, relying on self-generation and reinforcement learning with verifiable reward. Experimental results show that TiCo reduces duration error by 2.7x over its backbone and 1.6x over the strongest baseline, while preserving response quality.
Summary / 总结
TiCo is a time-controllable spoken dialogue model designed to generate spoken responses with precise duration control, addressing the lack of time awareness in existing models. The method introduces Spoken Time Markers (STM) that estimate elapsed speaking time during generation, enabling the model to adjust content to meet target durations, and is post-trained efficiently using self-generation and reinforcement learning without paired data. Experimental results demonstrate that TiCo reduces duration error by 2.7 times compared to its backbone and 1.6 times over the strongest baseline, while maintaining response quality.
TiCo是一种时间可控的口语对话模型，旨在生成具有精确时长控制的语音回复，解决了现有模型缺乏时间感知的问题。该方法引入了口语时间标记（STM），在生成过程中估计已用说话时间，使模型能够调整内容以达到目标时长，并通过自生成和强化学习进行高效后训练，无需配对数据。实验结果表明，TiCo将时长误差相比其基础模型降低了2.7倍，相比最强基线降低了1.6倍，同时保持了回复质量。
Learning Local Constraints for Reinforcement-Learned Content Generators
Authors: Debosmita Bhaumik, Julian Togelius, Georgios N. Yannakakis, Ahmed Khalifa
First: 2026-05-13T14:07:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T14:07:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Constraint-based game content generators that learn local constraints from existing content, such as Wave Function Collapse (WFC), can generate visually satisfying game levels but face challenges in guaranteeing global properties, such as playability. On the other hand, reinforcement-learning trained generators can guarantee global properties -- because such properties can easily be included in reward functions -- but the results can be visually dissatisfying. In this paper, we explore ways to combine these methods. Specifically, we constrain the action space of a PCGRL generator with constraints learned by WFC, effectively allowing the PCGRL generator to achieve global properties while forced to adhere to local constraints. To better analyze how this hybrid content generation method operates, we vary the number and type of inputs, and we test whether to randomly collapse the starting state and exclude rare patterns. While the method is sensitive to hyperparameter tuning, the best of our trained generators produce visually satisfying and playable puzzle-platform game levels -- such as Lode Runner levels -- with desired global properties.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为强化学习内容生成器学习局部约束
基于约束的游戏内容生成器（如波函数坍缩算法）通过从现有内容中学习局部约束，能够生成视觉上令人满意的游戏关卡，但在保证全局属性（如可玩性）方面面临挑战。另一方面，强化学习训练的内容生成器可以保证全局属性——因为此类属性易于纳入奖励函数——但生成结果可能在视觉上不尽如人意。本文探索了结合这两种方法的方式。具体而言，我们利用WFC学习到的约束来限制PCGRL生成器的动作空间，从而有效使PCGRL生成器在强制遵守局部约束的同时实现全局属性。为更深入分析这种混合内容生成方法的运作机制，我们改变了输入的数量和类型，并测试了是否随机坍缩初始状态及排除罕见模式。尽管该方法对超参数调优敏感，但训练出的最佳生成器能够生成视觉上令人满意且可玩的解谜平台游戏关卡（如《淘金者》关卡），并具备所需的全局属性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of combining local constraint learning with reinforcement learning for game content generation, where Wave Function Collapse (WFC) ensures visual quality but fails to guarantee global properties like playability, while reinforcement-learning-trained generators can achieve global properties via reward functions but often produce visually dissatisfying results. The proposed method constrains the action space of a PCGRL generator using constraints learned by WFC, forcing adherence to local constraints while pursuing global objectives. Experiments on Lode Runner levels show that, despite sensitivity to hyperparameter tuning, the best hybrid generators produce both visually satisfying and playable levels with desired global properties.
该论文针对游戏内容生成中局部约束学习与强化学习结合的问题展开研究，其中波函数坍缩（WFC）能保证视觉质量但难以确保可玩性等全局属性，而强化学习训练生成器可通过奖励函数实现全局属性但结果常缺乏视觉满意度。提出的方法通过WFC学习的约束限制PCGRL生成器的动作空间，使其在追求全局目标时强制遵守局部约束。在Lode Runner关卡上的实验表明，尽管对超参数调优敏感，最佳混合生成器能生成兼具视觉满意度和可玩性且具备所需全局属性的关卡。
Self-Supervised On-Policy Reinforcement Learning via Contrastive Proximal Policy Optimisation
Authors: Asim Osman, Sasha Abramowitz, Mark Bergh, Ulrich Armel Mbou Sob, Ruan John de Kock, Omayma Mahjoub, Oussama Hidaoui, Noah De Nicola, Arnol Manuel Fokam, Felix Chalumeau, Daniel Rajaonarivonivelomanantsoa, Siddarth Singh, Refiloe Shabe, Juan Claude Formanek, Simon Verster Du Toit, Arnu Pretorius
First: 2026-05-13T13:58:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T13:58:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Contrastive reinforcement learning (CRL) learns goal-conditioned Q-values through a contrastive objective over state-action and goal representations, removing the need for hand-crafted reward functions. Despite impressive success in achieving viable self-supervised learning in RL, all existing CRL algorithms rely on off-policy optimisation and are mostly constrained to continuous action spaces, with little research invested in discrete environments. This leaves CRL disconnected from widely used and effective, modern on-policy training pipelines adopted across both single-agent and multi-agent RL in continuous and discrete environments. To establish a first connection, we introduce Contrastive Proximal Policy Optimisation (CPPO). CPPO is an on-policy contrastive RL algorithm that derives policy advantages directly from contrastive Q-values and optimises them via the standard PPO objective, without requiring a reward function or a replay buffer. We evaluate CPPO across continuous and discrete, single-agent and cooperative multi-agent tasks. Whilst the existence of an on-policy approach is inherently useful, we observe that \textbf{CPPO not only significantly outperforms the previous CRL baselines in 14 out of 18 tasks, but also matches or exceeds PPO's performance, which uses hand-crafted dense rewards, in 12 out of the 18 tasks tested.}
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于对比近端策略优化的自监督在策略强化学习
对比强化学习（CRL）通过状态-动作与目标表征的对比目标学习目标条件Q值，无需手工设计奖励函数。尽管在实现可行的自监督强化学习方面取得了显著成功，但现有CRL算法均依赖离策略优化，且主要局限于连续动作空间，在离散环境中的研究甚少。这使得CRL与当前在连续和离散环境中单智能体与多智能体强化学习中广泛采用的高效在策略训练流程脱节。为建立初步联系，我们提出对比近端策略优化（CPPO）。CPPO是一种在策略对比强化学习算法，直接从对比Q值推导策略优势，并通过标准PPO目标进行优化，无需奖励函数或经验回放缓冲区。我们在连续/离散、单智能体/协作多智能体任务中评估CPPO。尽管在策略方法本身具有实用价值，但我们观察到：**CPPO不仅在18个任务中的14个显著优于先前CRL基线，而且在18个测试任务中的12个达到或超过了使用手工密集奖励的PPO性能。**
Summary / 总结
Contrastive reinforcement learning (CRL) learns goal-conditioned Q-values without hand-crafted rewards but has been limited to off-policy methods and continuous action spaces. To bridge this gap, the authors propose Contrastive Proximal Policy Optimisation (CPPO), an on-policy CRL algorithm that derives policy advantages from contrastive Q-values and optimizes them via the standard PPO objective, eliminating the need for reward functions or replay buffers. Evaluated across continuous and discrete, single-agent and cooperative multi-agent tasks, CPPO significantly outperforms previous CRL baselines in 14 out of 18 tasks and matches or exceeds PPO with dense rewards in 12 out of 18 tasks.
对比强化学习通过对比目标学习状态-动作与目标的表征来获取目标条件Q值，无需手工设计奖励函数，但现有方法局限于离策略优化和连续动作空间。为建立连接，作者提出对比近端策略优化，这是一种在策略对比强化学习算法，直接从对比Q值推导策略优势，并通过标准PPO目标进行优化，无需奖励函数或经验回放缓冲区。在连续与离散、单智能体与协作多智能体任务上的评估显示，CPPO在18个任务中的14个上显著优于先前对比强化学习基线，并在12个任务中达到或超过使用手工密集奖励的PPO性能。
Temper and Tilt Lead to SLOP: Reward Hacking Mitigation with Inference-Time Alignment
Authors: Ye Wang, Jing Liu, Toshiaki Koike-Akino
First: 2026-05-13T13:47:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T13:47:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inference-time alignment techniques offer a lightweight alternative or complement to costly reinforcement learning, while enabling continual adaptation as alignment objectives and reward targets evolve. Existing theoretical analyses justify these methods as approximations to sampling from distributions optimally tilted toward a given reward model. We extend these techniques by introducing reference-model temperature adjustment, which leads to further generalization of inference-time alignment to ensembles of generative reward models combined as a sharpened logarithmic opinion pool (SLOP). To mitigate reward hacking, we propose an algorithm for calibrating SLOP weight parameters and experimentally demonstrate that it improves robustness while preserving alignment performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：温度与倾斜导致SLOP：基于推理时对齐的奖励破解缓解方法
推理时对齐技术为昂贵的强化学习提供了一种轻量级替代或补充方案，同时能够随着对齐目标和奖励目标的演变实现持续适应。现有理论分析将这些方法视为对给定奖励模型最优倾斜分布的采样近似。我们通过引入参考模型温度调整来扩展这些技术，从而进一步将推理时对齐推广到生成式奖励模型的集成中，这些模型以锐化对数意见池（SLOP）的形式组合。为缓解奖励破解问题，我们提出了一种校准SLOP权重参数的算法，并通过实验证明该方法在保持对齐性能的同时提升了鲁棒性。

The authors propose extending these techniques by adjusting the reference model temperature and generalizing alignment to ensembles of generative reward models combined as a sharpened logarithmic opinion pool (SLOP). They introduce an algorithm to calibrate SLOP weight parameters, and experiments show that this approach improves robustness against reward hacking while maintaining alignment performance.
该论文针对推理时对齐中的奖励黑客问题，现有方法近似于从奖励倾斜分布中采样。作者通过调整参考模型温度并将对齐推广到生成式奖励模型集成（结合为锐化对数意见池SLOP）来扩展这些技术。他们提出了一种校准SLOP权重参数的算法，实验表明该方法在保持对齐性能的同时提高了对奖励黑客的鲁棒性。
HLS-Seek: QoR-Aware Code Generation for High-Level Synthesis via Proxy Comparative Reward Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qingyun Zou, Feng Yu, Hongshi Tan, Yao Chen, Bingsheng He, WengFai Wong
First: 2026-05-13T13:47:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T13:47:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
High-Level Synthesis (HLS) compiles algorithmic C/C++ descriptions into hardware, with Quality of Results (QoR) -- latency and resource utilization -- critically governed by pragma configurations and code structure. Existing LLM-based HLS approaches train for functional correctness but ignore QoR entirely. We observe that reinforcement learning (RL) for HLS does not require absolute synthesis results -- only relative comparisons between candidates. Based on this insight, we propose \textbf{HLS-Seek}, a QoR-aware NL-to-HLS framework that replaces expensive synthesis-in-the-loop RL with a comparative proxy reward model achieving 99.53\% Pareto-dominance accuracy. To prevent reward hacking, we introduce \textit{uncertainty-aware Monte Carlo (MC) dropout switching} that selectively invokes real Vitis HLS synthesis for low-confidence candidates and online updates the proxy, creating a self-improving reward system. HLS-Seek achieves 81.5\% syntax correctness pass@1 and 81.4\% Func@5 on HLS-eval with only 7B parameters, surpassing GPT-5.1 and other frontier models while achieving 8.5$\times$ faster training than real-reward RL. On QoR evaluation, HLS-Seek achieves the lowest latency on 16/30 kernels and Pareto-dominates HLS-specific baselines on 9 kernels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HLS-Seek：基于代理比较奖励强化学习的高层次综合QoR感知代码生成
高层次综合（HLS）将算法级C/C++描述编译为硬件，其结果质量（QoR）——延迟和资源利用率——关键受制于编译指示配置和代码结构。现有的基于LLM的HLS方法训练时注重功能正确性，但完全忽略QoR。我们观察到，用于HLS的强化学习（RL）不需要绝对的综合结果——仅需候选方案之间的相对比较。基于这一洞察，我们提出\textbf{HLS-Seek}，一个QoR感知的自然语言到HLS框架，用比较代理奖励模型替代昂贵的综合在环RL，实现了99.53%的帕累托支配准确率。为防止奖励破解，我们引入\textit{不确定性感知蒙特卡洛（MC）丢弃切换}，对低置信度候选方案选择性调用真实Vitis HLS综合，并在线更新代理，形成自我改进的奖励系统。HLS-Seek在HLS-eval上以仅7B参数实现了81.5%的语法正确性pass@1和81.4%的Func@5，超越了GPT-5.1及其他前沿模型，同时训练速度比真实奖励RL快8.5倍。在QoR评估中，HLS-Seek在16/30个内核上实现了最低延迟，并在9个内核上帕累托支配了HLS专用基线。
Summary / 总结
HLS-Seek addresses the problem that existing LLM-based High-Level Synthesis (HLS) approaches focus on functional correctness but ignore Quality of Results (QoR) such as latency and resource utilization. The method proposes a QoR-aware NL-to-HLS framework that replaces expensive synthesis-in-the-loop reinforcement learning with a comparative proxy reward model, achieving 99.53% Pareto-dominance accuracy, and introduces uncertainty-aware Monte Carlo dropout switching to prevent reward hacking by selectively invoking real synthesis for low-confidence candidates. Experimentally, HLS-Seek achieves 81.5% syntax correctness pass@1 and 81.4% Func@5 on HLS-eval with only 7B parameters, surpassing GPT-5.1 and other frontier models, while achieving 8.5x faster training than real-reward RL, and on QoR evaluation it achieves the lowest latency on 16/30 kernels and Pareto-dominates HLS-specific baselines on 9 kernels.
HLS-Seek针对现有基于LLM的高层次综合方法只关注功能正确性而忽略结果质量（如延迟和资源利用率）的问题。该方法提出了一种面向QoR的自然语言到HLS框架，用比较性代理奖励模型替代昂贵的综合在环强化学习，实现了99.53%的帕累托支配准确率，并引入不确定性感知的蒙特卡洛丢弃切换机制，通过对低置信度候选调用真实综合来防止奖励欺骗。实验结果显示，HLS-Seek在HLS-eval上仅用7B参数就达到了81.5%的语法正确率pass@1和81.4%的Func@5，超越了GPT-5.1等前沿模型，训练速度比真实奖励强化学习快8.5倍，在QoR评估中，它在30个内核中的16个上实现了最低延迟，并在9个内核上帕累托支配了HLS专用基线方法。
Scaling Retrieval-Augmented Reasoning with Parallel Search and Explicit Merging
Authors: Jiabei Liu, Wenyu Mao, Junfei Tan, Chunxu Shen, Lingling Yi, Jiancan Wu, Xiang Wang
First: 2026-05-13T13:46:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T13:46:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep search agents have proven effective in enhancing LLMs by retrieving external knowledge during multi-step reasoning. However, existing methods often generate a single query for retrieval at each reasoning step, limiting information coverage and introducing high noise. This may result in low signal-to-noise ratios (SNR) during search, degrading reasoning accuracy and leading to unnecessary reasoning steps. In this paper, we introduce MultiSearch, an RL-based framework that addresses these limitations through multi-query retrieval and explicit merging of retrieved information. At each reasoning step, MultiSearch generates queries from multiple perspectives and retrieves external information in parallel, expanding the scope of relevant information and mitigating the reliance on any single retrieval result. Then, the agent consolidates and refines retrieved information at the merging process, improving the SNR and ensuring more accurate reasoning. Additionally, we propose a reinforcement learning framework with a multi-process reward design to optimize agents for both multi-query retrieval and information consolidation. Extensive experiments on seven benchmarks demonstrate that MultiSearch outperforms baseline methods, enhancing the SNR of retrieval and improving reasoning performance in question-answering tasks.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces MultiSearch, a reinforcement learning-based framework designed to improve retrieval-augmented reasoning in large language models by addressing the limitations of single-query retrieval, which often results in low signal-to-noise ratios and inaccurate reasoning. The method generates multiple queries from diverse perspectives at each reasoning step, retrieves external information in parallel, and then explicitly merges the retrieved data to enhance information coverage and reduce noise. Experimental results on seven benchmarks show that MultiSearch outperforms baseline methods, significantly improving the signal-to-noise ratio of retrieval and boosting reasoning accuracy in question-answering tasks.
该论文提出了MultiSearch，一种基于强化学习的框架，旨在通过解决单查询检索的局限性（如低信噪比和不准确推理）来提升大语言模型的检索增强推理能力。该方法在每个推理步骤中从多个角度生成查询，并行检索外部信息，然后显式合并检索到的数据，以扩大信息覆盖范围并降低噪声。在七个基准测试上的实验结果表明，MultiSearch优于基线方法，显著提高了检索的信噪比，并提升了问答任务中的推理准确性。
MARLIN: Multi-Agent Game-Theoretic Reinforcement Learning for Sustainable LLM Inference in Cloud Datacenters
Authors: H. Moore, S. Qi, D. Milojicic, C. Bash, S. Pasricha
First: 2026-05-13T13:20:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T13:20:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have become increasingly prevalent in cloud-based platforms, propelled by the introduction of AI-based consumer and enterprise services. LLM inference requests in particular account for up to 90% of total LLM lifecycle energy use, dwarfing training energy costs. The rising volume of LLM inference requests is increasing environmental footprints, particularly carbon emissions and water consumption. To improve sustainability for LLM inference serving in cloud datacenter environments, we propose a novel multi-agent game-theoretic reinforcement learning framework called MARLIN to co-optimize time-to-first token (TTFT), carbon emissions, water usage, and energy costs associated with LLM inference. MARLIN demonstrates a reduction of at least 18% in TTFT, 33% in carbon emissions, 43% in water usage, and 11% in energy costs compared to state-of-the-art LLM inference management frameworks.

To improve sustainability, the authors propose MARLIN, a multi-agent game-theoretic reinforcement learning framework that co-optimizes time-to-first token (TTFT), carbon emissions, water usage, and energy costs. Experimental results show that MARLIN achieves at least an 18% reduction in TTFT, 33% in carbon emissions, 43% in water usage, and 11% in energy costs compared to state-of-the-art LLM inference management frameworks.

Addressing Finite-Horizon MDPs via Low-Rank Tensor Value Approximation
Authors: Sergio Rozada, Jose Luis Orejuela, Antonio G. Marques
First: 2025-01-17T23:10:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T13:08:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of learning optimal policies in finite-horizon Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) using low-rank reinforcement learning (RL) methods. In finite-horizon MDPs, the policies, and therefore the value functions (VFs) are not stationary. This aggravates the challenges of high-dimensional MDPs, as they suffer from the curse of dimensionality and high sample complexity. To address these issues, we propose modeling the VFs of finite-horizon MDPs as low-rank tensors, enabling a scalable representation that renders the problem of learning optimal policies tractable. Our approach focuses on VF approximation within a policy iteration framework, where low-rank policy evaluation is combined with greedy policy improvement to compute near-optimal policies. We introduce an optimization-based framework for solving the Bellman equations with low-rank constraints, along with block-coordinate descent (BCD) and block-coordinate gradient descent (BCGD) algorithms, both with theoretical convergence guarantees. We further establish that bounded low-rank policy evaluation error translates into bounded policy improvement in the finite-horizon setting. For scenarios where the system dynamics are unknown, we adapt the proposed BCGD method to estimate the VFs using sampled trajectories. Numerical experiments further demonstrate that the proposed framework reduces computational demands in controlled synthetic scenarios and more realistic resource allocation problems, while achieving competitive policy performance in terms of attained returns.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of learning optimal policies in finite-horizon Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), where non-stationary policies and value functions exacerbate the curse of dimensionality and high sample complexity. The authors propose modeling value functions as low-rank tensors within a policy iteration framework, combining low-rank policy evaluation with greedy improvement to compute near-optimal policies. They introduce optimization-based algorithms, including block-coordinate descent and block-coordinate gradient descent, with theoretical convergence guarantees, and show that bounded low-rank evaluation error leads to bounded policy improvement. Numerical experiments on synthetic and resource allocation problems demonstrate reduced computational demands while achieving competitive policy returns.
本文针对有限时域马尔可夫决策过程中策略与价值函数非平稳所导致的维度灾难和高样本复杂度问题，提出将价值函数建模为低秩张量，并在策略迭代框架中结合低秩策略评估与贪婪改进以计算近优策略。作者引入了基于优化的算法，包括块坐标下降和块坐标梯度下降，并提供了理论收敛保证，同时证明了有界低秩评估误差可转化为有界策略改进。在合成场景和资源分配问题的数值实验中，该方法在降低计算需求的同时实现了具有竞争力的策略回报。
Q-Flow: Stable and Expressive Reinforcement Learning with Flow-Based Policy
Authors: JaeHyeok Doo, Byeongguk Jeon, Seonghyeon Ye, Kimin Lee, Minjoon Seo
First: 2026-05-13T12:31:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T12:31:02+00:00
Comments: 27 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
There is growing interest in utilizing flow-based models as decision-making policies in reinforcement learning due to their high expressive capacity. However, effectively leveraging this expressivity for value maximization remains challenging, as naive gradient-based optimization requires backpropagating through numerical solvers and often leads to instability. Existing approaches typically address this issue by restricting the expressive capacity of flow-based policies, resulting in a trade-off between optimization stability and representational flexibility. To resolve this, we introduce Q-Flow, a framework that leverages the deterministic nature of flow dynamics to explicitly propagate terminal trajectory value to intermediate latent states along the policy-induced flow. This formulation enables stable policy optimization using intermediate value gradients without unrolling the numerical solver, effectively bridging the gap between stability and expressivity. We evaluate Q-Flow in the offline learning setting on the challenging OGBench suite, where it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by an average of 10.6 percentage points, while also enabling stable online adaptation within the same framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Q-Flow：基于流策略的稳定且富有表现力的强化学习方法
由于流模型具有高表达能力，将其作为强化学习中的决策策略日益受到关注。然而，有效利用这种表达能力以实现价值最大化仍具挑战性，因为基于梯度的朴素优化需要反向传播通过数值求解器，且常导致不稳定性。现有方法通常通过限制流策略的表达能力来解决此问题，导致优化稳定性与表示灵活性之间的权衡。为解决这一问题，我们提出Q-Flow框架，该框架利用流动力学的确定性特性，将终端轨迹价值显式传播至策略诱导流中的中间潜在状态。这种公式化方法使得无需展开数值求解器即可使用中间价值梯度进行稳定的策略优化，有效弥合了稳定性与表达能力之间的差距。我们在具有挑战性的OGBench套件上评估了离线学习设置下的Q-Flow，其平均性能比最先进的基线方法高出10.6个百分点，同时在同一框架内实现了稳定的在线自适应。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Q-Flow, a framework for reinforcement learning that uses flow-based models as policies to achieve high expressivity while maintaining stable optimization. The key motivation is that naive gradient-based optimization of flow-based policies requires backpropagating through numerical solvers, causing instability, and existing methods trade off expressivity for stability. Q-Flow resolves this by leveraging the deterministic nature of flow dynamics to propagate terminal trajectory value back to intermediate latent states, enabling stable policy optimization with intermediate value gradients without unrolling the solver. In offline learning experiments on the OGBench suite, Q-Flow consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines by an average of 10.6 percentage points and also supports stable online adaptation within the same framework.

Trajectory-Level Data Augmentation for Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tobias Schmähling, Matthias Burkhardt, Tobias Windisch
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-13T11:57:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T11:57:17+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 25 figures, Accepted at ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose a data augmentation method for offline reinforcement learning, motivated by active positioning problems. Particularly, our approach enables the training of off-policy models from a limited number of suboptimal trajectories. We introduce a trajectory-based augmentation technique that exploits task structure and the geometric relationship between rewards, value functions, and mathematical properties of logging policies. During data collection, our augmentation supports suboptimal logging policies, leading to higher data quality and improved offline reinforcement learning performance. We provide theoretical justification for these strategies and validate them empirically across positioning tasks of varying dimensionality and under partial observability.

Theoretical justification is provided, and empirical results on positioning tasks of varying dimensionality and under partial observability demonstrate significant performance gains.
该论文针对主动定位问题，提出了一种轨迹级别的数据增强方法，用于离线强化学习，旨在从有限的次优轨迹中有效训练模型。该方法利用任务结构以及奖励、价值函数和日志策略属性之间的几何关系来生成增强数据，从而提升数据质量和离线学习性能。论文提供了理论依据，并在不同维度和部分可观测的定位任务上进行了实验验证，结果表明该方法显著提升了性能。
GRIP-VLM: Group-Relative Importance Pruning for Efficient Vision-Language Models
Authors: Mingzhe Huang, Weijun Wang, Xin Ding, Liang Mi, Hao Wen, Yuanchun Li, Lichen Pang, Shansong Yang, Yunxin Liu, Ting Cao
First: 2026-05-13T11:32:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T11:32:03+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In Vision-Language Models (VLMs), processing a massive number of visual tokens incurs prohibitive computational overhead. While recent training-aware pruning methods attempt to selectively discard redundant tokens, they largely rely on continuous-gradient relaxations. However, visual token pruning is inherently a discrete, non-convex combinatorial problem; consequently, these continuous approximations frequently trap the optimization in sub-optimal local minima, especially under aggressive compression budgets. To overcome this fundamental bottleneck, we propose GRIP-VLM, a Group-Relative Importance Pruning framework driven by Reinforcement Learning. Rather than relying on smooth-gradient assumptions, GRIP-VLM formulates pruning as a Markov Decision Process, employing a Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) paradigm anchored by supervised warm-up to directly explore the discrete selection space. Integrated with a budget-aware scorer, our lightweight agent dynamically evaluates per-token importance and adapts to arbitrary compression ratios without retraining. Extensive experiments across diverse multimodal benchmarks demonstrate that GRIP-VLM consistently outperforms heuristic and supervised-learning baselines, achieving a superior Pareto frontier and delivering up to a 15\% inference speedup at equal accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GRIP-VLM：基于组相对重要性的高效视觉语言模型剪枝方法
在视觉语言模型（VLM）中，处理大量视觉令牌会带来高昂的计算开销。尽管近期基于训练感知的剪枝方法尝试选择性丢弃冗余令牌，但它们主要依赖连续梯度松弛。然而，视觉令牌剪枝本质上是一个离散、非凸的组合优化问题；因此，这些连续近似方法在激进压缩预算下常陷入次优局部极小值。为突破这一根本瓶颈，我们提出GRIP-VLM——一种基于强化学习的组相对重要性剪枝框架。GRIP-VLM不依赖平滑梯度假设，而是将剪枝建模为马尔可夫决策过程，采用基于监督预热的组相对策略优化（GRPO）范式直接探索离散选择空间。结合预算感知评分器，我们的轻量级智能体可动态评估每个令牌的重要性，并无需重新训练即可适应任意压缩比。跨多模态基准的大量实验表明，GRIP-VLM在性能上持续优于启发式及监督学习基线，实现了更优的帕累托前沿，并在同等精度下带来高达15%的推理加速。

A budget-aware scorer dynamically evaluates token importance for any compression ratio without retraining. 该论文针对视觉语言模型中处理大量视觉令牌导致计算开销过高的问题。现有训练感知剪枝方法依赖连续梯度松弛，但视觉令牌剪枝本质上是离散的非凸组合问题，导致优化陷入次优局部最小值。为此，作者提出GRIP-VLM框架，利用强化学习（结合监督预热的组相对策略优化）将剪枝建模为马尔可夫决策过程，并通过预算感知评分器动态评估令牌重要性，无需重新训练即可适应任意压缩比。实验表明，GRIP-VLM在多种多模态基准上持续优于启发式和监督学习基线，在同等精度下实现高达15%的推理加速，并达到更优的帕累托前沿。
The Geno-Synthetic Algorithm: Type-Factored Coevolutionary Optimization for Heterogeneous Genotypes and Assembled Phenotypes
Authors: Alex Bogdan
First: 2026-05-13T11:25:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T11:25:24+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many real-world optimization problems are not naturally homogeneous vectors but composite design objects with heterogeneous parameters: integers, real values, Booleans, categoricals, complex-valued descriptors, and embedding vectors. Standard evolutionary algorithms flatten these into a single chromosome and apply generic operators with rounding and repair, sacrificing representational fidelity. We introduce the Geno-Synthetic Algorithm (GSA), a type-factored coevolutionary framework in which gene families are partitioned by representational type, evolved in parallel with type-native operators, and assembled into executable phenotypes for joint fitness evaluation. GSA is formalized as a typed product-space search procedure with an explicit assembly operator. An open-source reference implementation (gsa-experiments, MIT-licensed) is released. A focused empirical study compares eight GSA variants against five baselines across seven benchmark problems (six synthetic plus the external COCO BBOB-MixInt suite) at budgets from 5,000 to 100,000 evaluations. The headline finding is architectural: GSA is the only method that operates when gene families include complex-valued descriptors or embedding vectors. On smooth synthetic multi-family problems, well-tuned flattened differential evolution remains the strongest baseline; on BBOB-MixInt at 100,000 evaluations, GSA_DIRECT becomes statistically indistinguishable from FLATTENED_DE while FLATTENED_EA drops from second to fifth rank, an asymptotic crossover. Ablations confirm that type-native operators are essential, elite credit dominates ensemble credit, and active assembly outperforms passive concatenation on gated benchmarks. The framework extends naturally to prompt and embedding optimization for large language model systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基因合成算法：面向异质基因型和组装表型的类型分解协同进化优化
许多现实世界的优化问题并非天然的同质向量，而是具有异质参数的复合设计对象：整数、实数值、布尔值、类别值、复值描述符和嵌入向量。标准进化算法将这些参数扁平化为单一染色体，并应用带有舍入和修复的通用算子，牺牲了表征保真度。我们提出基因合成算法（GSA），这是一种类型分解的协同进化框架，其中基因家族按表征类型划分，使用类型原生算子并行进化，并组装成可执行表型以进行联合适应度评估。GSA被形式化为一种带显式组装算子的类型化乘积空间搜索过程。我们发布了一个开源参考实现（gsa-experiments，MIT许可）。一项聚焦的实证研究比较了八种GSA变体与五种基线在七个基准问题（六个合成问题加上外部COCO BBOB-MixInt套件）上的表现，预算从5,000到100,000次评估不等。主要发现是架构性的：GSA是唯一能在基因家族包含复值描述符或嵌入向量时运行的方法。在平滑的合成多家族问题上，调优后的扁平化差分进化仍是最强基线；在BBOB-MixInt上以100,000次评估时，GSA_DIRECT在统计上与FLATTENED_DE无显著差异，而FLATTENED_EA从第二位降至第五位，出现渐近交叉。消融实验证实，类型原生算子至关重要，精英信用主导集成信用，且在门控基准上主动组装优于被动拼接。该框架可自然扩展到大型语言模型系统的提示和嵌入优化。
Summary / 总结
The Geno-Synthetic Algorithm (GSA) is motivated by the challenge that real-world optimization problems often involve heterogeneous parameter types (e.g., integers, reals, Booleans, categoricals, complex-valued descriptors, and embedding vectors), which standard evolutionary algorithms handle poorly by flattening into a single chromosome and applying generic operators with rounding and repair. GSA addresses this by partitioning gene families by representational type, evolving them in parallel with type-native operators, and assembling them into executable phenotypes for joint fitness evaluation, formalized as a typed product-space search procedure. In experiments across seven benchmark problems (six synthetic plus COCO BBOB-MixInt) with budgets from 5,000 to 100,000 evaluations, GSA uniquely operates when gene families include complex-valued descriptors or embedding vectors; while well-tuned flattened differential evolution is strongest on smooth synthetic problems, GSA_DIRECT becomes statistically indistinguishable from FLATTENED_DE on BBOB-MixInt at 100,000 evaluations, with ablations confirming the necessity of type-native operators and the superiority of elite credit and active assembly.
基因合成算法（GSA）的动机在于，现实优化问题常包含异构参数类型（如整数、实数、布尔值、类别值、复值描述符和嵌入向量），而标准进化算法通过将参数展平为单一染色体并应用通用算子（含舍入和修复）来处理，牺牲了表示保真度。GSA通过按表示类型划分基因家族，使用类型原生算子并行进化，并组装成可执行表型进行联合适应度评估来解决这一问题，形式化为类型化乘积空间搜索过程。在七个基准问题（六个合成问题加COCO BBOB-MixInt套件）上，预算从5,000到100,000次评估的实验中，GSA是唯一能在基因家族包含复值描述符或嵌入向量时运行的方法；在平滑合成多家族问题上，调优后的展平差分进化仍是最强基线，而在BBOB-MixInt上100,000次评估时，GSA_DIRECT与FLATTENED_DE统计上无差异，消融实验证实了类型原生算子的必要性以及精英信用和主动组装的优势。
Events as Triggers for Behavioral Diversity in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hannes Büchi, Manon Flageat, Eduardo Sebastián, Amanda Prorok
First: 2026-05-12T16:51:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T11:22:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective multi-agent cooperation requires agents to adopt diverse behaviors as task conditions evolve-and to do so at the right moment. Yet, current Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) frameworks that facilitate this diversity are still limited by the fact that they bind fixed behaviors to fixed agent identities. Consequently, they are ill-equipped for tasks where agents need to take on different roles at very specific moments in time. We argue that, to define these behavioral transitions, the missing ingredient is $\textbf{events}$. Events are changes in the state of the system that induce qualitative changes in the task. Based on this view, we introduce a framework that decouples agent identity from behavior, capturing a continuous manifold from which agents instantiate their behaviors in response to events. This framework is based on two elements. First, to build an expressive behavior manifold, we introduce Neural Manifold Diversity (NMD), a formal distance metric that remains well-defined when behaviors are transient and agent-agnostic. Second, we use an event-based hypernetwork that generates Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) modules over a shared team policy, enabling on-the-fly agent-policy reconfiguration in response to events. We prove that this construction ensures that diversity does not interfere with reward maximization by design. Empirical results demonstrate that our framework outperforms established baselines across benchmarks while exhibiting zero-shot generalization, and being the only method that solves tasks requiring sequential behavior reassignment.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation in current Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) frameworks that bind fixed behaviors to fixed agent identities, hindering cooperation in tasks requiring role changes at specific moments. To solve this, the authors propose an event-driven framework that decouples agent identity from behavior, using Neural Manifold Diversity (NMD) as a distance metric for transient, agent-agnostic behaviors and an event-based hypernetwork to generate Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) modules over a shared team policy for on-the-fly reconfiguration. The method is proven to not interfere with reward maximization, and experiments show it outperforms baselines across benchmarks, exhibits zero-shot generalization, and is the only approach solving tasks requiring sequential behavior reassignment.
该论文指出当前多智能体强化学习框架将固定行为绑定到固定智能体身份，难以处理需要智能体在特定时刻切换角色的任务。为此，作者提出一个基于事件的框架，将智能体身份与行为解耦，利用神经流形多样性作为度量瞬态、与智能体无关行为的距离指标，并通过事件驱动的超网络为共享团队策略生成低秩适配模块，实现实时策略重构。理论证明该方法不会干扰奖励最大化，实验结果表明其在多个基准测试中优于现有方法，具备零样本泛化能力，且是唯一能解决需要顺序行为重分配任务的方案。
TRUST-TAEA: A trustworthiness-guided two-archive evolutionary algorithm with variable-grouping sparse search for large-scale multi-objective optimization
Authors: JunYi Cui
First: 2026-05-13T10:36:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T10:36:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large-scale multi-objective optimization remains challenging because high-dimensional decision spaces, complex variable interactions, and limited function evaluation budgets make it difficult to balance convergence, diversity, and stability. Existing two-archive evolutionary algorithms can alleviate the conflict between convergence and diversity, but they often underuse archive reliability and problem-structure information, leading to inefficient search, incomplete front coverage, and late-stage archive drift. To address these issues, this paper proposes TRUST-TAEA, a trustworthiness-guided two-archive evolutionary algorithm. Archive trustworthiness is defined by integrating evolutionary progress with convergence-archive maturity, and is used to coordinate variable-grouping sparse search, anchor-probing compensatory search, and archive stabilization. TRUST-TAEA is evaluated on the LSMOP benchmark suite with 500--5000 decision variables and two or three objectives. Experimental results show that TRUST-TAEA achieves superior or highly competitive performance in terms of convergence, diversity, and stability. A three-objective day-ahead scheduling case of a grid-connected microgrid further demonstrates its practical applicability, where TRUST-TAEA obtains the best IGD$^+$ value and generates a feasible dispatch strategy balancing cost, emissions, and grid-power fluctuation.
Summary / 总结
Large-scale multi-objective optimization is challenging due to high-dimensional decision spaces and limited evaluation budgets, which hinder the balance of convergence, diversity, and stability. To address this, the authors propose TRUST-TAEA, a trustworthiness-guided two-archive evolutionary algorithm that defines archive trustworthiness by integrating evolutionary progress with convergence-archive maturity, and uses it to coordinate variable-grouping sparse search, anchor-probing compensatory search, and archive stabilization. Evaluated on the LSMOP benchmark suite with 500–5000 variables and two or three objectives, TRUST-TAEA achieves superior or highly competitive performance in convergence, diversity, and stability, and in a three-objective microgrid scheduling case, it obtains the best IGD⁺ value and generates a feasible dispatch strategy balancing cost, emissions, and grid-power fluctuation.
大规模多目标优化因高维决策空间和有限评估预算而极具挑战，难以平衡收敛性、多样性和稳定性。为此，作者提出TRUST-TAEA，一种可信度引导的双存档进化算法，通过整合进化进度与收敛存档成熟度定义存档可信度，并以此协调变量分组稀疏搜索、锚点探测补偿搜索和存档稳定化。在包含500至5000个决策变量、两或三个目标的LSMOP基准套件上评估，TRUST-TAEA在收敛性、多样性和稳定性方面表现优异或极具竞争力；在三目标并网微电网日前调度案例中，它获得了最佳IGD⁺值，并生成了平衡成本、排放和电网功率波动的可行调度策略。
Safe Bayesian Optimization for Uncertain Correlations Matrices in Linear Models of Co-Regionalization
Authors: Jannis Lübsen, Annika Eichler
First: 2026-05-13T10:14:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T10:14:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted at IFAC WC26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper extends safety guarantees for multi-task Bayesian optimization with uncertain correlation matrices from intrinsic co-reginalization models to linear models of co-reginalization. The latter allows for more flexible modeling of the inter-task correlations by composing multiple features. We derive uniform error bounds for vector-valued functions sampled from a Gaussian process with a linear model of co-reginalization kernel. Furthermore, we show the potential improvement of performance using linear models of co-reginalization in a numerical comparison on a safe multi-task Bayesian optimization benchmark.

The authors derive uniform error bounds for vector-valued functions sampled from a Gaussian process with a linear model of co-regionalization kernel. Numerical experiments on a safe multi-task Bayesian optimization benchmark demonstrate that the proposed approach achieves improved performance compared to existing methods.

Delightful Distributed Policy Gradient
Authors: Ian Osband
First: 2026-03-20T21:45:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T10:10:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Distributed reinforcement learning trains on data from stale, buggy, or mismatched actors, producing actions with high surprisal (negative log-probability) under the learner's policy. The core difficulty is not surprising data per se, but \emph{negative learning from surprising data}. High-surprisal failures can dominate finite-batch updates through large perpendicular components, while high-surprisal successes reveal opportunities the current policy would otherwise miss. The \textit{Delightful Policy Gradient} (DG) separates these cases by gating each update with delight, the product of advantage and surprisal, suppressing rare failures and preserving rare successes without behavior probabilities. In a tabular analysis, DG suppresses the perpendicular second moment of high-surprisal failures by a policy-overlap factor that vanishes as the learner improves. The advantage sign is essential for surprisal-based filtering: any learner-probability-only gate that suppresses rare failures also suppresses rare successes. On MNIST with simulated staleness, DG without off-policy correction outperforms importance-weighted PG with exact behavior probabilities. On a transformer sequence task with staleness, actor bugs, reward corruption, and rare discovery, DG often achieves nearly order-of-magnitude lower error. When all four frictions act simultaneously, its sample-efficiency advantage is order-of-magnitude and grows with task complexity.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of distributed reinforcement learning where data from stale, buggy, or mismatched actors leads to high-surprisal actions under the learner's policy, causing negative learning. The authors propose the Delightful Policy Gradient (DG) method, which gates each update using delight—the product of advantage and surprisal—to suppress rare failures while preserving rare successes without relying on behavior probabilities. In tabular analysis, DG reduces the perpendicular second moment of high-surprisal failures by a policy-overlap factor that diminishes as the learner improves. Experiments on MNIST with simulated staleness show DG outperforms importance-weighted PG with exact behavior probabilities, and on a transformer sequence task with staleness, actor bugs, reward corruption, and rare discovery, DG achieves nearly order-of-magnitude lower error, with its sample-efficiency advantage growing with task complexity under simultaneous frictions.
该论文针对分布式强化学习中，因数据来自过时、有缺陷或不匹配的智能体而导致学习者策略下出现高意外性动作，进而引发负向学习的问题。作者提出了愉悦策略梯度（DG）方法，通过使用优势与意外性的乘积——愉悦度——来门控每次更新，从而抑制罕见失败同时保留罕见成功，无需依赖行为概率。在表格分析中，DG通过一个随学习者改进而消失的策略重叠因子，抑制了高意外性失败的垂直二阶矩。在MNIST模拟过时性实验中，DG优于使用精确行为概率的重要性加权PG；在包含过时性、智能体缺陷、奖励破坏和罕见发现的Transformer序列任务中，DG实现了近一个数量级的误差降低，且在多种摩擦同时存在时，其样本效率优势随任务复杂度增长而扩大。
D-VLA: A High-Concurrency Distributed Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning Framework for Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Yucheng Guo, Yongjian Guo, Zhong Guan, Wen Huang, Haoran Sun, Haodong Yue, Xiaolong Xiang, Shuai Di, Zhen Sun, Luqiao Wang, Junwu Xiong, Yicheng Gong
First: 2026-05-13T09:54:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T09:54:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid evolution of Embodied AI has enabled Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models to excel in multimodal perception and task execution. However, applying Reinforcement Learning (RL) to these massive models in large-scale distributed environments faces severe systemic bottlenecks, primarily due to the resource conflict between high-fidelity physical simulation and the intensive VRAM/bandwidth demands of deep learning. This conflict often leaves overall throughput constrained by execution-phase inefficiencies. To address these challenges, we propose D-VLA, a high-concurrency, low-latency distributed RL framework for large-scale embodied foundation models. D-VLA introduces "Plane Decoupling," physically isolating high-frequency training data from low-frequency weight control to eliminate interference between simulation and optimization. We further design a four-thread asynchronous "Swimlane" pipeline, enabling full parallel overlap of sampling, inference, gradient computation, and parameter distribution. Additionally, a dual-pool VRAM management model and topology-aware replication resolve memory fragmentation and optimize communication efficiency. Experiments on benchmarks like LIBERO show that D-VLA significantly outperforms mainstream RL frameworks in throughput and sampling efficiency for billion-parameter VLA models. In trillion-parameter scalability tests, our framework maintains exceptional stability and linear speedup, providing a robust system for high-performance general-purpose embodied agents.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces D-VLA, a distributed reinforcement learning framework designed to address systemic bottlenecks in training large-scale Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models for Embodied AI, where resource conflicts between high-fidelity simulation and deep learning demands limit throughput. The method employs Plane Decoupling to separate training data from weight control, a four-thread asynchronous Swimlane pipeline for parallel sampling, inference, gradient computation, and parameter distribution, and a dual-pool VRAM management model with topology-aware replication to optimize memory and communication. Experimental results on benchmarks like LIBERO demonstrate that D-VLA significantly outperforms mainstream RL frameworks in throughput and sampling efficiency for billion-parameter VLA models, while maintaining exceptional stability and linear speedup in trillion-parameter scalability tests.
该论文提出了D-VLA，一种分布式强化学习框架，旨在解决大规模视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在具身智能训练中的系统瓶颈，即高保真物理模拟与深度学习资源需求之间的冲突限制了吞吐量。方法采用平面解耦技术分离训练数据与权重控制，设计四线程异步泳道流水线实现采样、推理、梯度计算和参数分布的完全并行，并通过双池VRAM管理模型和拓扑感知复制优化内存与通信效率。在LIBERO等基准测试上的实验表明，D-VLA在十亿参数VLA模型的吞吐量和采样效率上显著优于主流强化学习框架，并在万亿参数可扩展性测试中保持卓越稳定性和线性加速。
Learning to Approximate Uniform Facility Location via Graph Neural Networks
Authors: Chendi Qian, Christopher Morris, Stefanie Jegelka, Christian Sohler
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-02-13T18:08:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T09:47:05+00:00
Comments: ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural networks, particularly message-passing neural networks (MPNNs), are increasingly used as heuristics for hard combinatorial optimization problems. Yet many learning-based methods rely on supervision, reinforcement learning, or gradient estimators, causing high computational cost, unstable training, or limited guarantees. Classical approximation algorithms provide worst-case guarantees but are non-differentiable and cannot adapt to structure in natural input distributions. We study this tradeoff through Uniform Facility Location (UniFL), a problem with applications in clustering, summarization, logistics, and supply chains. We propose a fully differentiable MPNN that incorporates approximation-algorithmic principles without solver supervision or discrete relaxations. The model has provable approximation guarantees and empirically improves on standard approximation algorithms, narrowing the gap to integer linear programming.
中文标题/摘要

神经网络，特别是消息传递神经网络（MPNN），正越来越多地被用作解决困难组合优化问题的启发式方法。然而，许多基于学习的方法依赖于监督、强化学习或梯度估计器，导致计算成本高、训练不稳定或保证有限。经典近似算法提供最坏情况下的保证，但不可微且无法适应自然输入分布中的结构。我们通过均匀设施选址问题（UniFL）研究这种权衡，该问题在聚类、摘要、物流和供应链中具有应用。我们提出了一种完全可微的MPNN，它融合了近似算法原理，无需求解器监督或离散松弛。该模型具有可证明的近似保证，并在经验上优于标准近似算法，缩小了与整数线性规划的差距。

Teacher-Guided Policy Optimization for LLM Distillation
Authors: Xinyu Liu, Kechen Jiao, Chunyang Xiao, Runsong Zhao, Junhao Ruan, Bei Li, Jiahao Liu, Qifan Wang, Xin Chen, Jingang Wang, Tong Xiao, JingBo Zhu
First: 2026-05-13T09:20:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T09:20:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The convergence of reinforcement learning and imitation learning has positioned Reverse KL (RKL) as a promising paradigm for on-policy LLM distillation, aiming to unify exploration with teacher supervision. However, we identify a critical limitation: when the student and teacher distributions diverge significantly, standard RKL often fails to yield meaningful improvement due to uninformative negative feedback. To address this inefficiency, we propose Teacher-Guided Policy Optimization (TGPO), an on-policy algorithm that incorporates dense directional guidance by leveraging teacher predictions conditioned on the student's rollout. Because TGPO remains on-policy, the algorithm integrates seamlessly with existing RLVR frameworks without requiring additional data annotation. Experiments on complex reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that TGPO significantly outperforms standard baselines and is robust to different teachers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：教师引导的LLM蒸馏策略优化
强化学习与模仿学习的融合使反向KL散度成为在线LLM蒸馏的一种有前景的范式，旨在统一探索与教师监督。然而，我们发现一个关键局限：当学生与教师分布显著偏离时，标准反向KL散度常因无信息的负反馈而无法产生有意义的改进。为解决此低效问题，我们提出教师引导策略优化，一种利用教师基于学生轨迹预测的密集方向性指导的在线算法。由于TGPO保持在线特性，该算法可无缝集成到现有RLVR框架中，无需额外数据标注。在复杂推理基准上的实验表明，TGPO显著优于标准基线，且对不同教师具有鲁棒性。

To address this, the authors propose Teacher-Guided Policy Optimization (TGPO), an on-policy algorithm that incorporates dense directional guidance by leveraging teacher predictions conditioned on the student's rollout, integrating seamlessly with existing RLVR frameworks without extra data annotation. Experiments on complex reasoning benchmarks show that TGPO significantly outperforms standard baselines and remains robust across different teacher models.
