An Agentic AI Framework with Large Language Models and Chain-of-Thought for UAV-Assisted Logistics Scheduling with Mobile Edge Computing
Authors: Hanwen Zhang, Dusit Niyato, Wei Zhang, Xin Lou, Malcolm Yoke Hean Low
First: 2026-05-13T09:13:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T09:13:19+00:00
Comments: 15 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In cloud manufacturing, unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) can support both product collection and mobile edge computing (MEC). This joint operation forms a hybrid scheduling problem, where physical logistics decisions are coupled with computational task scheduling. In this paper, UAVs collect finished products from manufacturing stations and transport them back to a central depot. Meanwhile, computational tasks generated by industrial sensor devices at these stations are processed locally, at UAVs, or offloaded via UAVs to the cloud. This coupling makes the problem challenging. A UAV can provide MEC services only during its service window at a station, so routing decisions directly determine when UAV-assisted offloading is available. Routing decisions also affect the UAV energy budget and the availability of onboard computing and communication resources for computational task execution under task deadline constraints. To address this, we propose an agentic-AI-assisted optimization framework with two components. First, we develop an agentic AI that combines large language models, retrieval-augmented generation, and chain-of-thought reasoning to translate user input into an interpretable mathematical formulation for the hybrid scheduling problem. Second, we design a hierarchical deep reinforcement learning approach based on proximal policy optimization (PPO), where the upper layer learns UAV routing and the lower layer optimizes per-slot task execution and resource allocation. Simulation results show that the proposed framework yields more consistent formulations, while the hierarchical PPO achieves full product collection in 99.6% of the last 500 episodes and maintains a 100% deadline satisfaction rate, with more stable performance than the advantage actor-critic approach.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型与思维链的智能体AI框架：面向无人机辅助物流调度与移动边缘计算
在云制造中，无人机可同时支持产品收集与移动边缘计算。这种联合操作形成了混合调度问题，其中物理物流决策与计算任务调度相互耦合。本文中，无人机从制造站收集成品并运回中央仓库，同时处理这些站点工业传感器设备产生的计算任务——可在本地、无人机端或通过无人机卸载至云端执行。该耦合性使问题具有挑战性：无人机仅在站点服务窗口内提供MEC服务，因此路由决策直接决定无人机辅助卸载的可用时间，同时影响无人机能量预算及任务截止时间约束下机载计算与通信资源的可用性。为此，我们提出一种智能体AI辅助优化框架，包含两个组件：首先开发结合大语言模型、检索增强生成与思维链推理的智能体AI，将用户输入转化为混合调度问题的可解释数学公式；其次设计基于近端策略优化的分层深度强化学习方法，上层学习无人机路由，下层优化每时隙任务执行与资源分配。仿真结果表明，该框架能生成更一致的公式，分层PPO在最后500个回合中实现99.6%的完整产品收集率并保持100%的截止时间满足率，性能比优势演员-评论家方法更稳定。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the hybrid scheduling problem in cloud manufacturing where unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) must simultaneously handle product collection and mobile edge computing (MEC) tasks, with routing decisions impacting both energy budgets and computational offloading opportunities. The authors propose an agentic-AI-assisted optimization framework that first uses large language models, retrieval-augmented generation, and chain-of-thought reasoning to convert user input into a mathematical formulation, and then employs a hierarchical deep reinforcement learning approach based on proximal policy optimization (PPO) to learn UAV routing and per-slot task execution. Simulation results demonstrate that the framework produces consistent formulations, and the hierarchical PPO achieves full product collection in 99.6% of the last 500 episodes while maintaining a 100% deadline satisfaction rate, outperforming the advantage actor-critic approach in stability.
本文针对云制造中无人机同时执行产品收集与移动边缘计算任务的混合调度问题，其中路由决策影响能量预算和计算卸载机会。作者提出了一种基于智能体AI的优化框架，首先利用大语言模型、检索增强生成和思维链推理将用户输入转化为可解释的数学公式，然后设计基于近端策略优化的分层深度强化学习方法，上层学习无人机路由，下层优化每时隙的任务执行与资源分配。仿真结果表明，该框架能生成一致的公式，分层PPO在最后500个回合中实现了99.6%的产品完全收集率和100%的截止时间满足率，且性能比优势演员-评论家方法更稳定。
GAGPO: Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization
Authors: Siyuan Zhu, Chao Yu, Rongxin Yang, Zongkai Liu, Jinjun Hu, Qiwen Chen, Yibo Zhang
First: 2026-05-13T09:10:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T09:10:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has become a powerful paradigm for post-training large language model agents, yet credit assignment in multi-turn environments remains a challenge. Agents often receive sparse, trajectory-level rewards only at the end of an episode, making it difficult to determine which intermediate actions contributed to success or failure. As a result, propagating delayed outcomes back to individual decision steps without relying on costly auxiliary value models remains an open problem. We propose Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization (GAGPO), a critic-free reinforcement learning method for precise, step-aligned temporal credit assignment. GAGPO constructs a non-parametric grouped value proxy from sampled rollouts and uses it to compute TD/GAE-style temporal advantages, recursively propagating outcome supervision backward through time. Combined with group-wise advantage normalization and an action-level importance ratio, GAGPO extracts stable, localized optimization signals directly from multi-turn trajectories. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that GAGPO outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines. Further analyses demonstrate faster early-stage learning, improved interaction efficiency, and smoother optimization dynamics, suggesting that GAGPO offers a simple yet effective framework for multi-turn agentic reinforcement learning.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of credit assignment in multi-turn reinforcement learning for large language model agents, where sparse trajectory-level rewards make it difficult to identify which intermediate actions are responsible for outcomes. The authors propose Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization (GAGPO), a critic-free method that constructs a non-parametric grouped value proxy from sampled rollouts to compute temporal advantages, enabling step-aligned credit assignment without auxiliary value models. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop demonstrate that GAGPO outperforms strong baselines, with faster early-stage learning, improved interaction efficiency, and smoother optimization dynamics.
该论文针对多轮强化学习中大型语言模型代理的信用分配难题，即稀疏的轨迹级奖励难以确定中间动作的贡献。作者提出广义优势分组策略优化（GAGPO），一种无评论家的方法，通过从采样轨迹构建非参数分组价值代理来计算时间优势，实现无需辅助价值模型的步骤级信用分配。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，GAGPO优于强基线方法，具有更快的早期学习速度、更高的交互效率和更平滑的优化动态。
VIPO: Value Function Inconsistency Penalized Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xuyang Chen, Keyu Yan, Guojian Wang, Lin Zhao
First: 2025-04-16T10:23:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T09:05:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) learns effective policies from pre-collected datasets, offering a practical solution for applications where online interactions are risky or costly. Model-based approaches are particularly advantageous for offline RL, owing to their data efficiency and generalizability. However, due to inherent model errors, model-based methods often artificially introduce conservatism guided by heuristic uncertainty estimation, which can be unreliable. In this paper, we introduce VIPO, a novel model-based offline RL algorithm that incorporates self-supervised feedback from value estimation to enhance model training. Specifically, the model is learned by additionally minimizing the inconsistency between the value learned directly from the offline data and the value estimated from the model. We perform comprehensive evaluations from multiple perspectives to show that VIPO can learn a highly accurate model efficiently and consistently outperform existing methods. In particular, it achieves state-of-the-art performance on almost all tasks in both D4RL and NeoRL benchmarks. Overall, VIPO offers a general framework that can be readily integrated into existing model-based offline RL algorithms to systematically enhance model accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VIPO：价值函数不一致性惩罚的离线强化学习
离线强化学习从预收集的数据集中学习有效策略，为在线交互存在风险或成本高昂的应用提供了实用解决方案。基于模型的方法因其数据效率和泛化能力在离线强化学习中尤为有利。然而，由于固有的模型误差，基于模型的方法常通过启发式不确定性估计人为引入保守性，这并不可靠。本文提出VIPO，一种新颖的基于模型的离线强化学习算法，它利用价值估计的自监督反馈来增强模型训练。具体而言，模型学习时额外最小化直接从离线数据中学习到的价值与从模型估计的价值之间的不一致性。我们从多个角度进行全面评估，表明VIPO能高效学习高精度模型，并持续优于现有方法。特别是在D4RL和NeoRL基准测试中，它在几乎所有任务上均达到最先进性能。总体而言，VIPO提供了一个通用框架，可轻松集成到现有基于模型的离线强化学习算法中，系统性地提升模型精度。

The paper introduces VIPO, a model-based offline reinforcement learning algorithm that addresses the challenge of unreliable conservatism from heuristic uncertainty estimation in existing methods. The key motivation is to improve model accuracy by incorporating self-supervised feedback from value estimation, where the model is trained to minimize the inconsistency between the value learned directly from offline data and the value estimated from the model. Experimental results demonstrate that VIPO consistently outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance on almost all tasks in both D4RL and NeoRL benchmarks, and offers a general framework for enhancing model accuracy in model-based offline RL.
该论文提出了VIPO，一种基于模型的离线强化学习算法，旨在解决现有方法中因启发式不确定性估计导致的不可靠保守性问题。其核心动机是通过引入价值估计的自监督反馈来提升模型准确性，具体方法是在模型训练中额外最小化直接从离线数据学到的价值与模型估计价值之间的不一致性。实验结果表明，VIPO在D4RL和NeoRL基准测试的几乎所有任务上均达到最先进性能，并提供了一个通用框架，可系统性地增强现有基于模型的离线强化学习算法的模型准确性。
Switching Successor Measures for Hierarchical Zero-shot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Stefan Stojanovic, Alexandre Proutiere
First: 2026-05-13T08:58:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:58:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Hierarchical reinforcement learning can improve generalization by decomposing long-horizon decision-making into simpler subproblems. However, existing approaches often rely on restrictive design choices, such as fixed temporal abstractions or goal-conditioned objectives, which largely confine them to goal-reaching tasks and limit their applicability to general reward functions. In this paper, we introduce switching successor measures, an extension of successor measures that enables hierarchical control in zero-shot reinforcement learning without additional supervision, fixed horizons, or manually designed subgoals. We show that switching successor measures arise naturally from classical successor measures while preserving their underlying structure. Building on this result, we propose FB $π$-Switch, an algorithm that extracts both a high-level subgoal-selection policy and a low-level control policy directly from forward-backward (FB) representations, allowing hierarchical behavior to emerge from a single learned representation. Experiments on both goal-conditioned and general reward-based tasks show that FB $π$-Switch improves over non-hierarchical baselines and matches state-of-the-art hierarchical methods in goal-conditioned settings. These results demonstrate that structured successor representations provide a flexible foundation for hierarchical zero-shot reinforcement learning beyond goal-reaching tasks. Our project website is available at: https://stestokth.github.io/switching-successors/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于分层零样本强化学习的切换后继度量
分层强化学习通过将长时决策分解为更简单的子问题来提升泛化能力。然而，现有方法常依赖固定时间抽象或目标条件目标等限制性设计选择，这使其主要局限于目标达成任务，并限制了在通用奖励函数上的适用性。本文提出切换后继度量，这是后继度量的扩展，可在无需额外监督、固定时间跨度或手动设计子目标的情况下实现零样本强化学习中的分层控制。我们证明切换后继度量自然源于经典后继度量，同时保留其底层结构。基于此结果，我们提出FB π-Switch算法，该算法直接从正向-反向表示中提取高层子目标选择策略和低层控制策略，使分层行为能从单一学习表示中涌现。在目标条件任务和通用奖励任务上的实验表明，FB π-Switch优于非分层基线，并在目标条件设置中匹配最先进的分层方法。这些结果证明，结构化后继表示为超越目标达成任务的分层零样本强化学习提供了灵活基础。项目网站见：https://stestokth.github.io/switching-successors/。

Experiments on goal-conditioned and general reward-based tasks demonstrate that FB π-Switch outperforms non-hierarchical baselines and matches state-of-the-art hierarchical methods in goal-conditioned settings, showing that structured successor representations offer a flexible foundation for hierarchical zero-shot reinforcement learning beyond goal-reaching tasks.

Finding the Weakest Link: Adversarial Attack against Multi-Agent Communications
Authors: Maxwell Standen, Junae Kim, Claudia Szabo
First: 2026-05-13T08:32:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:32:30+00:00
Comments: Full version of the Extended Abstract presented at AAMAS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent systems rely on communication for information sharing and action coordination, which exposes a vulnerability to attacks. We investigate single-victim communication perturbation attacks against Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning-trained systems and propose methods that use gradient information from the Jacobian to identify which messages, agent, and timesteps are most susceptible to attack and have the greatest impact on the system. We enhance these methods with two proposed adversarial loss functions that trade-off attack success for attack impact which also create more effective perturbations. We empirically demonstrate the effectiveness of our methods against two different multi-agent communication methods in navigation, PredatorPrey, and TrafficJunction environments. Our results show that our novel message selection method achieves a similar or greater impact than random message selection across almost all tested scenarios. Our victim selection, message selection, tempo, and loss functions improve attack effectiveness in half of the thirty scenarios we tested.
中文标题/摘要
标题：寻找最薄弱环节：针对多智能体通信的对抗性攻击
多智能体系统依赖通信进行信息共享和行动协调，这暴露了易受攻击的脆弱性。我们研究了针对多智能体强化学习训练系统的单受害者通信扰动攻击，并提出利用雅可比矩阵的梯度信息来识别哪些消息、智能体和时间步最易受攻击且对系统影响最大。我们通过两种提出的对抗性损失函数增强了这些方法，这些函数在攻击成功率和攻击影响之间进行权衡，同时产生更有效的扰动。我们通过实验证明了我们的方法在导航、捕食者-猎物和交通路口环境中针对两种不同多智能体通信方法的有效性。结果表明，我们提出的消息选择方法在几乎所有测试场景中都能达到与随机消息选择相似或更大的影响。我们的受害者选择、消息选择、时机和损失函数在测试的三十个场景中有一半提高了攻击有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates adversarial attacks on multi-agent communication systems trained with Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning, motivated by the vulnerability of inter-agent message exchanges. The authors propose methods leveraging Jacobian gradient information to identify the weakest links—specific messages, agents, and timesteps—most susceptible to perturbation, and enhance these with two novel adversarial loss functions that balance attack success and impact. Experiments in navigation, PredatorPrey, and TrafficJunction environments demonstrate that the proposed message selection method achieves similar or greater impact than random selection in almost all scenarios, while victim selection, tempo, and loss functions improve attack effectiveness in half of the thirty tested scenarios.
本文研究了针对多智能体强化学习训练系统的通信对抗攻击，动机在于多智能体系统依赖通信进行信息共享和动作协调，这暴露了易受攻击的弱点。作者提出利用雅可比矩阵梯度信息识别最易受攻击且影响最大的消息、智能体和时间步，并设计了两种权衡攻击成功率和攻击影响的对抗损失函数来增强扰动效果。在导航、捕食者-猎物和交通路口环境中的实验表明，所提出的消息选择方法在几乎所有场景中达到或超过随机选择的攻击效果，而受害者选择、消息选择、时序和损失函数在三十个测试场景中的一半中提升了攻击有效性。
DAWM: Diffusion Action World Models for Offline Reinforcement Learning via Action-Inferred Transitions
Authors: Zongyue Li, Xiao Han, Yusong Li, Niklas Strauss, Matthias Schubert
First: 2025-09-23T20:06:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:29:03+00:00
Comments: ICML2025 workshop Building Physically Plausible World Models
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion-based world models have demonstrated strong capabilities in synthesizing realistic long-horizon trajectories for offline reinforcement learning (RL). However, many existing methods do not directly generate actions alongside states and rewards, limiting their compatibility with standard value-based offline RL algorithms that rely on one-step temporal difference (TD) learning. While prior work has explored joint modeling of states, rewards, and actions to address this issue, such formulations often lead to increased training complexity and reduced performance in practice. We propose \textbf{DAWM}, a diffusion-based world model that generates future state-reward trajectories conditioned on the current state, action, and return-to-go, paired with an inverse dynamics model (IDM) for efficient action inference. This modular design produces complete synthetic transitions suitable for one-step TD-based offline RL, enabling effective and computationally efficient training. Empirically, we show that conservative offline RL algorithms such as TD3BC and IQL benefit significantly from training on these augmented trajectories, consistently outperforming prior diffusion-based baselines across multiple tasks in the D4RL benchmark.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DAWM：基于动作推断转换的扩散动作世界模型用于离线强化学习
基于扩散的世界模型在离线强化学习中展现出强大的合成逼真长程轨迹能力。然而，许多现有方法不直接生成动作与状态和奖励，限制了它们与依赖一步时序差分学习的标准基于值的离线强化学习算法的兼容性。尽管先前工作探索了联合建模状态、奖励和动作以解决此问题，但这种公式化往往导致训练复杂度增加和实际性能下降。我们提出DAWM，一种基于扩散的世界模型，它根据当前状态、动作和待实现回报生成未来状态-奖励轨迹，并配以逆动力学模型进行高效动作推断。这种模块化设计产生完整合成转换，适用于基于一步TD的离线强化学习，实现有效且计算高效的训练。实验表明，保守的离线强化学习算法（如TD3BC和IQL）通过在这些增强轨迹上训练显著受益，在D4RL基准的多个任务上持续优于先前的扩散基线。

The proposed method generates future state-reward trajectories conditioned on the current state, action, and return-to-go, and pairs this with an inverse dynamics model for efficient action inference, creating complete synthetic transitions suitable for one-step TD-based offline RL. Experimental results on the D4RL benchmark demonstrate that conservative offline RL algorithms like TD3BC and IQL significantly benefit from training on these augmented trajectories, consistently outperforming prior diffusion-based baselines across multiple tasks.

Kernel-based guarantees for nonlinear parametric models in Bayesian optimization
Authors: Rafael Oliveira
First: 2026-05-13T08:24:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:24:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern Bayesian optimization and adaptive sampling methods increasingly rely on nonlinear parametric models, yet theoretical guarantees for such models under adaptive data collection remain limited. Existing analyses largely focus on Gaussian processes, kernel machines, linear models, or linearized neural approximations, leaving a gap between theory and the nonlinear models used in practice. We develop a kernel based framework for analyzing regularized nonlinear parametric models trained on adaptively collected data. Our approach uses kernels over the parameter space to induce reproducing kernel Hilbert space structures over the corresponding model class, yielding confidence bounds for models trained with broad classes of regularized convex losses. We show how these bounds can support convergence guarantees for nonlinear acquisition and surrogate models, including randomized regularized policies that select points by maximizing a trained random model. These results provide a unified route to analyzing nonlinear parametric models in Bayesian optimization and related adaptive optimization settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：贝叶斯优化中非线性参数模型的核方法保证
现代贝叶斯优化与自适应采样方法日益依赖非线性参数模型，然而此类模型在自适应数据收集下的理论保证仍十分有限。现有分析主要集中于高斯过程、核机器、线性模型或线性化神经近似，导致理论与实践中使用的非线性模型之间存在差距。我们开发了一种基于核的框架，用于分析在自适应收集数据上训练的正则化非线性参数模型。该方法利用参数空间上的核函数，在相应模型类上诱导再生核希尔伯特空间结构，从而为使用广泛正则化凸损失训练的模型提供置信界。我们展示了这些界如何支持非线性采集函数和代理模型的收敛性保证，包括通过最大化训练随机模型来选择点的随机正则化策略。这些结果为贝叶斯优化及相关自适应优化设置中分析非线性参数模型提供了统一途径。

The paper addresses the gap between theoretical guarantees and practical use of nonlinear parametric models in Bayesian optimization, where existing analyses are limited to Gaussian processes, kernel machines, or linearized approximations. The authors propose a kernel-based framework that uses kernels over the parameter space to induce reproducing kernel Hilbert space structures, enabling confidence bounds for models trained with regularized convex losses on adaptively collected data. Experimental results demonstrate that these bounds support convergence guarantees for nonlinear acquisition functions and surrogate models, including randomized regularized policies, providing a unified theoretical foundation for nonlinear parametric models in adaptive optimization settings.

GESR: A Genetic Programming-Based Symbolic Regression Method with Gene Editing
Authors: Yanjie Li, Liping Zhang, Min Wu, Weijun Li, Lina Yu, Jingyi Liu, Yusong Deng, Mingzhu Wan, Xin Ning
First: 2026-05-11T15:00:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:20:22+00:00
Comments: 70 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mathematical formulas serve as a language through which humans communicate with nature. Discovering mathematical laws from scientific data to describe natural phenomena has been a long-standing pursuit of humanity for centuries. In the field of artificial intelligence, this challenge is known as the symbolic regression problem. Among existing symbolic regression approaches, Genetic Programming (GP) based on evolutionary algorithms remains one of the most classical and widely adopted methods. GP simulates the evolutionary process across generations through genetic mutation and crossover. However, mutations and crossovers in GP are entirely random. While this randomness effectively mimics natural evolution, it inevitably produces both beneficial and detrimental variations. If there existed a metaphorical `God` capable of foreseeing which genetic mutations or crossovers would yield superior outcomes and performing targeted gene editing accordingly, the efficiency of evolution could be substantially improved. Motivated by this idea, we propose in this paper a symbolic regression approach based on gene editing, termed GESR. In GESR, we trained two "hands of God" (two BERT models). Among them, the first leverages the BERT's masked language modeling capability to guide the mutation of genes (expression symbols). The other BERT model guides the crossover of individual genes by predicting the crossover point. Experimental results demonstrate that GESR significantly improves computational efficiency compared with traditional GP algorithms and achieves strong overall performance across multiple symbolic regression tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GESR：一种基于基因编辑的遗传编程符号回归方法
数学公式是人类与自然沟通的语言。从科学数据中发现数学规律以描述自然现象，是数百年来人类不懈的追求。在人工智能领域，这一挑战被称为符号回归问题。在现有的符号回归方法中，基于进化算法的遗传编程（GP）仍是最经典且广泛采用的方法之一。GP通过基因突变和交叉模拟逐代进化过程。然而，GP中的突变和交叉完全随机。这种随机性虽有效模拟了自然进化，但不可避免地同时产生有益和有害的变异。如果存在一个隐喻性的“上帝”，能够预见哪些基因突变或交叉会产生更优结果，并进行靶向基因编辑，进化效率将大幅提升。受此启发，本文提出一种基于基因编辑的符号回归方法，称为GESR。在GESR中，我们训练了两个“上帝之手”（两个BERT模型）。其中，第一个利用BERT的掩码语言建模能力指导基因（表达式符号）的突变。另一个BERT模型通过预测交叉点来指导个体基因的交叉。实验结果表明，与传统GP算法相比，GESR显著提高了计算效率，并在多个符号回归任务中取得了优异的整体性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes GESR, a genetic programming-based symbolic regression method enhanced with gene editing to overcome the inefficiency of random mutations and crossovers in traditional GP. The key idea is to train two BERT models as 'hands of God': one uses masked language modeling to guide beneficial gene mutations, and the other predicts optimal crossover points. Experimental results show that GESR significantly improves computational efficiency and achieves strong overall performance across multiple symbolic regression tasks compared to conventional GP algorithms.
该论文提出了一种基于基因编辑的遗传编程符号回归方法GESR，旨在解决传统GP中随机变异和交叉导致的效率低下问题。核心思路是训练两个BERT模型作为“上帝之手”：一个利用掩码语言建模能力指导有益的基因变异，另一个通过预测交叉点来引导个体基因的交叉。实验结果表明，与传统的GP算法相比，GESR显著提高了计算效率，并在多个符号回归任务中取得了优异的整体性能。
The Horizon Threshold in Cooperative Multi-Agent Reward-Free Exploration
Authors: Idan Barnea, Orin Levy, Yishay Mansour
First: 2026-02-01T21:44:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:02:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning in the setting of reward-free exploration, where multiple agents jointly explore an unknown MDP in order to learn its dynamics (without observing rewards). We focus on a tabular finite-horizon MDP and adopt a phased learning framework. In each learning phase, multiple agents independently interact with the environment. More specifically, in each learning phase, each agent is assigned a policy, executes it, and observes the resulting trajectory. Our primary goal is to characterize the tradeoff between the number of learning phases and the number of agents, especially when the number of learning phases is small. Our results identify a regime change governed by the horizon $H$. When the number of learning phases equals $H$, we present a computationally efficient algorithm that uses only $\tilde{O}(S^6 H^6 A / ε^2)$ agents to obtain an $ε$ approximation of the dynamics (i.e., yields an $ε$-optimal policy for any reward function). We complement our algorithm with a lower bound showing that any algorithm restricted to $ρ< H$ phases requires at least $A^{H/ρ}$ agents to achieve constant accuracy. Thus, we show that having $Θ(H)$ learning phases is both necessary and sufficient when restricting the number of agents to be polynomial.

我们研究了无奖励探索场景下的协作多智能体强化学习，其中多个智能体共同探索未知的马尔可夫决策过程以学习其动态（不观察奖励）。我们聚焦于表格型有限视界马尔可夫决策过程，并采用分阶段学习框架。在每个学习阶段，多个智能体独立与环境交互。具体而言，每个学习阶段中，每个智能体被分配一个策略，执行该策略，并观察生成的轨迹。我们的主要目标是刻画学习阶段数量与智能体数量之间的权衡，尤其是在学习阶段数量较少的情况下。 我们的结果揭示了由视界$H$主导的机制转变。当学习阶段数量等于$H$时，我们提出了一种计算高效的算法，仅需使用$\tilde{O}(S^6 H^6 A / ε^2)$个智能体即可获得动态的$ε$近似（即为任意奖励函数生成$ε$最优策略）。我们通过下界补充了该算法，表明任何限制在$ρ< H$个阶段的算法至少需要$A^{H/ρ}$个智能体才能达到恒定精度。因此，我们证明当限制智能体数量为多项式时，拥有$Θ(H)$个学习阶段既是必要的也是充分的。

ERPPO: Entropy Regularization-based Proximal Policy Optimization
Authors: Changha Lee, Gyusang Cho
First: 2026-05-13T08:01:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:01:20+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) is a variant of the Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) algorithm, specifically tailored for multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). MAPPO optimizes cooperative multi-agent settings by employing a centralized critic with decentralized actors. However, in case of multi-dimensional environment, MAPPO can not extract optimal policy due to non-stationary agent observation. To overcome this problem, we introduce a novel approach, Entropy Regularization-based Proximal Policy Optimization (ERPPO). For the policy optimization, we first define the object detection ambiguity under multi-dimensional observation environment. Distributional Spatiotemporal Ambiguity (DSA) learner is trained to estimate object detection uncertainty in non-stationary constraints. Then, we enhance PPO with a novel Entropy Regularization term. This regularization dynamically adjusts the policy update by applying a stronger (L1) regularization in high-ambiguity observation to encourage significant exploratory actions and a weaker (L2) regularization in low-ambiguity observation to stabilize the proximal policy optimization. This approach is designed to enhance the probability of successful object localization in time-critical operations by reducing detection failures and optimizing search policy. Experiments on a testbed with AirSim-based maritime searching scenarios show that the proposed ERPPO improves accuracy performance. Our proposed method improves higher gradient than MAPPO. Qualitative results confirm that ERPPO effectiveness in terms of suppressing false detection in visually uncertain conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ERPPO：基于熵正则化的近端策略优化
多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO）是近端策略优化（PPO）算法的一种变体，专门针对多智能体强化学习（MARL）设计。MAPPO通过采用集中式评论家与分散式行动者来优化合作性多智能体场景。然而，在多维环境情况下，由于智能体观测的非平稳性，MAPPO无法提取最优策略。为解决此问题，我们提出了一种新方法——基于熵正则化的近端策略优化（ERPPO）。在策略优化中，我们首先定义了多维观测环境下的目标检测模糊性。分布时空模糊性（DSA）学习器被训练用于估计非平稳约束下的目标检测不确定性。然后，我们通过引入一种新颖的熵正则化项来增强PPO。该正则化通过在高模糊性观测中应用更强的L1正则化以鼓励显著的探索性动作，并在低模糊性观测中应用较弱的L2正则化以稳定近端策略优化，从而动态调整策略更新。该方法旨在通过减少检测失败和优化搜索策略，提高时间关键操作中成功定位目标的概率。在基于AirSim的海上搜索场景测试平台上的实验表明，所提出的ERPPO提升了准确率性能。我们的方法相比MAPPO获得了更高的梯度。定性结果证实了ERPPO在视觉不确定条件下抑制虚假检测的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) in extracting optimal policies under multi-dimensional environments due to non-stationary agent observations. To overcome this, the authors propose Entropy Regularization-based Proximal Policy Optimization (ERPPO), which introduces a Distributional Spatiotemporal Ambiguity (DSA) learner to estimate object detection uncertainty and incorporates a novel entropy regularization term into PPO. This term applies stronger L1 regularization in high-ambiguity observations to encourage exploration and weaker L2 regularization in low-ambiguity observations to stabilize updates. Experiments on AirSim-based maritime searching scenarios demonstrate that ERPPO achieves higher gradient improvements and effectively suppresses false detections in visually uncertain conditions compared to MAPPO.
该论文针对多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO）在多维环境中因智能体观测非平稳而无法提取最优策略的问题，提出了一种基于熵正则化的近端策略优化方法（ERPPO）。该方法通过训练分布时空模糊度（DSA）学习器来估计非平稳约束下的目标检测不确定性，并在PPO中引入新的熵正则化项：在高模糊度观测下使用更强的L1正则化以鼓励探索性动作，在低模糊度观测下使用较弱的L2正则化以稳定策略优化。在基于AirSim的海上搜索场景测试中，实验结果表明ERPPO相比MAPPO获得了更高的梯度提升，并在视觉不确定条件下有效抑制了误检。
TMPO: Trajectory Matching Policy Optimization for Diverse and Efficient Diffusion Alignment
Authors: Jiaming Li, Chenyu Zhu, Nanxi Yi, Youjun Bao, Li Sun, Quanying Lv, Xiang Fang, Daizong Liu, Jianjun Li, Kun He, Bowen Zhou, Zhiyuan Ma
First: 2026-05-09T04:41:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T08:00:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has shown extraordinary potential in aligning diffusion models to downstream tasks, yet most of them still suffer from significant reward hacking, which degrades generative diversity and quality by inducing visual mode collapse and amplifying unreliable rewards. We identify the root cause as the mode-seeking nature of these methods, which maximize expected reward without effectively constraining probability distribution over acceptable trajectories, causing concentration on a few high-reward paths. In contrast, we propose Trajectory Matching Policy Optimization (TMPO), which replaces scalar reward maximization with trajectory-level reward distribution matching. Specifically, TMPO introduces a Softmax Trajectory Balance (Softmax-TB) objective to match the policy probabilities of K trajectories to a reward-induced Boltzmann distribution. We prove that this objective inherits the mode-covering property of forward KL divergence, preserving coverage over all acceptable trajectories while optimizing reward. To further reduce multi-trajectory training time on large-scale flow-matching models, TMPO incorporates Dynamic Stochastic Tree Sampling, where trajectories share denoising prefixes and branch at dynamically scheduled steps, reducing redundant computation while improving training effectiveness. Extensive results across diverse alignment tasks such as human preference, compositional generation and text rendering show that TMPO improves generative diversity over state-of-the-art methods by 9.1%, and achieves competitive performance in all downstream and efficiency metrics, attaining the optimal trade-off between reward and diversity.
Sharpness-Guided Group Relative Policy Optimization via Probability Shaping
Authors: Tue Le, Linh Ngo Van, Trung Le
First: 2025-10-29T08:07:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T07:57:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become a practical route to improve large language model reasoning, and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is a widely used optimizer in this setting. However, RLVR training is typically performed with limited control over generalization. We revisit GRPO through a robustness-based generalization view, where the generalization loss is upper bounded by a combination of the empirical loss and a sharpness surrogate measured by the gradient norm. Building on this perspective, we propose Sharpness-Guided GRPO (GRPO-SG), a simple token-weighted variant of GRPO that downweights tokens likely to cause overly large gradients, reducing sharp updates and stabilizing optimization, thereby improving generalization. Experiments across mathematical reasoning, logic puzzles and tool-augmented question answering show consistent improvements over GRPO, along with smoother gradient-norm trajectories, supporting GRPO-SG as a simple and effective generalization-oriented upgrade to GRPO for RLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于概率塑形的锐度引导组相对策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的实用途径，其中组相对策略优化（GRPO）是该场景下广泛使用的优化器。然而，RLVR训练通常对泛化能力的控制有限。我们从基于鲁棒性的泛化视角重新审视GRPO，发现泛化损失的上界由经验损失与梯度范数度量的锐度替代项共同界定。基于此视角，我们提出锐度引导GRPO（GRPO-SG），这是一种简单的GRPO词元加权变体，通过降低易引发过大梯度的词元权重，减少剧烈更新并稳定优化过程，从而提升泛化性能。在数学推理、逻辑谜题和工具增强问答等任务上的实验表明，GRPO-SG相较于GRPO具有持续改进效果，同时梯度范数轨迹更平滑，验证了GRPO-SG作为面向泛化的GRPO简单有效升级方案在RLVR中的价值。

Test-time Offline Reinforcement Learning on Goal-related Experience
Authors: Marco Bagatella, Mert Albaba, Jonas Hübotter, Georg Martius, Andreas Krause
First: 2025-07-24T21:11:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T07:56:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Foundation models compress a large amount of information in a single, large neural network, which can then be queried for individual tasks. There are strong parallels between this widespread framework and offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning algorithms: a universal value function is trained on a large number of goals, and the policy is evaluated on a single goal in each test episode. Extensive research in foundation models has shown that performance can be substantially improved through test-time training, specializing the model to the current goal. We find similarly that test-time offline reinforcement learning on experience related to the test goal can lead to substantially better policies at modest compute costs. We propose a novel self-supervised data selection criterion, which selects transitions from an offline dataset according to their relevance to the current state and quality with respect to the evaluation goal. We demonstrate across a wide range of high-dimensional loco-navigation and manipulation tasks that fine-tuning a policy on the selected data for a few gradient steps leads to significant performance gains over standard offline pre-training. Our goal-conditioned test-time training (GC-TTT) algorithm applies this routine in a receding-horizon fashion during evaluation, adapting the policy to the current trajectory as it is being rolled out. Finally, we study compute allocation at inference, demonstrating that, at comparable costs, GC-TTT induces performance gains that are not achievable by scaling model size.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于目标相关经验的测试时离线强化学习
基础模型将大量信息压缩到单个大型神经网络中，随后可针对特定任务进行查询。这种广泛应用的框架与离线目标条件强化学习算法存在显著相似性：通用价值函数在大量目标上训练，而策略在每个测试回合中针对单一目标进行评估。基础模型的大量研究表明，通过测试时训练（使模型专门适应当前目标）可显著提升性能。我们同样发现，针对测试目标相关经验进行测试时离线强化学习，能以适中的计算成本获得更优策略。我们提出一种新颖的自监督数据选择准则，根据离线数据集中转换与当前状态的相关性及其对评估目标的质量进行筛选。在多种高维运动导航与操作任务中，我们证明：对所选数据进行少量梯度步的微调，其性能显著优于标准离线预训练。我们的目标条件测试时训练（GC-TTT）算法在评估过程中以滚动时域方式应用该流程，使策略在轨迹生成过程中自适应调整。最后，我们研究了推理时的计算资源分配，证明在可比成本下，GC-TTT带来的性能提升无法通过扩大模型规模实现。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of improving offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning by adapting the policy at test time, drawing inspiration from test-time training in foundation models. The authors propose a novel self-supervised data selection criterion that picks transitions from an offline dataset based on their relevance to the current state and quality relative to the evaluation goal. Their method, called GC-TTT, fine-tunes the policy on this selected data for a few gradient steps in a receding-horizon fashion during evaluation. Experiments on high-dimensional loco-navigation and manipulation tasks show that this approach yields significant performance gains over standard offline pre-training, and that at comparable compute costs, GC-TTT outperforms scaling model size.
该论文针对离线目标条件强化学习在测试时适应策略的问题，借鉴基础模型中的测试时训练思想。作者提出了一种新颖的自监督数据选择标准，根据当前状态的相关性和评估目标的质量，从离线数据集中挑选转换样本。其方法GC-TTT在评估过程中以滚动时域方式对选定数据进行少量梯度步的微调。在高维运动导航和操作任务上的实验表明，该方法相比标准离线预训练取得了显著的性能提升，并且在相同计算成本下，GC-TTT优于扩大模型规模的效果。
Centralized Adaptive Sampling for Reliable Co-Training of Independent Multi-Agent Policies
Authors: Nicholas E. Corrado, Josiah P. Hanna
First: 2025-08-01T20:07:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T06:44:44+00:00
Comments: RLC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Independent on-policy policy gradient algorithms are widely used for multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) in cooperative and no-conflict games, but they are known to converge sub-optimally when each agent's individual policy gradient points away from an optimal joint equilibrium. Going beyond prior work, we observe that sub-optimal convergence can still arise even when the expected individual policy gradients of each agent point toward the optimal joint solution. After collecting a finite set of trajectories, stochasticity in independent action sampling can cause the joint data distribution to deviate from the expected joint on-policy distribution. This \textit{sampling error} w.r.t. the joint on-policy distribution produces inaccurate gradient estimates that can make agents converge sub-optimally. We hypothesize that joint sampling error can be reduced through coordinated action selection and that doing so will increase the reliability of policy gradient learning in MARL (i.e., the probability of converging to an optimal joint policy). To test this hypothesis, we first introduce an adaptive action sampling approach to reduce joint sampling error in the Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution setting. Our method, Cooperative Sampling Error Reduction (CoSER), continually adapts a centralized behavior policy to place higher probability on joint actions that are under-sampled w.r.t. the current joint policy. We then empirically evaluate CoSER on a diverse set of multi-agent games and demonstrate that (1) CoSER reduces joint sampling error more efficiently than independent on-policy sampling and (2) this reduction increases the reliability of independent policy gradient algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向独立多智能体策略可靠协同训练的中心化自适应采样
独立同策略策略梯度算法广泛应用于合作与无冲突博弈中的多智能体强化学习，但已知当每个智能体的个体策略梯度偏离最优联合均衡时，此类算法会收敛至次优解。超越先前研究，我们观察到即使每个智能体的期望个体策略梯度指向最优联合解，次优收敛仍可能发生。在收集有限轨迹集后，独立动作采样的随机性会导致联合数据分布偏离期望的联合同策略分布。这种关于联合同策略分布的采样误差会产生不准确的梯度估计，使智能体收敛至次优解。我们假设通过协调动作选择可减少联合采样误差，且此举将提升多智能体强化学习中策略梯度学习的可靠性（即收敛至最优联合策略的概率）。为验证该假设，我们首先在集中训练分散执行框架下引入一种自适应动作采样方法以减少联合采样误差。我们的方法——协同采样误差缩减——持续调整集中式行为策略，对当前联合策略下采样不足的联合动作赋予更高概率。随后我们在多种多智能体博弈中实证评估CoSER，证明：(1) CoSER比独立同策略采样更高效地减少联合采样误差；(2) 这种减少提升了独立策略梯度算法的可靠性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses sub-optimal convergence in independent on-policy policy gradient algorithms for multi-agent reinforcement learning, even when expected gradients point toward optimal joint solutions. The authors identify that stochasticity in independent action sampling causes joint data distribution to deviate from the expected on-policy distribution, leading to inaccurate gradient estimates. To mitigate this, they propose Cooperative Sampling Error Reduction (CoSER), an adaptive centralized sampling method that reduces joint sampling error by prioritizing under-sampled joint actions during centralized training with decentralized execution. Experiments on diverse multi-agent games show that CoSER reduces joint sampling error more efficiently than independent on-policy sampling and improves the reliability of policy gradient learning.
该论文研究了独立同策略策略梯度算法在多智能体强化学习中即使每个智能体的期望梯度指向最优联合解时仍会出现次优收敛的问题。作者发现独立动作采样的随机性导致联合数据分布偏离期望的同策略分布，从而产生不准确的梯度估计。为此，他们提出了一种自适应集中式采样方法CoSER，通过在集中训练分散执行框架下优先采样当前联合策略下采样不足的联合动作来减少联合采样误差。在多种多智能体游戏上的实验表明，CoSER比独立同策略采样更有效地降低了联合采样误差，并提高了策略梯度学习的可靠性。
expo: Exploration-prioritized policy optimization via adaptive kl regulation and gaussian curriculum sampling
Authors: Mingxiong Lin, Zhangquan Gong, Maowen Tang, Qian Li, Chuangchuang Wang, Jian Ma, Sutian Huang, Kai Tang, Haonan Lu
First: 2026-05-11T03:19:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T06:42:03+00:00
Comments: Duplicate submission of arXiv:2605.11403
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the standard paradigm for LLM mathematical reasoning, where Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) serves as the mainstream algorithm. We point out two understudied inefficiencies existing in GRPO. First, the fixed KL penalty coefficient overly restricts policy exploration at stages where the model requires significant deviation from the reference policy. Second, uniform sampling of training questions ignores that moderately difficult problems provide the most informative gradient signals for optimization. We propose Exploration-Prioritized Policy Optimization (EXPO) with two lightweight plug-in modules. The Accuracy-Conditioned KL Scaling (AKL) dynamically adjusts KL regularization strength through a smooth nonlinear function of batch average accuracy, relaxing the penalty when the model underperforms and strengthening it when the model achieves good results. The Gaussian Curriculum Sampling (GCS) assigns sampling weights to questions following a Gaussian distribution centered at moderate accuracy around 0.5, focusing training on the model's learning frontier. We conduct extensive experiments on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B and Qwen3-8B-Base over six mathematical reasoning benchmarks. The results show EXPO steadily surpasses vanilla GRPO. It obtains an absolute gain of 13.34 on AIME 2025 pass@32, rising from 63.33 percent to 76.67 percent, and achieves an average pass@32 improvement of 2.66 on the 8B model. The much larger performance gains on pass@32 compared with pass@1 demonstrate that EXPO effectively enlarges the model's exploration boundary under a fixed inference cost budget.
中文标题/摘要
标题：expo：基于自适应KL调节与高斯课程采样的探索优先策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为大语言模型数学推理的标准范式，其中组相对策略优化（GRPO）是主流算法。我们指出GRPO存在两个未被充分研究的低效问题。首先，固定的KL惩罚系数在模型需要显著偏离参考策略的阶段过度限制了策略探索。其次，训练问题的均匀采样忽略了中等难度问题能为优化提供最具信息量的梯度信号。我们提出探索优先策略优化（EXPO），包含两个轻量级即插即用模块。准确率条件KL缩放（AKL）通过批次平均准确率的平滑非线性函数动态调整KL正则化强度，在模型表现不佳时放松惩罚，在模型取得良好结果时加强惩罚。高斯课程采样（GCS）以中等准确率（约0.5）为中心的高斯分布为问题分配采样权重，将训练聚焦于模型的学习前沿。我们在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B和Qwen3-8B-Base上，针对六个数学推理基准进行了大量实验。结果表明EXPO稳定超越原始GRPO。在AIME 2025 pass@32上获得13.34的绝对增益，从63.33%提升至76.67%，并在8B模型上实现pass@32平均提升2.66。与pass@1相比，pass@32上更大的性能增益表明EXPO在固定推理成本预算下有效扩大了模型的探索边界。
Selective Off-Policy Reference Tuning with Plan Guidance
Authors: Duc Anh Le, Tien-Phat Nguyen, Thien Huu Nguyen, Linh Ngo Van, Trung Le
First: 2026-05-12T04:25:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T06:41:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards helps reasoning, but GRPO-style methods stall on hard prompts where all sampled rollouts fail. SORT adds a repair update for those failures without changing rollout generation: it derives a plan from the reference solution, compares token probabilities with and without that plan, and gives higher weight to tokens that become more predictable under plan conditioning. This turns all-wrong prompts into selective, structure-aware learning signals instead of uniform imitation. Across three backbones and eight reasoning benchmarks, SORT improves over GRPO and guidance baselines, with largest gains on weaker models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于计划引导的选择性离策略参考调优
基于可验证奖励的强化学习有助于推理，但GRPO风格的方法在困难提示上会停滞，因为所有采样轨迹均失败。SORT针对这些失败添加了修复更新，而不改变轨迹生成方式：它从参考解中推导出计划，比较有无该计划下的词元概率，并对在计划条件下变得更可预测的词元赋予更高权重。这将全错提示转化为选择性、结构感知的学习信号，而非统一模仿。在三个骨干网络和八个推理基准上，SORT相比GRPO及引导基线均有提升，且在较弱模型上增益最大。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes Selective Off-Policy Reference Tuning (SORT) to address the limitation of GRPO-style reinforcement learning methods that stall on hard prompts where all sampled rollouts fail. SORT introduces a repair update that derives a plan from the reference solution, compares token probabilities with and without plan conditioning, and assigns higher weight to tokens that become more predictable under plan guidance, thereby converting all-wrong prompts into selective, structure-aware learning signals. Experimental results across three backbones and eight reasoning benchmarks show that SORT consistently outperforms GRPO and guidance baselines, with the largest gains observed on weaker models.
