High-Order Epistasis Detection Using Factorization Machine with Quadratic Optimization Annealing and MDR-Based Evaluation
Authors: Shuta Kikuchi, Shu Tanaka
Venue: 2026 International Conference on Quantum Communications, Networking, and Computing (QCNC), pp. 924-929
First: 2026-01-05T07:41:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T06:27:59+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Detecting high-order epistasis is a fundamental challenge in genetic association studies due to the combinatorial explosion of candidate locus combinations. Although multifactor dimensionality reduction (MDR) is a widely used method for evaluating epistasis, exhaustive MDR-based searches become computationally infeasible as the number of loci or the interaction order increases. In this paper, we define the epistasis detection problem as a black-box optimization problem and solve it with a factorization machine with quadratic-optimization annealing (FMQA). We propose an efficient epistasis detection method based on FMQA, in which the classification error rate (CER) computed by MDR is used as a black-box objective function. Experimental evaluations were conducted using simulated case-control datasets with predefined high-order epistasis. The results demonstrate that the proposed method successfully identified ground-truth epistasis across various interaction orders and the numbers of genetic loci within a limited number of iterations. These results indicate that the proposed method is effective and computationally efficient for high-order epistasis detection.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于二次优化退火的因子机与MDR评估的高阶上位性检测
检测高阶上位性是遗传关联研究中的一个基本挑战，因为候选位点组合存在组合爆炸问题。尽管多因子降维法（MDR）是评估上位性的常用方法，但随着位点数量或交互阶数的增加，基于MDR的穷举搜索在计算上变得不可行。本文将上位性检测问题定义为黑箱优化问题，并使用带有二次优化退火的因子机（FMQA）进行求解。我们提出了一种基于FMQA的高效上位性检测方法，其中MDR计算的分类错误率（CER）被用作黑箱目标函数。使用具有预定义高阶上位性的模拟病例对照数据集进行了实验评估。结果表明，所提方法在有限迭代次数内成功识别了不同交互阶数和遗传位点数量的真实上位性。这些结果表明，所提方法对于高阶上位性检测是有效且计算高效的。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of detecting high-order epistasis in genetic association studies, where exhaustive searches become computationally infeasible due to combinatorial explosion. The authors propose a method that formulates epistasis detection as a black-box optimization problem, solved using a factorization machine with quadratic optimization annealing (FMQA), with the classification error rate from multifactor dimensionality reduction (MDR) serving as the objective function. Experiments on simulated case-control datasets with predefined high-order epistasis show that the method successfully identifies ground-truth interactions across various orders and numbers of loci within limited iterations, demonstrating its effectiveness and computational efficiency.
该论文针对遗传关联研究中高阶上位性检测的挑战，即由于候选位点组合爆炸导致穷举搜索在计算上不可行。作者提出了一种方法，将上位性检测定义为黑箱优化问题，并使用带有二次优化退火的因子分解机（FMQA）求解，其中以多因子降维（MDR）计算的分类错误率作为目标函数。在具有预定义高阶上位性的模拟病例对照数据集上的实验表明，该方法能在有限迭代次数内成功识别各种交互阶数和遗传位点数量的真实上位性，证明了其有效性和计算效率。
Bridging Domain Gaps with Target-Aligned Generation for Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Minung Kim, Jeongmo Kim, Gwanwoo Choi, Seungyul Han
First: 2026-05-13T06:23:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T06:23:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cross-domain offline reinforcement learning aims to adapt a policy from a source domain to a target domain using only pre-collected datasets, where environment dynamics may differ. A key challenge is to leverage source data while reducing distributional mismatch, particularly when the target dataset is extremely limited. To address this, we propose Target-aligned Coverage Expansion (TCE), a framework that decides how source data should be used, either by directly incorporating target-near transitions or by expanding state coverage through target-aligned generation, guided by theoretical analysis. TCE builds on a dual score-based generative model to synthesize target-consistent transitions over an expanded state region. Extensive experiments across diverse cross-domain environments show that TCE consistently outperforms state-of-the-art cross-domain offline RL baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向离线强化学习的跨域桥接：基于目标对齐生成弥合领域差距
跨域离线强化学习旨在仅利用预收集数据集，将策略从源域迁移至环境动态可能不同的目标域。核心挑战在于在目标数据集极度有限时，既能利用源数据又能减少分布不匹配。为此，我们提出目标对齐覆盖扩展（TCE）框架，通过理论分析指导源数据的使用方式：直接整合接近目标的转移数据，或通过目标对齐生成扩展状态覆盖。TCE基于双评分生成模型，在扩展状态区域合成与目标一致的转移数据。跨多种跨域环境的实验表明，TCE持续优于最先进的跨域离线强化学习基线方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses cross-domain offline reinforcement learning, where a policy must be adapted from a source to a target domain with differing dynamics using only pre-collected data, a challenge exacerbated by limited target datasets. To mitigate distributional mismatch, the authors propose Target-aligned Coverage Expansion (TCE), a framework that theoretically guides the use of source data either by incorporating target-near transitions or by generating target-aligned transitions via a dual score-based generative model to expand state coverage. Extensive experiments across diverse cross-domain environments demonstrate that TCE consistently outperforms state-of-the-art cross-domain offline RL baselines.
该论文针对跨领域离线强化学习问题，即仅利用预收集数据将策略从源领域适应到动态环境不同的目标领域，尤其在目标数据集极其有限时面临分布不匹配的挑战。为此，作者提出目标对齐覆盖扩展（TCE）框架，通过理论分析指导源数据的使用方式，要么直接整合接近目标状态的转移，要么利用双评分生成模型合成目标一致的转移以扩展状态覆盖。在多种跨领域环境中的大量实验表明，TCE始终优于最先进的跨领域离线强化学习基线方法。
Multi-Dimensional Behavioral Evaluation of Agentic Stock Prediction Systems Using Large Language Model Judges with Closed-Loop Reinforcement Learning Feedback
Authors: Mohammad Al Ridhawi, Mahtab Haj Ali, Hussein Al Osman
First: 2026-05-07T06:31:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T05:25:23+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 5 figures, 14 tables. Research Article submitted to Journal of Forecasting (Wiley)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Forecast evaluation in finance has relied on aggregate accuracy metrics and predictive-accuracy tests built on point-forecast errors. These instruments evaluate forecast outputs but cannot evaluate the process of forecast generation, which is increasingly relevant as forecasting systems become agentic, issuing forecasts through sequences of interdependent autonomous decisions whose individual quality is hidden by output-level errors. We propose a behavioral forecast-evaluation methodology that complements accuracy tests by assessing the intermediate decision process itself. Behavioral traces logged at every autonomous decision point are grouped into five-day episodes and scored along six domain-specific dimensions (regime detection, routing, adaptation, risk calibration, strategy coherence, error recovery) by an ensemble of three large language model (LLM) judges. A perturbation procedure that corrupts one dimension while leaving the other five intact confirms dimension specificity, with cross-model agreement reaching Krippendorff's $α= 0.85$. The composite behavioral score correlates at Spearman $ρ= 0.72$ with realized 20-day Sharpe ratio from offline backtesting. Closing the loop, the framework converts deficient per-dimension scores into a credit-assigned penalty added to the Soft Actor-Critic reward. Three fine-tuning cycles, confined to the validation period, produce on the held-out 2017-2025 test period a one-day MAPE reduction from 0.61% to 0.54% (11.5% relative; $p<0.001$, Cohen's $d=0.31$), significant under a Diebold-Mariano test of equal predictive accuracy ($\mathrm{DM}=-7.83$) and localized by a Giacomini-White conditional predictive ability test to the high-volatility regime. The methodology is application-agnostic. Results are from offline backtesting and do not address effects specific to live deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型评委与闭环强化学习反馈的智能股票预测系统多维度行为评估
金融领域的预测评估历来依赖基于点预测误差的总体准确率指标和预测精度检验。这些工具评估预测输出，但无法评估预测生成过程——随着预测系统变得智能化，通过一系列相互依赖的自主决策序列发布预测，其单个决策质量被输出级误差所掩盖，这一过程评估日益重要。我们提出一种行为预测评估方法，通过评估中间决策过程本身来补充精度检验。在每个自主决策点记录的行为轨迹被分组为五天片段，并由三个大语言模型评委组成的集成系统沿着六个领域特定维度（状态检测、路由、适应、风险校准、策略一致性、错误恢复）进行评分。一种扰动程序（破坏一个维度而保持其他五个维度完整）确认了维度特异性，跨模型一致性达到Krippendorff's α=0.85。复合行为评分与离线回测中实现的20天夏普比率呈Spearman ρ=0.72的相关性。在闭环中，该框架将每个维度的不足评分转换为信用分配惩罚，添加到Soft Actor-Critic奖励中。三个微调周期（限于验证期）在保留的2017-2025年测试期内将一天MAPE从0.61%降至0.54%（相对降低11.5%；p<0.001，Cohen's d=0.31），在Diebold-Mariano等预测精度检验中显著（DM=-7.83），并通过Giacomini-White条件预测能力检验定位到高波动状态。该方法论与应用无关。结果来自离线回测，不涉及实时部署特有的影响。
Summary / 总结
This paper proposes a behavioral evaluation methodology for agentic stock prediction systems, motivated by the limitation of traditional aggregate accuracy metrics that cannot assess the intermediate decision process. The method logs behavioral traces at each autonomous decision point, groups them into five-day episodes, and scores them along six domain-specific dimensions using an ensemble of three LLM judges. A perturbation procedure confirms dimension specificity with cross-model agreement at Krippendorff's α=0.85, and the composite behavioral score correlates with realized 20-day Sharpe ratio at Spearman ρ=0.72. By converting deficient per-dimension scores into a credit-assigned penalty added to the Soft Actor-Critic reward, three fine-tuning cycles reduce one-day MAPE from 0.61% to 0.54% (11.5% relative; p<0.001) on the held-out 2017-2025 test period, with significance confirmed by Diebold-Mariano and Giacomini-White tests.
本文提出了一种针对智能体股票预测系统的行为评估方法，其动机在于传统聚合准确率指标无法评估中间决策过程。该方法记录每个自主决策点的行为轨迹，将数据分组为五天一个的片段，并由三个大语言模型评审员组成的集成系统在六个领域特定维度上进行评分。扰动实验证实了维度特异性，跨模型一致性达到Krippendorff α=0.85，且综合行为评分与回测中实现的20天夏普比率之间的斯皮尔曼相关系数为0.72。通过将有缺陷的维度得分转换为信用分配惩罚项并加入软演员-评论家奖励，三个微调周期在2017-2025年测试集上将一日MAPE从0.61%降至0.54%（相对降低11.5%，p<0.001），Diebold-Mariano和Giacomini-White检验均证实了显著性。
JEDI: Joint Embedding Diffusion World Model for Online Model-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jing Yu Lim, Rushi Shah, Zarif Ikram, Samson Yu, Haozhe Ma, Tze-Yun Leong, Dianbo Liu
First: 2026-05-13T05:07:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T05:07:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion world models have recently become competitive for online model-based reinforcement learning, but current approaches expose a tension: pixel diffusion is effective but computationally expensive while the latest latent diffusion approach improves efficiency yet performs subpar. The latter also relies on separately trained latents rather than the end-to-end world-model objectives that have driven much of modern MBRL progress. In particular, JEPA-style predictive representation learning has emerged as an especially promising direction for world modeling and MBRL. Concurrently, diffusion-style objectives have gained traction across multiple domains, with iterative refinement as a promising approach for multimodal and stochastic targets. Taken together, these trends motivate Joint Embedding DIffusion (JEDI), the first online end-to-end latent diffusion world model. JEDI learns its latent space directly from the diffusion denoising loss with a JEPA framework, using denoising to learn and predict future latents rather than relying on reconstruction and pretrained models. We provide a theoretical motivation showing that conventional JEPA objectives induce a predictive information bottleneck, and that conditional diffusion denoising admits a closely related predictive-compression decomposition. Empirically, JEDI is competitive on Atari100k and outperforms the baseline with seperately trained latents where directly comparable. Relative to the pixel diffusion baseline, JEDI uses 43% less VRAM, over 3$\times$ faster world-model sampling, and 2.5$\times$ faster training. JEDI also exhibits a markedly different task-level performance profile from the pixel baseline, suggesting that end-to-end predictive latents change more than compute alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：JEDI：面向在线基于模型强化学习的联合嵌入扩散世界模型
扩散世界模型近期在在线基于模型的强化学习中展现出竞争力，但当前方法存在矛盾：像素扩散虽有效但计算成本高，而最新的潜在扩散方法虽提升了效率却表现欠佳。后者还依赖单独训练的潜在变量，而非推动现代MBRL进步的端到端世界模型目标。特别是，JEPA风格的预测性表征学习已成为世界建模和MBRL极具前景的方向。与此同时，扩散风格的目标在多个领域获得关注，迭代细化成为处理多模态和随机目标的有效方法。综合这些趋势，我们提出联合嵌入扩散（JEDI），这是首个在线端到端潜在扩散世界模型。JEDI通过JEPA框架直接从扩散去噪损失中学习其潜在空间，利用去噪来学习和预测未来潜在变量，而非依赖重建和预训练模型。我们提供理论动机表明，传统JEPA目标会引发预测信息瓶颈，而条件扩散去噪则具有紧密相关的预测-压缩分解。实验上，JEDI在Atari100k上具有竞争力，并在直接可比情况下优于使用单独训练潜在变量的基线。与像素扩散基线相比，JEDI减少43%的VRAM使用，世界模型采样速度提升3倍以上，训练速度提升2.5倍。JEDI在任务级性能表现上也与像素基线显著不同，表明端到端预测性潜在变量带来的变化不仅限于计算效率。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces JEDI, a joint embedding diffusion world model for online model-based reinforcement learning, motivated by the tension between computationally expensive pixel diffusion and subpar latent diffusion approaches that rely on separately trained latents. JEDI addresses this by learning its latent space end-to-end from the diffusion denoising loss within a JEPA framework, using denoising to predict future latents without reconstruction or pretrained models, supported by a theoretical connection between JEPA objectives and conditional diffusion. Experimentally, JEDI matches or outperforms baselines on Atari100k, using 43% less VRAM, achieving over 3x faster world-model sampling, and 2.5x faster training, while exhibiting a distinct task-level performance profile from pixel diffusion baselines.
该论文提出了JEDI，一种用于在线基于模型的强化学习的联合嵌入扩散世界模型，其动机源于计算昂贵的像素扩散与性能欠佳且依赖单独训练潜在变量的潜在扩散之间的张力。JEDI通过在一个JEPA框架内直接从扩散去噪损失中端到端学习潜在空间来解决这一问题，利用去噪来预测未来潜在变量，无需重建或预训练模型，并提供了JEPA目标与条件扩散之间的理论联系。实验上，JEDI在Atari100k上达到或超越基线，使用43%更少的显存，实现超过3倍更快的世界模型采样和2.5倍更快的训练，同时展现出与像素扩散基线截然不同的任务级性能特征。
Asymmetric On-Policy Distillation: Bridging Exploitation and Imitation at the Token Level
Authors: Nan Jia, Haojin Yang, Xing Ma, Jiesong Lian, Shuailiang Zhang, Weipeng Zhang, Ke Zeng, Xunliang Cai, Zequn Sun
First: 2026-05-07T15:02:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T04:44:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student on its own trajectories with token-level teacher feedback and often outperforms off-policy distillation and standard reinforcement learning. However, we find that its standard advantage weighted policy gradient suffers from three structural weaknesses, including high variance updates, vanishing gradients in zero-advantage regions, and exploration bottlenecks when corrective signals are insufficient. We therefore propose Asymmetric On-Policy Distillation (AOPD), which replaces ineffective negative reinforcement with localized divergence minimization in non-positive advantage regions while preserving positive reinforcement learning. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that AOPD consistently outperforms standard OPD, with average gains of 4.09 / 8.34 under strong / weak initialization, respectively. AOPD also maintains higher policy entropy during training and better capability retention during sequential tool-use adaptation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非对称同策略蒸馏：在词元层面桥接利用与模仿
同策略蒸馏（OPD）利用词元级别的教师反馈，在学生自身轨迹上训练模型，通常优于异策略蒸馏和标准强化学习。然而，我们发现其标准的优势加权策略梯度存在三个结构性缺陷，包括高方差更新、零优势区域的梯度消失以及纠正信号不足时的探索瓶颈。为此，我们提出非对称同策略蒸馏（AOPD），该方法在非正优势区域用局部散度最小化替代无效的负强化，同时保留正强化学习。数学推理基准实验表明，AOPD在强/弱初始化下分别平均提升4.09/8.34个点，持续优于标准OPD。此外，AOPD在训练过程中保持更高的策略熵，并在顺序工具使用适应中展现出更好的能力保持性。
Summary / 总结
On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student model using its own trajectories with token-level teacher feedback, but its standard advantage-weighted policy gradient suffers from high variance, vanishing gradients in zero-advantage regions, and exploration bottlenecks. To address these issues, the authors propose Asymmetric On-Policy Distillation (AOPD), which replaces ineffective negative reinforcement with localized divergence minimization in non-positive advantage regions while preserving positive reinforcement learning. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that AOPD consistently outperforms standard OPD, achieving average gains of 4.09 under strong initialization and 8.34 under weak initialization, while also maintaining higher policy entropy and better capability retention during sequential tool-use adaptation.
在线策略蒸馏（OPD）利用学生模型自身轨迹和逐词元的教师反馈进行训练，但其标准优势加权策略梯度存在高方差、零优势区域梯度消失以及探索瓶颈等结构性问题。为此，作者提出非对称在线策略蒸馏（AOPD），该方法在非正优势区域用局部散度最小化替代无效的负强化，同时保留正强化学习。在数学推理基准上的实验表明，AOPD 持续优于标准 OPD，在强初始化和弱初始化下分别平均提升 4.09 和 8.34，同时在训练中保持更高的策略熵，并在顺序工具使用适应中展现出更好的能力保持性。
Differentiable Evolutionary Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Sitao Cheng, Tianle Li, Xuhan Huang, Xunjian Yin, Difan Zou
First: 2025-12-15T14:50:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T04:43:51+00:00
Comments: Work in Progress. We release our code and model at https://github.com/sitaocheng/DERL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Crafting effective reward signals remains a central challenge in Reinforcement Learning (RL), especially for complex reasoning tasks. Existing automated reward optimization methods typically rely on derivative-free search heuristics that treat the reward function as a black box, failing to exploit the causal dynamics between reward structure modifications and policy performance. We introduce Differentiable Evolutionary Reinforcement Learning (DERL), a bi-level framework for the autonomous discovery of optimal reward structures. DERL employs a Meta-Optimizer that evolves a reward function through the composition of structured atomic primitives to guide an inner-loop policy. Unlike prior black-box methods, DERL introduces differentiability into the meta-optimization process by updating the Meta-Optimizer using policy gradients derived from inner-loop validation performance. This allows for the progressive learning of a "meta-gradient" for task success, providing the system with dense, actionable feedback. We validate DERL across diverse reasoning domains: embodied agent (ALFWorld), scientific simulation (ScienceWorld), and mathematical reasoning (GSM8K, MATH). Results show that DERL achieves state-of-the-art performance on agent benchmarks, substantially outperforming non-differentiable baselines-especially in out-of-distribution generalization. Trajectory analyses confirm that DERL captures the intrinsic causal structure of tasks, enabling fully autonomous, self-improving agent alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：可微进化强化学习
设计有效的奖励信号仍是强化学习（RL）的核心挑战，尤其在复杂推理任务中。现有自动化奖励优化方法通常依赖无导数搜索启发式算法，将奖励函数视为黑箱，未能利用奖励结构修改与策略性能之间的因果动态。我们提出可微进化强化学习（DERL），一种用于自主发现最优奖励结构的双层框架。DERL采用元优化器，通过结构化原子原语的组合进化奖励函数，以指导内循环策略。与以往黑箱方法不同，DERL通过使用内循环验证性能导出的策略梯度更新元优化器，将可微性引入元优化过程。这使得系统能够逐步学习任务成功的“元梯度”，提供密集且可操作的反馈。我们在多个推理领域验证了DERL：具身智能体（ALFWorld）、科学模拟（ScienceWorld）和数学推理（GSM8K、MATH）。结果表明，DERL在智能体基准测试中达到最先进性能，显著优于不可微基线方法——尤其在分布外泛化方面。轨迹分析证实，DERL捕捉了任务的内在因果结构，实现了完全自主、自我改进的智能体对齐。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Differentiable Evolutionary Reinforcement Learning (DERL), a bi-level framework designed to address the challenge of automated reward optimization in reinforcement learning, particularly for complex reasoning tasks. Unlike prior derivative-free methods that treat reward functions as black boxes, DERL makes the meta-optimization process differentiable by updating a Meta-Optimizer using policy gradients derived from inner-loop validation performance, enabling the progressive learning of a meta-gradient for task success. Experimental validation across diverse domains including embodied agent tasks (ALFWorld), scientific simulations (ScienceWorld), and mathematical reasoning (GSM8K, MATH) demonstrates that DERL achieves state-of-the-art performance, significantly outperforming non-differentiable baselines, especially in out-of-distribution generalization, and trajectory analyses confirm its ability to capture intrinsic causal task structures for autonomous agent alignment.
该论文提出了可微分进化强化学习（DERL），这是一个双层框架，旨在解决强化学习中奖励自动优化的挑战，特别是针对复杂推理任务。与先前将奖励函数视为黑箱的无导数方法不同，DERL通过使用内循环验证性能导出的策略梯度来更新元优化器，使元优化过程变得可微分，从而逐步学习任务成功的元梯度。在包括具身智能体任务（ALFWorld）、科学模拟（ScienceWorld）和数学推理（GSM8K、MATH）等多个推理领域的实验验证表明，DERL达到了最先进的性能，显著优于不可微分的基线方法，尤其在分布外泛化方面表现突出，轨迹分析也证实了其能够捕捉任务的内在因果结构，实现完全自主的智能体对齐。
Consolidation-Expansion Operator Mechanics:A Unified Framework for Adaptive Learning
Authors: Debashis Guha
First: 2026-05-11T04:19:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T04:13:03+00:00
Comments: 38 pages; Corrected author affiliation on title page in v2; no scientific changes
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Every adaptive learning system must alternate between two operations: consolidating what it already knows and expanding into new evidence. We propose \emph{Consolidation-Expansion Operator Mechanics} (OpMech), a framework that makes this structure precise. The central object is the \emph{order-gap} $\Ogap(θ; e)$, the degree to which a consolidation operator~$Q$ and an expansion operator~$P_e$ fail to commute at a given knowledge state. Because the order-gap is computable from the system's own trajectory, it serves as a real-time control signal: large values indicate that the system is still sensitive to the ordering of consolidation and expansion; once the order-gap falls and stays small, further processing is unlikely to change the outcome. Three results give the signal precise meaning: the order-gap decays along convergent trajectories; a persistently large order-gap implies the system is far from its settled state; and an order-gap-based stopping rule terminates with provable guarantees in both noiseless and bounded-noise settings. The framework applies across five domains: bandits, reinforcement learning, stochastic optimization, continual learning, and recursive language models. We give conditions under which the order-gap reliably tracks convergence in three representative cases. We develop the recursive language model application in detail, showing how OpMech replaces heuristic stopping rules and fixed recursion budgets with principled, evidence-driven alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巩固-扩展算子机制：自适应学习的统一框架
每个自适应学习系统必须在两种操作之间交替：巩固已有知识并扩展至新证据。我们提出“巩固-扩展算子机制”（OpMech），该框架精确刻画了这一结构。核心对象是“序间隙”$\Ogap(θ; e)$，即巩固算子$Q$与扩展算子$P_e$在给定知识状态下未能交换的程度。由于序间隙可从系统自身轨迹计算得出，它可作为实时控制信号：大值表明系统对巩固与扩展的顺序仍敏感；一旦序间隙下降并保持较小，进一步处理不太可能改变结果。三个结果赋予该信号精确含义：序间隙沿收敛轨迹衰减；持续大的序间隙意味着系统远离稳定状态；基于序间隙的停止规则在无噪声和有界噪声设置下均具有可证明的保证。该框架适用于五个领域：赌博机、强化学习、随机优化、持续学习和递归语言模型。我们给出了序间隙在三个代表性案例中可靠跟踪收敛的条件。我们详细开发了递归语言模型应用，展示了OpMech如何用基于原则、证据驱动的替代方案取代启发式停止规则和固定递归预算。
Exploring the holographic entropy cone via reinforcement learning
Authors: Temple He, Jaeha Lee, Hirosi Ooguri
First: 2026-01-27T19:00:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T04:09:47+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 10 figures, 2 tables; v2: minor clarifications, version appearing in JHEP
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop a reinforcement learning algorithm to study the holographic entropy cone. Given a target entropy vector, our algorithm searches for a graph realization whose min-cut entropies match the target vector. If the target vector does not admit such a graph realization, it must lie outside the cone, in which case the algorithm finds a graph whose corresponding entropy vector most nearly approximates the target and allows us to probe the location of the facets. For the $\sf N=3$ cone, we confirm that our algorithm successfully rediscovers monogamy of mutual information beginning with a target vector outside the holographic entropy cone. We then apply the algorithm to the $\sf N=6$ cone, analyzing the 6 "mystery" extreme rays of the subadditivity cone from arXiv:2412.15364 that satisfy all known holographic entropy inequalities yet lacked graph realizations. We found realizations for 3 of them, proving they are genuine extreme rays of the holographic entropy cone, while providing evidence that the remaining 3 are not realizable, implying unknown holographic inequalities exist for $\sf N=6$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过强化学习探索全息熵锥
我们开发了一种强化学习算法来研究全息熵锥。给定一个目标熵向量，我们的算法搜索一个图实现，其最小割熵与目标向量匹配。如果目标向量不允许这样的图实现，则它必须位于锥外，此时算法会找到一个图，其对应的熵向量最接近目标，并允许我们探测锥面的位置。对于$\sf N=3$锥，我们确认算法成功地从全息熵锥外的目标向量重新发现了互信息的单配性。然后我们将算法应用于$\sf N=6$锥，分析了arXiv:2412.15364中子可加性锥的6条“神秘”极射线，这些射线满足所有已知的全息熵不等式但缺乏图实现。我们为其中3条找到了实现，证明它们是全息熵锥的真正极射线，同时提供证据表明其余3条不可实现，这意味着$\sf N=6$存在未知的全息不等式。
Summary / 总结
This paper develops a reinforcement learning algorithm to explore the holographic entropy cone, motivated by the need to determine whether a given entropy vector can be realized by a graph model whose min-cut entropies match the target. The method trains an agent to iteratively construct and adjust graph realizations, and if no exact realization exists, the algorithm finds the closest approximation to probe the cone's facets. For the N=3 cone, the algorithm successfully rediscovers monogamy of mutual information from a target vector outside the cone, and for N=6, it finds realizations for 3 of the 6 mystery extreme rays from arXiv:2412.15364, proving they are genuine, while providing evidence that the remaining 3 are not realizable, indicating unknown holographic inequalities exist for N=6.
本文开发了一种强化学习算法来探索全息熵锥，其动机是判断给定熵向量是否能通过图模型实现，使得最小割熵与目标匹配。该方法训练智能体迭代构建和调整图实现，若无法精确实现，则算法找到最接近的近似以探测锥的各个面。对于N=3锥，算法从锥外目标向量成功重新发现了互信息的单配性；对于N=6锥，算法为arXiv:2412.15364中6个神秘极射线中的3个找到了图实现，证明它们是真正的极射线，同时提供证据表明其余3个不可实现，暗示N=6存在未知的全息不等式。
Revisiting Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards from a Contrastive Perspective
Authors: Feng Zhang, Xinhong Ma, Ziqiang Dong, Xi Leng, Jianfei Zhao, Xin Sun, Yang Yang, Guanjun Jiang
First: 2026-05-13T04:02:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T04:02:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
RLVR has become a widely adopted paradigm for improving LLMs' reasoning capabilities, and GRPO is one of its most representative algorithms. In this paper, we first show that GRPO admits an equivalent discriminative reformulation as a weighted positive-negative score difference. Under this view, GRPO increases sequence-level scores of verified positive rollouts and decreases those of negative rollouts, where the scores are averages of clipped token-level importance sampling ratios. This reformulation reveals two structural limitations of GRPO: likelihood-misaligned scoring, where clipped ratio-based surrogate scores are optimized instead of generation likelihoods, and score-insensitive credit assignment, where rollout-level credit is assigned without accounting for relative score gaps between positive and negative rollouts in the same group. To address these limitations, we propose ConSPO, a framework for Contrastive Sequence-level Policy Optimization in RLVR. ConSPO replaces GRPO's clipped ratio-based scores with length-normalized sequence log-probabilities, aligning the optimized rollout scores with the likelihoods used in autoregressive generation. It then optimizes a group-wise InfoNCE-style objective that contrasts each positive rollout against negative distractors from the same group, enabling credit assignment to depend on their relative scores. This contrastive formulation amplifies updates for poorly separated positives while concentrating suppressive updates on high-scoring negatives. Moreover, ConSPO introduces a curriculum-scheduled margin, guiding optimization from coarse positive-negative ordering in early training toward stronger separation in later stages. Extensive evaluations across diverse backbone models, parameter scales, and training datasets show that ConSPO consistently outperforms several strong RLVR baselines on challenging mathematical reasoning benchmarks.
Summary / 总结
The paper revisits Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for improving large language models' reasoning, focusing on the GRPO algorithm. The authors first show that GRPO is equivalent to a discriminative reformulation as a weighted positive-negative score difference, which reveals two limitations: likelihood-misaligned scoring and score-insensitive credit assignment. To address these, they propose ConSPO, a contrastive sequence-level policy optimization framework that replaces GRPO's clipped ratio-based scores with length-normalized sequence log-probabilities and uses an InfoNCE-style objective with curriculum-scheduled margins. Extensive experiments across various backbone models and datasets demonstrate that ConSPO consistently outperforms strong RLVR baselines on challenging mathematical reasoning benchmarks.
该论文重新审视了用于提升大语言模型推理能力的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）范式，重点关注GRPO算法。作者首先证明GRPO等价于一个加权正负分数差异的判别式重构，这揭示了两个结构缺陷：似然不匹配的评分和分数不敏感的信用分配。为解决这些问题，他们提出了ConSPO，一种对比性序列级策略优化框架，用长度归一化的序列对数概率替代GRPO的裁剪比率评分，并采用带有课程调度边界的InfoNCE风格目标函数。在多种骨干模型、参数规模和训练数据集上的广泛实验表明，ConSPO在具有挑战性的数学推理基准测试中持续优于多个强RLVR基线方法。
Reinforced Collaboration in Multi-Agent Flow Networks
Authors: Zheng Wang, Yuang Liu, Yangkai Ding
First: 2026-05-13T03:26:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T03:26:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-agent systems provide a powerful way to extend large language models (LLMs) by decomposing a complex task into specialized subtasks handled by different agents. However, their performance is often hindered by error propagation, arising from suboptimal workflow design or inaccurate agent outputs, which can propagate through the agent collaboration process and degrade final results. To address the challenges, we present MANGO (Multi-Agent Network Gradient Optimization), a data-driven framework that organizes and refines agent collaboration via a flow network constructed from past successful workflows. MANGO integrates reinforcement learning and textual gradients to jointly optimize workflow paths and agent behaviors, while a skipping mechanism prevents redundant updates to well-optimized agents for improving efficiency. Extensive experiments on seven benchmarks show that MANGO achieves up to 12.8% performance improvement over state-of-the-art baselines, enhances efficiency by 47.4%, and generalizes effectively to unseen domains. Our code and datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/openJiuwen-ai/agent-store/tree/main/community/mango.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses error propagation in multi-agent LLM systems caused by suboptimal workflows and inaccurate agent outputs. It proposes MANGO, a data-driven framework that constructs a flow network from past successful workflows and uses reinforcement learning with textual gradients to jointly optimize workflow paths and agent behaviors, incorporating a skipping mechanism to avoid redundant updates. Experiments on seven benchmarks show MANGO achieves up to 12.8% performance improvement over state-of-the-art baselines, enhances efficiency by 47.4%, and generalizes effectively to unseen domains.
该论文针对多智能体大语言模型系统中因工作流设计不佳或智能体输出不准确导致的错误传播问题，提出了MANGO框架。该框架基于历史成功工作流构建流网络，通过强化学习和文本梯度联合优化工作流路径与智能体行为，并引入跳过机制避免对已优化智能体的冗余更新。在七个基准上的实验表明，MANGO相比现有最优方法性能提升最高达12.8%，效率提高47.4%，并能有效泛化到未见领域。
Revisiting DAgger in the Era of LLM-Agents
Authors: Changhao Li, Rushi Qiang, Jiawei Huang, Chenxiao Gao, Chao Zhang, Niao He, Bo Dai
First: 2026-05-13T02:40:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T02:40:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-horizon LM agents learn from multi-turn interaction, where a single early mistake can alter the subsequent state distribution and derail the whole trajectory. Existing recipes fall short in complementary ways: supervised fine-tuning provides dense teacher supervision but suffers from covariate shift because it is trained on off-policy teacher trajectories; while reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards avoids this off-policy mismatch by learning from on-policy rollouts but with only sparse outcome feedback. We address this dilemma by revisiting Dataset Aggregation (DAgger) for multi-turn LM agents: the algorithm collects trajectories through a turn-level interpolation of student and teacher policies, and the student is then trained on these trajectories using supervised labels provided by the teacher. By directly interacting with environments, we expose the model to realistic states likely to be encountered during deployment, thereby effectively mitigating covariate shift. Besides, since the student is learned by mimicking the teacher's behavior, it receives rich feedback during learning. To demonstrate DAgger enjoys the benefits of both worlds, we tested the algorithm to train a software-engineering agent with 4B- and 8B-scale student models. On SWE-bench Verified, our DAgger-style training improves over the strongest post-training baseline by +3.9 points at 4B and +3.6 points at 8B. The resulting 4B agent reaches 27.3%, outperforming representative published 8B SWE-agent systems, while the 8B agent achieves 29.8%, surpassing SWE-Gym-32B and coming within 5 points of stronger 32B-scale agents. Together with consistent gains on the held-out SWE-Gym split, these results suggest the effectiveness of DAgger for modern long-horizon LM agents.
Summary / 总结
The paper revisits Dataset Aggregation (DAgger) to address the covariate shift problem in long-horizon language model agents, where supervised fine-tuning suffers from off-policy mismatch and reinforcement learning provides only sparse feedback. The method collects trajectories via turn-level interpolation of student and teacher policies, then trains the student on these trajectories with teacher-provided supervised labels, exposing the model to realistic deployment states and providing rich feedback. On SWE-bench Verified, DAgger-style training improves over the strongest post-training baseline by +3.9 points for a 4B model and +3.6 points for an 8B model, with the 4B agent reaching 27.3% and the 8B agent achieving 29.8%, outperforming several larger-scale systems.
该论文重新审视了数据集聚合（DAgger）方法，以解决长周期语言模型智能体中的协变量偏移问题，其中监督微调因离策略不匹配而受限，而强化学习仅提供稀疏反馈。该方法通过学生和教师策略的回合级插值收集轨迹，然后使用教师提供的监督标签在这些轨迹上训练学生，使模型暴露于部署中可能遇到的真实状态，并提供丰富的反馈。在SWE-bench Verified上，DAgger风格训练使4B模型比最强后训练基线提升3.9个百分点，8B模型提升3.6个百分点，其中4B智能体达到27.3%，8B智能体达到29.8%，超越了多个更大规模的系统。
Table-R1: Region-based Reinforcement Learning for Table Understanding
Authors: Zhenhe Wu, Jian Yang, Zhongjiang He, Changzai Pan, Jie Zhang, Jiaheng Liu, Xianjie Wu, Yu Zhao, Shuangyong Song, Yongxiang Li, Zhoujun Li, Xueling Li
First: 2025-05-18T13:40:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T02:38:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tables present unique challenges for language models due to their structured row-column interactions, necessitating specialized approaches for effective comprehension. While large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated potential in table reasoning through prompting and techniques like chain-of-thought (CoT) and program-of-thought (PoT), optimizing their performance for table question answering remains underexplored. In this paper, we introduce region-based Table-R1, a novel reinforcement learning approach that enhances LLM table understanding by integrating region evidence into reasoning steps. Our method employs Region-Enhanced Supervised Fine-Tuning (RE-SFT) to guide models in identifying relevant table regions before generating answers, incorporating textual, symbolic, and program-based reasoning. Additionally, Table-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization (TARPO) introduces a mixed reward system to dynamically balance region accuracy and answer correctness, with decaying region rewards and consistency penalties to align reasoning steps. Experiments show that Table-R1 achieves an average performance improvement of 14.36 points across multiple base models on three benchmark datasets, even outperforming baseline models with ten times the parameters, while TARPO reduces response token consumption by 67.5% compared to GRPO, significantly advancing LLM capabilities in efficient tabular reasoning.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Table-R1, a reinforcement learning approach designed to improve language models' understanding of tables by incorporating region-based evidence into reasoning steps. The method consists of two key components: Region-Enhanced Supervised Fine-Tuning (RE-SFT), which trains models to identify relevant table regions before generating answers using textual, symbolic, and program-based reasoning, and Table-Aware Group Relative Policy Optimization (TARPO), which employs a mixed reward system to balance region accuracy and answer correctness with decaying rewards and consistency penalties. Experimental results demonstrate that Table-R1 achieves an average performance improvement of 14.36 points across multiple base models on three benchmark datasets, outperforming baseline models with ten times the parameters, while TARPO reduces response token consumption by 67.5% compared to GRPO, significantly advancing efficient tabular reasoning.
本文提出了Table-R1，一种基于强化学习的方法，通过将区域证据整合到推理步骤中来提升语言模型对表格的理解能力。该方法包含两个关键组件：区域增强监督微调（RE-SFT），指导模型在生成答案前识别相关表格区域，并融合文本、符号和基于程序的推理；以及表格感知组相对策略优化（TARPO），采用混合奖励系统动态平衡区域准确性和答案正确性，并引入衰减区域奖励和一致性惩罚来对齐推理步骤。实验结果表明，Table-R1在三个基准数据集上平均性能提升14.36分，超越了参数规模大十倍的基线模型，同时TARPO相比GRPO减少了67.5%的响应令牌消耗，显著推进了高效表格推理能力。
THINKSAFE: Self-Generated Safety Alignment for Reasoning Models
Authors: Seanie Lee, Sangwoo Park, Yumin Choi, Gyeongman Kim, Minki Kang, Jihun Yun, Dongmin Park, Jongho Park, Sung Ju Hwang
First: 2026-01-30T16:31:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T02:16:49+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 13 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large reasoning models (LRMs) achieve remarkable performance by leveraging reinforcement learning (RL) on reasoning tasks to generate long chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning. However, this over-optimization often prioritizes compliance, making models vulnerable to harmful prompts. To mitigate this safety degradation, recent approaches rely on external teacher distillation, yet this introduces a distributional discrepancy that degrades native reasoning. We formalize safety realignment as a KL projection onto the safe simplex and prove that the student's own safety-filtered distribution is the unique KL-optimal target, while any external teacher incurs an irreducible excess KL penalty. Guided by this analysis, we propose ThinkSafe, a self-generated alignment framework that restores safety without external teachers. Our key insight is that while compliance suppresses safety mechanisms, models often retain latent knowledge to identify harm. ThinkSafe unlocks this via lightweight refusal steering, which preserves the KL-optimal target while increasing the acceptance rate. Experiments on DeepSeek-R1-Distill and Qwen3 show ThinkSafe significantly improves safety while preserving reasoning proficiency, and achieves superior safety and comparable reasoning to GRPO with roughly an order of magnitude less compute. Code, models, and datasets are available at https://github.com/seanie12/ThinkSafe and https://huggingface.co/Seanie-lee/collections.
中文标题/摘要
标题：THINKSAFE：推理模型的自我生成安全对齐
大型推理模型（LRM）通过在推理任务上应用强化学习（RL）生成长链式思维（CoT）推理，取得了显著性能。然而，这种过度优化往往优先考虑合规性，使模型易受有害提示的影响。为缓解这种安全退化，近期方法依赖外部教师蒸馏，但这引入了分布差异，损害了原生推理能力。我们将安全重对齐形式化为KL投影到安全单纯形上，并证明学生自身的安全过滤分布是唯一的KL最优目标，而任何外部教师都会引入不可约的额外KL惩罚。基于此分析，我们提出ThinkSafe，一种无需外部教师的自我生成对齐框架。我们的关键见解是：尽管合规性抑制了安全机制，模型通常仍保留识别危害的潜在知识。ThinkSafe通过轻量级拒绝引导解锁这一能力，在保持KL最优目标的同时提高接受率。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill和Qwen3上的实验表明，ThinkSafe显著提升了安全性，同时保持了推理能力，并以约一个数量级的计算量实现了优于GRPO的安全性和可比的推理性能。代码、模型和数据集见https://github.com/seanie12/ThinkSafe和https://huggingface.co/Seanie-lee/collections。

大型推理模型在通过强化学习优化推理任务时，常因过度追求合规性而导致安全性下降。针对这一问题，作者将安全重对齐形式化为对安全单纯形的KL投影，证明模型自身的安全过滤分布是唯一的最优目标，而外部教师蒸馏会引入不可约的额外KL惩罚。他们提出ThinkSafe框架，通过轻量级拒绝引导来解锁模型潜在的危害识别知识，无需外部教师即可恢复安全性。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill和Qwen3上的实验表明，ThinkSafe在显著提升安全性的同时保持了推理能力，并以约一个数量级的计算量实现了优于GRPO的安全性和相当的推理性能。
On the Sample Complexity of Differentially Private Policy Optimization
Authors: Yi He, Xingyu Zhou
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2025-10-24T00:21:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T01:55:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted at NeurIPS 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy optimization (PO) is a cornerstone of modern reinforcement learning (RL), with diverse applications spanning robotics, healthcare, and large language model training. The increasing deployment of PO in sensitive domains, however, raises significant privacy concerns. In this paper, we initiate a theoretical study of differentially private policy optimization, focusing explicitly on its sample complexity. We first formalize an appropriate definition of differential privacy (DP) tailored to PO, addressing the inherent challenges arising from on-policy learning dynamics and the subtlety involved in defining the unit of privacy. We then systematically analyze the sample complexity of widely-used PO algorithms, including policy gradient (PG), natural policy gradient (NPG) and more, under DP constraints and various settings, via a unified framework. Our theoretical results demonstrate that privacy costs can often manifest as lower-order terms in the sample complexity, while also highlighting subtle yet important observations in private PO settings. These offer valuable practical insights for privacy-preserving PO algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：差分隐私策略优化的样本复杂度研究
策略优化是现代强化学习的基石，广泛应用于机器人技术、医疗保健及大型语言模型训练等领域。然而，其在敏感领域的部署日益增多，引发了显著的隐私问题。本文首次对差分隐私策略优化展开理论研究，重点聚焦其样本复杂度。我们首先针对策略优化定制了合适的差分隐私定义，解决了在线学习动态带来的固有挑战以及隐私单元定义中的微妙问题。随后，通过统一框架系统分析了在差分隐私约束及多种设置下，包括策略梯度、自然策略梯度等广泛使用的策略优化算法的样本复杂度。理论结果表明，隐私成本通常表现为样本复杂度中的低阶项，同时揭示了隐私策略优化中微妙但重要的观察结果，为隐私保护策略优化算法提供了宝贵的实践见解。

CoFlow: Coordinated Few-Step Flow for Offline Multi-Agent Decision Making
Authors: Guowei Zou, Haitao Wang, Beiwen Zhang, Boning Zhang, Hejun Wu
First: 2026-05-02T14:12:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T01:42:20+00:00
Comments: 34 pages, 15 figures, 10 tables. Project page: https://guowei-zou.github.io/coflow/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Generative models have emerged as a promising paradigm for offline multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), but existing approaches require many iterative sampling steps. Recent few-step acceleration methods either distill a joint teacher into independent students or apply averaged velocity fields independently to each agent. Unfortunately, these few-step approaches hurt inter-agent coordination. We show that the efficiency-coordination trade-off is not inherent: single-pass multi-agent generation can preserve coordination when the velocity field is natively joint-coupled. We propose Coordinated few-step Flow (CoFlow), an architecture that combines Coordinated Velocity Attention (CVA) with Adaptive Coordination Gating. A finite-difference consistency surrogate further replaces memory-prohibitive Jacobian-vector product backpropagation through the averaged velocity field with two stop-gradient forward passes. Across 60 configurations spanning MPE, MA-MuJoCo, and SMAC, CoFlow matches or surpasses Gaussian policies, value-based methods, transformer policies, diffusion models, and prior flow baselines on episodic return. Three independent coordination probes confirm that CoFlow's improvements arise from inter-agent coordination rather than per-agent capacity. A denoising-step sweep shows that single-pass inference suffices on every configuration. CoFlow reaches state-of-the-art coordination quality in 1-3 denoising steps under both centralized and decentralized execution. Project Page: https://guowei-zou.github.io/coflow/
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoFlow：面向离线多智能体决策的协调少步流
生成模型已成为离线多智能体强化学习（MARL）的一种有前景范式，但现有方法需要大量迭代采样步骤。近期少步加速方法要么将联合教师模型蒸馏为独立学生模型，要么对每个智能体独立应用平均速度场。然而，这些少步方法损害了智能体间的协调性。我们证明效率-协调权衡并非固有：当速度场是原生联合耦合时，单步多智能体生成可以保持协调性。我们提出协调少步流（CoFlow），一种结合协调速度注意力（CVA）与自适应协调门控的架构。有限差分一致性代理进一步用两次停止梯度前向传播替代了通过平均速度场的、内存禁止的雅可比向量积反向传播。在涵盖MPE、MA-MuJoCo和SMAC的60种配置中，CoFlow在回合回报上匹配或超越了高斯策略、基于值的方法、Transformer策略、扩散模型及先前流基线。三项独立协调探测证实CoFlow的提升源于智能体间协调而非单智能体能力。去噪步数扫描表明单步推理在所有配置上均足够。在集中式和分散式执行下，CoFlow在1-3步去噪中达到了最先进的协调质量。 项目页面：https://guowei-zou.github.io/coflow/

The paper addresses the efficiency-coordination trade-off in offline multi-agent reinforcement learning, where existing few-step generative models sacrifice inter-agent coordination for speed. The authors propose CoFlow, a method that combines Coordinated Velocity Attention (CVA) with Adaptive Coordination Gating to maintain joint-coupled velocity fields, and uses a finite-difference consistency surrogate to avoid memory-heavy Jacobian-vector products. Across 60 configurations in MPE, MA-MuJoCo, and SMAC, CoFlow matches or surpasses baselines including Gaussian policies, value-based methods, and diffusion models in episodic return, with three coordination probes confirming improvements stem from inter-agent coordination, and single-pass inference sufficing in all settings to achieve state-of-the-art coordination in 1-3 denoising steps under both centralized and decentralized execution.
该论文针对离线多智能体强化学习中的效率-协调权衡问题，指出现有少步生成模型在加速时会损害智能体间的协调性。作者提出CoFlow方法，通过结合协调速度注意力（CVA）和自适应协调门控来保持联合耦合的速度场，并利用有限差分一致性替代方法避免内存密集的雅可比向量积反向传播。在MPE、MA-MuJoCo和SMAC的60种配置中，CoFlow在回合回报上匹配或超越了高斯策略、基于价值的方法、扩散模型等基线，三项独立协调探测证实其改进源于智能体间协调而非个体能力，且单步推理在所有设置中均足够，在1-3步去噪下达到集中式和分散式执行中的最优协调质量。
ChipMATE: Multi-Agent Training via Reinforcement Learning for Enhanced RTL Generation
Authors: Zhongkai Yu, Yichen Lin, Chenyang Zhou, Yuwei Zhang, Kun Zhou, Junxia Cui, Haotian Ye, Zhengding Hu, Zaifeng Pan, Ruiyi Wang, Yujie Zhao, Hejia Zhang, Jingbo Shang, Jishen Zhao, Yufei Ding
First: 2026-05-13T01:04:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T01:04:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing API-based agentic systems for RTL code generation are fundamentally misaligned with industrial practice: they assume a golden testbench is available at generation time, rely on closed-source APIs incompatible with chip vendors' air-gapped security requirements, and cannot be trained on vendors' proprietary RTL codebases, leaving valuable internal data unused. Recent self-trained models address the deployment constraint but remain single-turn generators that overlook the critical role of verification in real industrial flows. To bridge these gaps, we present ChipMATE, the first self-trained multi-agent framework for RTL generation. Inspired by industrial practice where correctness emerges from cross-comparison between independently written RTL modules and reference models, ChipMATE pairs a Verilog agent with a Python reference-model agent that mutually verify each other's outputs without any golden oracle. We design a backtrack-based inference workflow to prevent error propagation across turns, and a two-stage training pipeline that first trains each agent individually to saturate its code-generation capability, then trains the team jointly to collaborate effectively. To support the training, we further build a hybrid data-generation framework that produces 64.4K high-quality reference model training samples. ChipMATE achieves 75.0\% and 80.1\% pass@1 on VerilogEval V2 with 4B and 9B base models, outperforming all existing self-trained models and even DeepSeek V4 with 1600B parameters. Our code and model weights are publicly available in https://github.com/zhongkaiyu/ChipMATE.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ChipMATE：基于强化学习的多智能体训练以增强RTL生成
现有的基于API的RTL代码生成智能体系统与工业实践根本不一致：它们假设在生成时存在黄金测试平台，依赖与芯片供应商气隙安全要求不兼容的闭源API，并且无法在供应商的专有RTL代码库上进行训练，导致宝贵的内部数据未被利用。最近的自训练模型解决了部署约束，但仍然是单轮生成器，忽略了验证在真实工业流程中的关键作用。为弥合这些差距，我们提出了ChipMATE，这是首个用于RTL生成的自训练多智能体框架。受工业实践中正确性源于独立编写的RTL模块与参考模型之间交叉比较的启发，ChipMATE将Verilog智能体与Python参考模型智能体配对，两者在没有黄金标准的情况下相互验证彼此的输出。我们设计了一种基于回溯的推理工作流以防止跨轮错误传播，以及一个两阶段训练流程：首先单独训练每个智能体以饱和其代码生成能力，然后联合训练团队以有效协作。为支持训练，我们进一步构建了一个混合数据生成框架，产生了64.4K个高质量参考模型训练样本。ChipMATE在VerilogEval V2上使用4B和9B基础模型分别实现了75.0%和80.1%的pass@1，优于所有现有的自训练模型，甚至优于具有1600B参数的DeepSeek V4。我们的代码和模型权重已在https://github.com/zhongkaiyu/ChipMATE公开。

The proposed method is a self-trained multi-agent framework pairing a Verilog agent with a Python reference-model agent that mutually verify each other's outputs without a golden oracle, using a backtrack-based inference workflow and a two-stage training pipeline. ChipMATE achieves 75.0% and 80.1% pass@1 on VerilogEval V2 with 4B and 9B base models, outperforming all existing self-trained models and even DeepSeek V4 with 1600B parameters.
ChipMATE解决了现有基于API的RTL代码生成智能体系统与工业实践不匹配的问题，这些系统假设存在黄金测试平台、依赖封闭API且无法利用专有代码库。该方法提出首个自训练多智能体框架，将Verilog智能体与Python参考模型智能体配对，无需黄金标准即可相互验证输出，并采用基于回溯的推理流程和两阶段训练流程。ChipMATE在VerilogEval V2上使用4B和9B基础模型分别达到75.0%和80.1%的pass@1，超越了所有现有自训练模型，甚至包括拥有1600B参数的DeepSeek V4。
Bayesian Model Merging
Authors: Kaiyang Li, Shaobo Han, Qing Su, Shihao Ji
First: 2026-05-13T00:36:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T00:36:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model merging aims to combine multiple task-specific expert models into a single model without joint retraining, offering a practical alternative to multi-task learning when data access or computational budget is limited. Existing methods, however, face two key limitations: (1) they overlook the valuable inductive bias of strong anchor models and estimate the merged weights from scratch, and (2) they rely on a shared hyperparameter setting across different modules of the network, lacking a global optimization strategy. This paper introduces Bayesian Model Merging (BMM), a plug-and-play bi-level optimization framework, where the inner level formulates the model merging as an activation-based Bayesian regression under a strong prior induced by an anchor model, yielding an efficient closed-form solution; and the outer level leverages a Bayesian optimization procedure to search module-specific hyperparameters globally based on a small validation set. Furthermore, we reveal a key alignment between activation statistics and task vectors, enabling us to derive a data-free variant of BMM that estimates the Gram matrix for regression without any auxiliary data. Across extensive benchmarks, including up to 20-task merging in vision and 5-task merging in language, BMM consistently outperforms all plug-and-play anchor baselines (e.g., TA, WUDI-Merging, and TSV). In particular, on the ViT-L/14 benchmark for 8-task merging, a single merged model reaches 95.1, closely matching the average performance of eight task-specific experts (95.8).
Summary / 总结
Bayesian Model Merging (BMM) is introduced to address two limitations in existing model merging methods: the neglect of strong anchor models as inductive biases and the lack of global optimization for module-specific hyperparameters. The proposed plug-and-play bi-level optimization framework formulates the inner level as activation-based Bayesian regression with a strong prior from an anchor model, yielding a closed-form solution, while the outer level uses Bayesian optimization to search hyperparameters globally based on a small validation set. Additionally, a data-free variant is derived by aligning activation statistics with task vectors. Extensive experiments on up to 20-task merging in vision and 5-task merging in language show that BMM consistently outperforms baselines like TA, WUDI-Merging, and TSV; notably, on the ViT-L/14 benchmark for 8-task merging, the merged model achieves 95.1, closely matching the average expert performance of 95.8.
贝叶斯模型合并（BMM）旨在解决现有模型合并方法的两大局限：忽视强锚定模型作为归纳偏置，以及缺乏对网络不同模块超参数的全局优化策略。该方法提出一种即插即用的双层优化框架，内层将模型合并建模为基于激活的贝叶斯回归，并利用锚定模型提供强先验，从而得到高效的闭式解；外层则基于小验证集通过贝叶斯优化全局搜索模块特定超参数。此外，通过揭示激活统计量与任务向量之间的对齐关系，推导出无需辅助数据的无数据变体。在视觉任务多达20项合并和语言任务5项合并的广泛基准测试中，BMM持续优于TA、WUDI-Merging和TSV等即插即用基线方法；特别是在ViT-L/14的8项任务合并基准上，合并模型达到95.1，与八个任务专家平均性能95.8非常接近。
When Diffusion Breaks Constraints: Sequential Autoregressive Generation with RL and MCTS
Authors: Zirui Zhao, Boye Niu, Harold Soh, David Hsu, Wee Sun Lee
First: 2025-12-01T03:38:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T00:13:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Data-driven generative models excel in language and vision, but diffusion models often fail in constrained planning and design tasks, exhibiting severe constraint violations in engineering inverse design, molecular generation, multi-robot planning, and floorplan/scene synthesis even with projection or guidance. Such tasks combine hard-to-specify semantic goals with strict geometric or physical constraints (e.g., non-overlap, connectivity), yielding feasible solutions that lie on low-dimensional, small, and sometimes disconnected regions of the output space. This paper studies the failure mode through tangram generation from language, where seven fixed shapes must form a text-described silhouette while remaining connected and non-overlapping, and a simplified rectangle composition task with a learned bounding-box constraint. We find diffusion models struggle to satisfy constraints, consistent with difficulty generating samples near low-dimensional submanifolds. Motivated by locally feasible reparameterizations, we reformulate constrained generation as discrete autoregressive sequential generation. Reinforcement learning improves feasibility and task success, and Monte Carlo tree search quantifies the value of look-ahead when feasible regions shrink. Overall, the empirical, theoretical, and prior-work evidence points to a structural limitation of continuous density matching on this class of constrained-generation problems, and suggests sequential constraint-aware generation as a promising alternative.
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates why diffusion models fail in constrained generation tasks like engineering design and molecular generation, where strict geometric or physical constraints must be satisfied. Using tangram and rectangle composition tasks, the authors demonstrate that diffusion models struggle to generate samples near low-dimensional submanifolds, leading to severe constraint violations. To address this, they reformulate constrained generation as a discrete autoregressive sequential generation problem, employing reinforcement learning to improve feasibility and task success, and Monte Carlo tree search to quantify the value of look-ahead in shrinking feasible regions. Experimental results confirm that this sequential approach significantly outperforms diffusion models in satisfying constraints, highlighting a structural limitation of continuous density matching for such problems.
该论文探讨了扩散模型在工程逆向设计、分子生成等约束生成任务中失败的原因，这些任务需要满足严格的几何或物理约束。通过七巧板和矩形组合任务，作者发现扩散模型难以在低维子流形附近生成样本，导致严重违反约束。为此，他们将约束生成重新表述为离散自回归序列生成问题，利用强化学习提高可行性和任务成功率，并采用蒙特卡洛树搜索量化可行区域缩小时的向前看价值。实验结果表明，这种序列方法在满足约束方面显著优于扩散模型，揭示了连续密度匹配在此类问题上的结构性局限。
Flow Matching for Offline Reinforcement Learning with Discrete Actions
Authors: Fairoz Nower Khan, Nabuat Zaman Nahim, Ruiquan Huang, Haibo Yang, Peizhong Ju
First: 2026-02-05T19:13:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T00:11:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative policies based on diffusion models and flow matching have shown strong promise for offline reinforcement learning (RL), but their applicability remains largely confined to continuous action spaces. To address a broader range of offline RL settings, we extend flow matching to a general framework that supports discrete action spaces with multiple objectives. Specifically, we replace continuous flows with continuous-time Markov chains, trained using a Q-weighted flow matching objective. We then extend our design to multi-agent settings, mitigating the exponential growth of joint action spaces via a factorized conditional path. We theoretically show that, under idealized conditions, optimizing this objective recovers the optimal policy. Extensive experiments further demonstrate that our method performs robustly across diverse settings and benchmarks, including high-dimensional control, multi-agent games, and dynamically changing preferences over multiple objectives, while outperforming traditional offline RL methods in practical multi-modal decision-making scenarios. Our discrete framework can also be applied to continuous-control problems through action quantization, providing a flexible trade-off between representational complexity and performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向离散动作离线强化学习的流匹配方法
基于扩散模型和流匹配的生成式策略在离线强化学习中展现出显著潜力，但其应用仍主要局限于连续动作空间。为覆盖更广泛的离线强化学习场景，我们将流匹配扩展至支持多目标离散动作空间的通用框架。具体而言，我们采用连续时间马尔可夫链替代连续流，并通过Q加权流匹配目标进行训练。随后将设计扩展至多智能体场景，利用因子化条件路径缓解联合动作空间的指数级增长。理论证明，在理想条件下优化该目标可恢复最优策略。大量实验表明，本方法在高维控制、多智能体博弈及多目标动态偏好变化等多样化场景与基准测试中均表现稳健，并在实际多模态决策场景中优于传统离线强化学习方法。通过动作量化，该离散框架还可应用于连续控制问题，在表征复杂度与性能间提供灵活权衡。

This paper extends flow matching, a generative modeling technique previously limited to continuous actions, to offline reinforcement learning with discrete action spaces. The authors replace continuous flows with continuous-time Markov chains and train them using a Q-weighted flow matching objective, further extending the framework to multi-agent settings via a factorized conditional path to handle exponential joint action spaces. Theoretically, they show that optimizing this objective recovers the optimal policy under idealized conditions. Experimentally, their method performs robustly across diverse benchmarks including high-dimensional control, multi-agent games, and multi-objective preference changes, outperforming traditional offline RL methods in multi-modal decision-making, and can also be applied to continuous control via action quantization.

Quantifying Potential Observation Missingness in Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Leo Benac, Abhishek Sharma, Alihan Huyuk, Finale Doshi-Velez
First: 2026-05-12T23:56:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T23:56:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inverse reinforcement learning (IRL), which infers reward functions from demonstrations, is a valuable tool for modeling and understanding decision-making behavior. Many variants of IRL have been developed to capture complexities of human decision-making, such as subjective beliefs, imperfect planning, and dynamic goals. However, an often-overlooked issue in real-world behavioral datasets is that the recorded data may be missing observations that were available to the original decision-maker. In use-inspired settings such as healthcare, this can make expert actions appear suboptimal, even when they were near-optimal given the information available at the time. As a result, the rewards learned by standard IRL may be misleading. In this paper, we identify the minimal perturbations to the recorded observations needed for the expert's actions to appear optimal. We develop a practical algorithm for this problem and demonstrate its utility for quantifying the possible extent of missing observations in behavioral datasets through extensive experiments on synthetic navigation tasks, a cancer treatment simulator, and ICU treatment data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量化逆强化学习中潜在观测缺失问题
逆强化学习（IRL）通过从示范中推断奖励函数，是建模和理解决策行为的重要工具。为捕捉人类决策的复杂性（如主观信念、非完美规划及动态目标），研究者已开发出多种IRL变体。然而，现实行为数据集中常被忽视的问题是：记录数据可能缺失原始决策者实际可用的观测信息。在医疗等应用场景中，这会导致专家行为看似次优——即便在给定当时可用信息时这些行为接近最优。因此，标准IRL习得的奖励函数可能具有误导性。本文识别了使专家行为呈现最优性所需对记录观测的最小扰动，开发了该问题的实用算法，并通过合成导航任务、癌症治疗模拟器及ICU治疗数据的大量实验，验证了该方法在量化行为数据集中潜在观测缺失程度方面的效用。

This paper addresses the overlooked issue of missing observations in inverse reinforcement learning (IRL), where recorded behavioral data may lack information that was available to the original decision-maker, causing expert actions to appear suboptimal and learned rewards to be misleading. The authors propose a method to identify the minimal perturbations to recorded observations required for expert actions to appear optimal, and develop a practical algorithm for this purpose. Extensive experiments on synthetic navigation tasks, a cancer treatment simulator, and ICU treatment data demonstrate the algorithm's utility in quantifying the possible extent of missing observations in behavioral datasets.
本文针对逆强化学习中一个常被忽视的问题——记录的行为数据可能缺失原始决策者可用的信息，导致专家行为看似次优且学到的奖励函数具有误导性。作者提出了一种方法，通过识别对记录观测的最小扰动使专家行为显得最优，并开发了实用算法。在合成导航任务、癌症治疗模拟器和ICU治疗数据上的大量实验表明，该算法能有效量化行为数据中可能存在的观测缺失程度。
FireScope: Wildfire Risk Raster Prediction with a Chain-of-Thought Oracle
Authors: Mario Markov, Stefan Maria Ailuro, Luc Van Gool, Konrad Schindler, Danda Pani Paudel
First: 2025-11-21T11:45:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T23:27:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Predicting wildfire risk is a reasoning-intensive spatial problem that requires the integration of visual, climatic, and geographic factors to infer continuous risk maps. Existing methods lack the causal reasoning and multimodal understanding required for reliable generalization. We introduce FireScope-Bench, a large-scale dataset and benchmark that couples Sentinel-2 imagery and climate data with expert-defined risk rasters across the USA, and real wildfire events in Europe for cross-continental evaluation. Building on this dataset, we propose FireScope, a VLM-based reasoning-to-generation framework that learns from both reinforcement learning and visual supervision to predict risk rasters with complementary reasoning traces. When trained in the USA and tested in Europe, FireScope achieves substantial performance gains, while expert feedback and automated analysis confirm that its reasoning traces are faithful and semantically meaningful. Our findings demonstrate that reasoning can ground raster prediction models, improving both generalization and interpretability. To our knowledge, this is the first framework to (1) demonstrate that language-based reasoning can improve generalization in visual generation, (2) propose a high-resolution wildfire risk model that can be applied across continents, and (3) enable systematic studies of robust cross-continental generalization for multimodal fire risk models. We believe that FireScope-Bench has the potential to serve as a foundation for advancing reasoning-driven, interpretable and generalizable spatial modeling. Data and source code will be made publicly available.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces FireScope, a framework for predicting wildfire risk rasters that integrates visual, climatic, and geographic factors through reasoning-intensive spatial modeling. To address the lack of causal reasoning and multimodal understanding in existing methods, the authors first create FireScope-Bench, a large-scale dataset combining Sentinel-2 imagery, climate data, and expert-defined risk rasters across the USA, with real wildfire events in Europe for cross-continental evaluation. They then propose FireScope, a vision-language model (VLM) based reasoning-to-generation framework that learns from both reinforcement learning and visual supervision to predict risk rasters while generating complementary reasoning traces. When trained on USA data and tested in Europe, FireScope achieves substantial performance gains, and expert feedback along with automated analysis confirms that its reasoning traces are faithful and semantically meaningful. The results demonstrate that language-based reasoning can improve generalization and interpretability in raster prediction, marking the first framework to show that reasoning enhances visual generation, propose a high-resolution cross-continental wildfire risk model, and enable systematic studies of robust cross-continental generalization for multimodal fire risk models.
该论文提出了FireScope框架，用于通过推理密集型空间建模预测野火风险栅格，整合了视觉、气候和地理因素。针对现有方法缺乏因果推理和多模态理解的问题，作者首先创建了FireScope-Bench，这是一个大规模数据集，结合了美国各地的Sentinel-2影像、气候数据和专家定义的风险栅格，并包含欧洲的真实野火事件用于跨大陆评估。在此基础上，他们提出了FireScope，一种基于视觉语言模型的推理到生成框架，通过强化学习和视觉监督进行训练，在预测风险栅格的同时生成补充性推理轨迹。当在美国数据上训练并在欧洲测试时，FireScope取得了显著的性能提升，专家反馈和自动化分析证实其推理轨迹忠实且语义有意义。结果表明，基于语言的推理可以提升栅格预测的泛化能力和可解释性，这是首个证明推理能改善视觉生成的框架，提出了高分辨率的跨大陆野火风险模型，并实现了对多模态火灾风险模型稳健跨大陆泛化的系统性研究。
Entropy Aware Reward Guidance for Diffusion Language Model Alignment
Authors: Atula Tejaswi, Litu Rout, Constantine Caramanis, Sanjay Shakkottai, Sujay Sanghavi
First: 2026-02-04T19:37:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T22:42:52+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reward guidance, also known as posterior sampling, is a popular method for test-time adaptation and post-training in continuous diffusion models. In this paper, we study reward guidance for discrete diffusion language models; now, one cannot differentiate through the natural outputs of the model because they are discrete tokens. We introduce a novel mechanism called EntRGi (Entropy aware Reward Guidance) to address this issue. EntRGi dynamically interpolates between continuous token relaxations and sampled hard tokens, on a token-by-token basis, using the diffusion model's predictive entropy. We demonstrate that EntRGi maintains both reward model reliability and optimization accuracy, while existing approaches sacrifice one for the other. We empirically validate our approach on 7B-parameter diffusion language models across two settings: (1) test-time adaptation, and (2) RGRL (Reward Guided Reinforcement Learning), our recipe for post-training on reward-guided data, showing consistent improvements over state-of-the-art methods. Our code is available at https://atutej.github.io/entrgi-rgrl
中文标题/摘要
标题：熵感知奖励引导的扩散语言模型对齐
奖励引导（也称为后验采样）是连续扩散模型中测试时适应和训练后调整的流行方法。本文研究离散扩散语言模型的奖励引导；由于模型输出为离散令牌，无法直接通过其自然输出进行微分。我们提出了一种名为EntRGi（熵感知奖励引导）的新机制来解决此问题。EntRGi利用扩散模型的预测熵，在逐令牌基础上动态插值连续令牌松弛与采样的硬令牌。我们证明EntRGi能同时保持奖励模型可靠性和优化准确性，而现有方法往往牺牲其一。我们在7B参数扩散语言模型上进行了实证验证，涵盖两种设置：（1）测试时适应，以及（2）RGRL（奖励引导强化学习）——我们针对奖励引导数据的训练后调整方案，结果显示该方法持续优于现有最先进技术。代码已开源：https://atutej.github.io/entrgi-rgrl

Experiments on 7B-parameter diffusion language models show that EntRGi maintains both reward model reliability and optimization accuracy, outperforming state-of-the-art methods in test-time adaptation and a novel post-training recipe called RGRL.

Adaptive Smooth Tchebycheff Attention for Multi-Objective Policy Optimization
Authors: Alejandro Murillo-Gonzalez, Mahmoud Ali, Lantao Liu
Venue: RSS
First: 2026-05-12T21:32:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T21:32:57+00:00
Comments: To appear in the Proceedings of Robotics: Science and Systems (RSS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Multi-objective reinforcement learning in robotic domains requires balancing complex, non-convex trade-offs between conflicting objectives. While linear scalarization methods provide stability, they are theoretically incapable of recovering solutions within non-convex regions of the Pareto front. Conversely, static non-linear scalarizations (e.g., Tchebycheff) can theoretically access these regions but often suffer from severe gradient variance and optimization instability in deep RL. In this work, we propose an Adaptive Smooth Tchebycheff framework that resolves this tension by dynamically modulating the curvature of the optimization landscape. We introduce a novel conflict-driven controller that regulates the optimization smoothness based on real-time gradient interference. This allows the agent to anneal toward precise, non-convex scalarization when objectives align, while elastically reverting to stable, smooth approximations when destructive gradient conflicts emerge. We validate our approach on a challenging robotic stealth visual search task -- a proxy for monitoring of protected/fragile ecosystems -- where an agent must balance search, exposure/interference minimization and exploration speed. Extensive ablations confirm that our conflict-aware adaptation enables the robust discovery of Pareto-optimal policies in non-convex regions inaccessible to linear baselines and unstable for static non-linear methods. Website: https://alejandromllo.github.io/research/pasta/
中文标题/摘要
标题：自适应平滑切比雪夫注意力用于多目标策略优化
机器人领域的多目标强化学习需要在冲突目标之间平衡复杂的非凸权衡。线性标量化方法虽提供稳定性，但理论上无法恢复帕累托前沿非凸区域内的解。相反，静态非线性标量化（如切比雪夫方法）理论上可访问这些区域，但在深度强化学习中常遭受严重的梯度方差和优化不稳定性。本文提出自适应平滑切比雪夫框架，通过动态调节优化景观曲率来解决这一矛盾。我们引入一种新颖的冲突驱动控制器，基于实时梯度干扰调节优化平滑度。当目标一致时，智能体可退火至精确的非凸标量化；当出现破坏性梯度冲突时，则弹性恢复至稳定的平滑近似。我们在具有挑战性的机器人隐蔽视觉搜索任务（作为受保护/脆弱生态系统监测的代理任务）上验证了该方法，该任务要求智能体平衡搜索、暴露/干扰最小化与探索速度。大量消融实验证实，我们的冲突感知自适应方法能够在线性基线无法访问且静态非线性方法不稳定的非凸区域中，稳健地发现帕累托最优策略。 网站：https://alejandromllo.github.io/research/pasta/

This paper addresses the challenge of multi-objective reinforcement learning in robotics, where conflicting objectives often form non-convex Pareto fronts. Evaluated on a robotic stealth visual search task, the method outperforms linear and static non-linear baselines by robustly discovering Pareto-optimal policies in non-convex regions, as confirmed by extensive ablation studies.
该论文针对机器人领域中多目标强化学习面临的非凸帕累托前沿优化难题，提出了一种自适应平滑切比雪夫框架。该方法通过冲突驱动控制器实时监测梯度干扰，动态调整优化曲率，在目标一致时采用精确的非凸标量化，在梯度冲突时回退到稳定的平滑近似。在机器人隐蔽视觉搜索任务上的实验表明，该方法能够稳健地发现线性基线无法触及的非凸帕累托最优策略，且优于静态非线性方法，消融实验进一步验证了其有效性。
Pragmatic Curiosity: A Unified Framework for Hybrid Learning and Optimization via Active Inference
Authors: Yingke Li, Anjali Parashar, Enlu Zhou, Chuchu Fan
First: 2026-02-05T18:42:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T21:13:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many engineering and scientific workflows rely on expensive black-box evaluations, requiring sequential decisions that must both improve task performance and reduce uncertainty. Bayesian optimization (BO) and Bayesian experimental design (BED) provide powerful but largely separate treatments of goal-directed optimization and information-seeking experimentation, leaving limited guidance for hybrid settings in which learning and optimization are intrinsically coupled. We propose Pragmatic Curiosity (PraC), a unified framework for hybrid learning and optimization via active inference. PraC evaluates candidate queries by trading information gain about a task-relevant latent symbol against an expected regret-based potential over outcomes. This formulation exposes three operational design choices: which latent quantity should be clarified, how task value is encoded as regret, and how strongly information gain should be exchanged against pragmatic value. We instantiate PraC across three regimes of increasing complexity: decision-oriented plume monitoring with fixed global symbols and known downstream losses, targeted active search with induced local symbols and evolving coverage goals, and composite Bayesian optimization with hierarchical regret learning under unknown preferences. Across these regimes, PraC reduces downstream decision risk, improves coverage of critical outcome regions, and jointly learns predictive and preference structures without relying on task-specific staging rules.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Pragmatic Curiosity (PraC), a unified framework for hybrid learning and optimization that addresses the gap between Bayesian optimization and Bayesian experimental design. The method evaluates candidate queries by balancing information gain about task-relevant latent symbols against expected regret-based potential, offering three design choices: the latent quantity to clarify, the encoding of task value as regret, and the trade-off strength between information and pragmatic value. Experiments across plume monitoring, targeted active search, and composite Bayesian optimization show that PraC reduces downstream decision risk, improves coverage of critical regions, and jointly learns predictive and preference structures without task-specific rules.
该论文提出了实用好奇心（PraC），一个用于混合学习与优化的统一框架，旨在弥合贝叶斯优化与贝叶斯实验设计之间的鸿沟。该方法通过平衡关于任务相关潜在符号的信息增益与基于遗憾的预期潜力来评估候选查询，提供了三个设计选择：要澄清的潜在量、任务价值作为遗憾的编码方式，以及信息与实用价值之间的权衡强度。在羽流监测、目标主动搜索和复合贝叶斯优化等实验中的结果表明，PraC降低了下游决策风险，改善了对关键结果区域的覆盖，并在无需任务特定规则的情况下联合学习了预测和偏好结构。
Simulating Students or Sycophantic Problem Solving? On Misconception Faithfulness of LLM Simulators
Authors: Heejin Do, Shashank Sonkar, Mrinmaya Sachan
First: 2026-05-12T20:55:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T20:55:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) can fluently generate student-like responses, making them attractive as simulated students for training and evaluating AI tutors and human educators. Yet such simulators are typically evaluated by output similarity to real students, not by whether they behave like students with coherent misconceptions during interaction. We introduce a controlled framework for evaluating misconception faithfulness, whether a simulator maintains a misconception-driven belief state and updates selectively when feedback addresses the underlying misconception. Central to our framework is a misconception-contrastive feedback protocol that compares targeted feedback against two controls: misaligned feedback (targeting a different but plausible misconception) and generic feedback (only identifying answer is wrong). We propose Selective Flip Score (SFS), which quantifies how much more often a simulator flips its answer under targeted feedback than under contrastive controls. Across seven LLMs (4B-120B), multiple datasets, and prompting strategies, simulators exhibit near-zero SFS, correcting their answers at similarly high rates regardless of feedback relevance. Further analyses reveal a sycophantic failure mode: models behave less like students with misconceptions but more like problem-solvers who treat any corrective signal as a cue to abandon the simulated belief and re-solve from internal knowledge. To address this, we develop a post-training pipeline spanning supervised fine-tuning (SFT), preference optimization, and reinforcement learning (RL) with an SFS-aligned reward; SFT yields notable gains up to +0.56, and SFS-aligned RL provides more consistent improvements than preference optimization. Our results establish misconception faithfulness as a challenging yet trainable property, motivating a shift from static output matching toward interactive, belief-aware student modeling.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem that LLM-based student simulators are typically evaluated by output similarity rather than whether they maintain coherent misconceptions during interaction. The authors propose a controlled framework using a misconception-contrastive feedback protocol and a Selective Flip Score (SFS) to measure misconception faithfulness. Experiments across seven LLMs show near-zero SFS, indicating that simulators treat any corrective feedback as a cue to re-solve from internal knowledge rather than updating misconceptions. A post-training pipeline combining SFT, preference optimization, and SFS-aligned RL improves SFS by up to +0.56, demonstrating that misconception faithfulness is a trainable property.
该论文指出，基于LLM的学生模拟器通常仅通过输出相似性评估，而非考察其在交互中是否保持连贯的误解。作者提出一个受控框架，采用误解对比反馈协议和选择性翻转分数（SFS）来衡量误解忠实度。在七个LLM上的实验显示SFS接近零，表明模拟器将任何纠正性反馈视为重新求解的提示，而非更新误解。结合SFT、偏好优化和SFS对齐强化学习的后训练流程将SFS提升高达0.56，证明误解忠实度是可训练的。
CoT-Guard: Small Models for Strong Monitoring
Authors: Nirav Diwan, Han Wang, Berkcan Kapusuzoglu, Ramin Moradi, Supriyo Chakraborty, Giri Iyengar, Sambit Sahu, Huan Zhang, Gang Wang
First: 2026-05-12T20:49:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T20:49:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Monitoring the chain-of-thought (CoT) of reasoning models is a promising approach for detecting covert misbehavior (i.e., hidden objectives) in code generation tasks. While large models (GPT-5, Gemini-3-Flash) can serve as effective CoT monitors, they are expensive to deploy due to the lengthy reasoning traces and high API cost, emphasizing the need for smaller, cheaper alternatives. Nevertheless, we find that current small models (4B--8B) struggle to detect hidden objectives despite access to the CoT, frequently misattributing them as part of the user query. To address this, we propose a post-training pipeline combining supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL), where SFT narrows the gap for in-domain tasks by distilling detection behavior from stronger monitors, and RL on hard and subtly crafted hidden objectives helps the model generalize to out-of-domain monitoring tasks. To validate this generalization, we evaluate under a realistic threat model motivated by practical supply-chain attacks, where the adversary is a third-party LLM router injecting hidden objectives into code-generation requests through either prompt manipulation or code manipulation attacks. To push beyond objectives that large monitors already saturate, we also introduce four new challenging tasks even for strong monitors. Finally, we introduce CoT-Guard, a 4B-parameter monitor that demonstrates superior generalization performance under both prompt and code manipulation attacks, achieving a G-mean^2 (i.e., TNR x TPR) of 75% and outperforming GPT-5.4 (56%), GPT-5-mini (41%), and Qwen3-32B (54%), while closing the gap to Gemini-3-Flash (83%). These results demonstrate that CoT-Guard provides a practical and cost-effective user-side defense, substantially improving hidden-objective detection while avoiding the deployment cost of large monitors.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoT-Guard：小型模型实现强效监控
监控推理模型的思维链（CoT）是检测代码生成任务中隐蔽不当行为（即隐藏目标）的一种有前景的方法。虽然大型模型（如GPT-5、Gemini-3-Flash）可作为有效的CoT监控器，但由于其冗长的推理轨迹和高昂的API成本，部署成本过高，因此需要更小、更便宜的替代方案。然而，我们发现当前的小型模型（4B-8B参数）即使能访问CoT，也难以检测隐藏目标，经常将其误判为用户查询的一部分。为解决这一问题，我们提出了一种结合监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）的后训练流程：SFT通过从更强监控器中蒸馏检测行为，缩小领域内任务的差距；而RL则针对精心构造的困难隐藏目标进行训练，帮助模型泛化到领域外监控任务。为验证这种泛化能力，我们在一个由实际供应链攻击驱动的现实威胁模型下进行评估，其中攻击者是第三方LLM路由器，通过提示操纵或代码操纵攻击将隐藏目标注入代码生成请求。为了突破大型监控器已饱和的目标，我们还引入了四个即使对强监控器也具挑战性的新任务。最后，我们提出了CoT-Guard，一个4B参数的监控器，在提示操纵和代码操纵攻击下均展现出卓越的泛化性能，实现了75%的G-mean²（即TNR×TPR），优于GPT-5.4（56%）、GPT-5-mini（41%）和Qwen3-32B（54%），同时缩小了与Gemini-3-Flash（83%）的差距。这些结果表明，CoT-Guard提供了一种实用且经济高效的用户端防御，显著提升了隐藏目标检测能力，同时避免了大型监控器的部署成本。

Reinforcement Learning for Unsupervised Domain Adaptation in Spatio-Temporal Echocardiography Segmentation
Authors: Arnaud Judge, Nicolas Duchateau, Thierry Judge, Roman A. Sandler, Joseph Z. Sokol, Christian Desrosiers, Olivier Bernard, Pierre-Marc Jodoin
First: 2025-10-16T02:55:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T20:27:30+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, accepted for publication in IEEE TMI
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Domain adaptation methods aim to bridge the gap between datasets by enabling knowledge transfer across domains, reducing the need for additional expert annotations. However, many approaches struggle with reliability in the target domain, an issue particularly critical in medical image segmentation, where accuracy and anatomical validity are essential. This challenge is further exacerbated in spatio-temporal data, where the lack of temporal consistency can significantly degrade segmentation quality, and particularly in echocardiography, where the presence of artifacts and noise can further hinder segmentation performance. To address these issues, we present RL4Seg3D, an unsupervised domain adaptation framework for 2D + time echocardiography segmentation. RL4Seg3D integrates novel reward functions and a fusion scheme to enhance key landmark precision in its segmentations while processing full-sized input videos. By leveraging reinforcement learning for image segmentation, our approach improves accuracy, anatomical validity, and temporal consistency while also providing, as a beneficial side effect, a robust uncertainty estimator, which can be used at test time to further enhance segmentation performance. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework on over 30,000 echocardiographic videos, showing that it outperforms standard domain adaptation techniques without the need for any labels on the target domain. Code is available at https://github.com/arnaudjudge/RL4Seg3D.

Beyond Softmax: A Natural Parameterization for Categorical Random Variables
Authors: Alessandro Manenti, Cesare Alippi
First: 2025-09-29T12:55:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T20:11:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Latent categorical variables are frequently found in deep learning architectures. They can model actions in discrete reinforcement-learning environments, represent categories in latent-variable models, or express relations in graph neural networks. Despite their widespread use, their discrete nature poses significant challenges to gradient-descent learning algorithms. While a substantial body of work has offered improved gradient estimation techniques, we take a complementary approach. Specifically, we: 1) revisit the ubiquitous $\textit{softmax}$ function and demonstrate its limitations from an information-geometric perspective; 2) replace the $\textit{softmax}$ with the $\textit{catnat}$ function, a function composed of a sequence of hierarchical binary splits; we prove that this choice offers significant advantages to gradient descent due to the resulting diagonal Fisher Information Matrix. A rich set of experiments - including graph structure learning, variational autoencoders, and reinforcement learning - empirically show that the proposed function improves the learning efficiency and yields models characterized by consistently higher test performance. $\textit{Catnat}$ is simple to implement and seamlessly integrates into existing codebases. Moreover, it remains compatible with standard training stabilization techniques and, as such, offers a better alternative to the $\textit{softmax}$ function.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越Softmax：分类随机变量的自然参数化方法
潜在分类变量在深度学习架构中频繁出现。它们可以建模离散强化学习环境中的动作、表示潜变量模型中的类别，或在图神经网络中表达关系。尽管应用广泛，但其离散性质给梯度下降学习算法带来了重大挑战。虽然已有大量研究提出了改进的梯度估计技术，我们则采用互补方法。具体而言：1）重新审视广泛使用的$\textit{softmax}$函数，并从信息几何角度揭示其局限性；2）用$\textit{catnat}$函数替代$\textit{softmax}$，该函数由一系列层次化二元分裂组成；我们证明这一选择因产生对角Fisher信息矩阵而为梯度下降带来显著优势。丰富的实验（包括图结构学习、变分自编码器和强化学习）表明，所提函数能提升学习效率，并生成具有持续更高测试性能的模型。$\textit{Catnat}$实现简单，可无缝集成到现有代码库中，且与标准训练稳定技术兼容，因此是$\textit{softmax}$函数的更优替代方案。
