The authors introduce the catnat function, which decomposes categorical variables into hierarchical binary splits, and prove that this parameterization yields a diagonal Fisher Information Matrix, thereby improving gradient descent efficiency. Extensive experiments across graph structure learning, variational autoencoders, and reinforcement learning demonstrate that catnat consistently enhances learning efficiency and test performance, while being simple to implement and compatible with existing training techniques.

ODRPO: Ordinal Decompositions of Discrete Rewards for Robust Policy Optimization
Authors: Nirmal Patel, Fei Wang, Inderjit Dhillon
First: 2026-05-12T19:17:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T19:17:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) utilizes Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) for non-verifiable domains such as long-form question answering and open-ended instruction following. These domains often rely on LLM based auto-raters to provide granular, multi-tier discrete rewards (e.g., 1-10 rubrics) that are inherently stochastic due to prompt sensitivity and sampling randomness. We empirically verify the stochasticity of auto-raters that can propagate and corrupt standard advantage estimators like GRPO and MaxRL, as a noisy reward samples can skew normalization statistics and degrade the global learning signal. Empirically, sampling more rewards and taking majority voting may reduce the noise and improve performance, but this approach is computationally expensive. To address this bottleneck, we introduce $\textbf{O}$rdinal $\textbf{D}$ecomposition for $\textbf{R}$obust $\textbf{P}$olicy $\textbf{O}$ptimization ($\textbf{ODRPO}$), a framework that structurally isolates evaluation noise by decomposing discrete rewards into a sequence of ordinal binary indicators. By independently computing and accumulating advantages across these progressively challenging success thresholds, ODRPO prevents outlier evaluations from corrupting the global update while establishing an implicit, variance-aware learning curriculum. Empirically, ODRPO achieves robust performance on Qwen2.5-7B and Qwen3-4B models, outperforming baselines with relative improvements of upto 14.8% on FACTS-grounding-v2 and 7.5% on Alpaca-Evals. Critically, these gains are achieved with negligible training-time overhead, as ODRPO requires no additional compute per step compared to standard estimators. Supported by theoretical analysis confirming its optimization stability, ODRPO provides a scalable and robust framework for aligning models within the noisy, discrete evaluation landscape of modern RLAIF.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ODRPO：面向鲁棒策略优化的离散奖励序数分解方法
大语言模型（LLM）的对齐在非可验证领域（如长文本问答和开放式指令遵循）中利用基于AI反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）。这些领域通常依赖基于LLM的自动评分器提供细粒度、多层次的离散奖励（如1-10分制），但由于提示敏感性和采样随机性，这些奖励本质上具有随机性。我们通过实验验证了自动评分器的随机性，这种随机性可能传播并破坏GRPO和MaxRL等标准优势估计器，因为噪声奖励样本会扭曲归一化统计量并降低全局学习信号。实验表明，采样更多奖励并采用多数投票可降低噪声并提升性能，但这种方法计算成本高昂。为解决这一瓶颈，我们提出序数分解鲁棒策略优化（ODRPO）框架，该框架通过将离散奖励分解为一系列序数二元指标，从结构上隔离评估噪声。通过独立计算并累积这些渐进式成功阈值上的优势，ODRPO可防止异常评估破坏全局更新，同时建立隐式的方差感知学习课程。实验表明，ODRPO在Qwen2.5-7B和Qwen3-4B模型上实现了鲁棒性能，在FACTS-grounding-v2和Alpaca-Evals上分别相对基线提升高达14.8%和7.5%。关键的是，这些增益几乎不增加训练时间开销，因为ODRPO相比标准估计器每步无需额外计算。在理论分析验证其优化稳定性的支持下，ODRPO为在现代RLAIF的噪声离散评估环境中对齐模型提供了可扩展且鲁棒的框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of noisy discrete rewards in Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) for aligning Large Language Models, where auto-raters produce stochastic multi-tier scores that corrupt standard advantage estimators like GRPO and MaxRL. The authors propose ODRPO (Ordinal Decomposition for Robust Policy Optimization), which decomposes discrete rewards into a sequence of ordinal binary indicators, computing advantages independently across success thresholds to isolate evaluation noise and create a variance-aware learning curriculum. Experiments on Qwen2.5-7B and Qwen3-4B models show that ODRPO achieves relative improvements of up to 14.8% on FACTS-grounding-v2 and 7.5% on Alpaca-Evals over baselines, with negligible training-time overhead and theoretical guarantees of optimization stability.
该论文针对基于AI反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）中对齐大语言模型时离散奖励的噪声问题，其中自动评分器产生的随机多级分数会破坏GRPO和MaxRL等标准优势估计器。作者提出ODRPO（面向鲁棒策略优化的序数分解方法），将离散奖励分解为一系列序数二元指标，通过独立计算不同成功阈值上的优势来隔离评估噪声，并建立隐式的方差感知学习课程。在Qwen2.5-7B和Qwen3-4B模型上的实验表明，ODRPO在FACTS-grounding-v2和Alpaca-Evals上分别实现了相比基线最高14.8%和7.5%的相对改进，且训练开销可忽略不计，同时具备优化稳定性的理论保证。
Multi-Armed Sampling Problem and the End of Exploration
Authors: Mohammad Pedramfar, Siamak Ravanbakhsh
First: 2025-07-14T20:50:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T19:14:11+00:00
Comments: 29th International Conference on Artificial Intelligence and Statistics (AISTATS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces the framework of multi-armed sampling, which serves as the sampling counterpart to the optimization problem of multi-armed bandits. Our primary motivation is to rigorously examine the exploration-exploitation trade-off in the context of sampling. We systematically define plausible notions of regret for this framework and establish corresponding lower bounds. We then propose a simple algorithm that achieves near-optimal regret bounds. Our theoretical results suggest that, in contrast to optimization, sampling barely requires any exploration. To further connect our findings with those of multi-armed bandits, we define a continuous family of problems and associated regret measures that smoothly interpolate and unify multi-armed sampling and multi-armed bandit problems using a temperature parameter. We believe that the multi-armed sampling framework and our findings in this setting can play a foundational role in the study of sampling, including recent neural samplers, much like the role of multi-armed bandits in reinforcement learning. In particular, our work sheds light on the role of exploration (or lack thereof) and the convergence properties of algorithms for entropy-regularized reinforcement learning, fine-tuning of pretrained models and reinforcement learning with human feedback (RLHF).
中文标题/摘要
标题：多臂采样问题与探索的终结
本文提出了多臂采样框架，作为多臂老虎机优化问题的采样对应物。我们的主要动机是在采样背景下严格审视探索-利用权衡。我们系统性地为该框架定义了合理的遗憾概念，并建立了相应的下界。随后，我们提出了一种简单的算法，实现了接近最优的遗憾界。我们的理论结果表明，与优化相比，采样几乎不需要任何探索。为了进一步将我们的发现与多臂老虎机联系起来，我们定义了一个连续的问题族及其相关的遗憾度量，通过温度参数平滑地插值并统一了多臂采样和多臂老虎机问题。我们相信，多臂采样框架及其在此背景下的发现可以在采样研究中发挥基础性作用，包括最近的神经采样器，正如多臂老虎机在强化学习中的作用一样。特别是，我们的工作揭示了探索（或缺乏探索）的作用，以及熵正则化强化学习、预训练模型微调和基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）算法的收敛性质。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces the multi-armed sampling framework as a counterpart to multi-armed bandit optimization, motivated by the need to rigorously examine the exploration-exploitation trade-off in sampling. The authors define regret notions for this framework, establish lower bounds, and propose a simple algorithm achieving near-optimal regret. Their theoretical results show that, unlike optimization, sampling requires minimal exploration. They further unify multi-armed sampling and bandits via a temperature parameter, and the findings have implications for entropy-regularized reinforcement learning, fine-tuning, and RLHF.
本文提出了多臂采样框架，作为多臂老虎机优化问题的采样对应，旨在严格研究采样中的探索-利用权衡。作者定义了该框架下的遗憾概念，建立了下界，并提出了一种实现接近最优遗憾的简单算法。理论结果表明，与优化不同，采样几乎不需要探索。他们还通过温度参数将多臂采样与多臂老虎机问题统一起来，该发现对熵正则化强化学习、微调和基于人类反馈的强化学习具有启示意义。
Macro-Action Based Multi-Agent Instruction Following through Value Cancellation
Authors: Wo Wei Lin, Ethan Rathbun, Enrico Marchesini Xiang Zhi Tan
First: 2026-05-12T19:01:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T19:01:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) in real-world use cases may need to adapt to external natural language instructions that interrupt ongoing behavior and conflict with long-horizon objectives. However, conditioning rewards on instructions introduces a fundamental failure mode as Bellman updates couple value estimates across instruction contexts, leading to inconsistent values when instructions interrupt macro-actions. We propose Macro-Action Value Correction for Instruction Compliance (MAVIC), which corrects Bellman backups at instruction boundaries by correcting the incoming instruction objective and restoring the continuation value under the current objective. Unlike reward shaping, MAVIC modifies the bootstrapping target itself, enabling consistent value estimation under stochastic instruction switching within a unified policy. We provide theoretical analysis and an actor-critic implementation, and show that MAVIC achieves high instruction compliance while preserving base task performance in increasingly complex cooperative multi-agent environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于宏动作的多智能体指令跟随：通过价值校正实现
多智能体强化学习在实际应用中可能需要适应外部自然语言指令，这些指令会中断正在进行的动作并与长期目标冲突。然而，将奖励与指令关联会引入一种根本性失败模式：贝尔曼更新在不同指令上下文中耦合价值估计，导致指令中断宏动作时价值不一致。我们提出面向指令遵从的宏动作价值校正方法（MAVIC），该方法通过校正指令边界处的贝尔曼回溯：修正传入的指令目标，并在当前目标下恢复延续价值。与奖励塑形不同，MAVIC直接修改自举目标本身，从而在统一策略下实现随机指令切换时的一致价值估计。我们提供了理论分析与演员-评论家实现，并证明MAVIC在日益复杂的协作多智能体环境中能保持高指令遵从性，同时维持基础任务性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) systems needing to follow external natural language instructions that may interrupt ongoing macro-actions and conflict with long-term goals, where standard Bellman updates cause inconsistent value estimates across different instruction contexts. To solve this, the authors propose Macro-Action Value Correction for Instruction Compliance (MAVIC), a method that corrects Bellman backups at instruction boundaries by adjusting the incoming instruction objective and restoring the continuation value under the current objective, thereby modifying the bootstrapping target itself rather than using reward shaping. Experimental results in increasingly complex cooperative multi-agent environments demonstrate that MAVIC achieves high instruction compliance while preserving base task performance.
该论文针对多智能体强化学习系统需要遵循外部自然语言指令的问题，这些指令可能中断正在进行的宏动作并与长期目标冲突，而标准贝尔曼更新会导致不同指令上下文下的价值估计不一致。为此，作者提出了基于宏动作的指令遵从价值校正方法（MAVIC），通过在指令边界处校正贝尔曼备份，调整传入的指令目标并恢复当前目标下的延续价值，从而修改自举目标本身而非使用奖励塑形。在日益复杂的合作多智能体环境中的实验结果表明，MAVIC在保持基础任务性能的同时实现了高指令遵从率。
Plan Before You Trade: Inference-Time Optimization for RL Trading Agents
Authors: Eun Go, Rohan Deb, Arindam Banerjee
First: 2026-05-12T18:58:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T18:58:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning agents for portfolio management are typically trained and deployed as static policies, with no mechanism for using price forecasts at inference time. We propose $\text{FPILOT}$ (**Fin**ancial **P**lugin **I**nference-time **L**earning for **O**ptimal **T**rading), a plugin inference-time optimization framework inspired by Model Predictive Control (MPC). Our key structural insight is that future prices mostly do not depend on one agent's portfolio allocation, so a suitable predictive model can produce a multi-step price trajectory without iterative action-conditioned rollouts as in typical reinforcement learning. At each decision step, we use the forecaster's predicted price trajectory to construct an allocation-based imagined return objective, and optimize the policy at inference-time before executing one step of the trade. Our framework is compatible with any pre-trained agent and adapts the policy to the forecaster's predictions without any retraining. Evaluated across five policy learning algorithms on the TradeMaster DJ30 benchmark, $\text{FPILOT}$ produces consistent improvements in total return and return-based risk-adjusted metrics (Sharpe, Sortino, Calmar), with stochastic policies benefiting more than deterministic ones. Further, using synthetic forecasts at calibrated quality levels, we show that gains consistently improve with forecaster quality, suggesting that our performance will improve based on advances in financial forecasting.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces FPILOT, a plugin inference-time optimization framework for reinforcement learning trading agents, motivated by the limitation that static policies cannot utilize price forecasts during deployment. The method adapts Model Predictive Control by using a predictive model to generate multi-step price trajectories, which are then used to construct an allocation-based imagined return objective for optimizing the policy at each decision step without retraining. Experimental results on the TradeMaster DJ30 benchmark show consistent improvements in total return and risk-adjusted metrics across five policy learning algorithms, with gains scaling with forecaster quality.
该论文提出了FPILOT，一种用于强化学习交易代理的插件式推理时优化框架，其动机在于静态策略在部署时无法利用价格预测的局限性。该方法借鉴模型预测控制，通过预测模型生成多步价格轨迹，并基于此构建分配相关的想象回报目标，在每个决策步骤优化策略而无需重新训练。在TradeMaster DJ30基准上的实验表明，该方法在五种策略学习算法上均能持续提升总回报和风险调整指标，且收益随预测质量提高而增加。
Learning a Continue-Thinking Token for Enhanced Test-Time Scaling
Authors: Liran Ringel, Elad Tolochinsky, Yaniv Romano
First: 2025-06-12T20:28:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T18:56:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time scaling has emerged as an effective approach for improving language model performance by utilizing additional compute at inference time. Recent studies have shown that overriding end-of-thinking tokens (e.g., replacing "</think>" with "Wait") can extend reasoning steps and improve accuracy. In this work, we explore whether a dedicated continue-thinking token can be learned to trigger extended reasoning. We augment a distilled version of DeepSeek-R1 with a single learned "<|continue-thinking|>" token, training only its embedding via reinforcement learning while keeping the model weights frozen. Our experiments show that this learned token achieves improved accuracy on standard math benchmarks compared to both the baseline model and a test-time scaling approach that uses a fixed token (e.g., "Wait") for budget forcing. In particular, we observe that in cases where the fixed-token approach enhances the base model's accuracy, our method achieves a markedly greater improvement. For example, on the GSM8K benchmark, the fixed-token approach yields a 1.3% absolute improvement in accuracy, whereas our learned-token method achieves a 4.2% improvement over the base model that does not use budget forcing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习一个持续思考标记以增强测试时扩展
测试时扩展已成为一种有效方法，通过在推理时利用额外计算来提升语言模型性能。近期研究表明，覆盖结束思考标记（例如将“</think>”替换为“Wait”）可以延长推理步骤并提高准确性。在这项工作中，我们探讨是否可以学习一个专用的持续思考标记来触发扩展推理。我们为DeepSeek-R1的蒸馏版本增加一个单一的学习标记“<|continue-thinking|>”，仅通过强化学习训练其嵌入，同时保持模型权重冻结。实验表明，与基线模型以及使用固定标记（如“Wait”）进行预算强制测试时扩展的方法相比，该学习标记在标准数学基准上实现了更高的准确性。特别地，我们观察到，在固定标记方法提升基础模型准确性的情况下，我们的方法取得了显著更大的改进。例如，在GSM8K基准上，固定标记方法使准确性绝对提升1.3%，而我们的学习标记方法相比未使用预算强制的基础模型实现了4.2%的提升。

Training LLMs with Reinforcement Learning for Intent-Aware Personalized Question Answering
Authors: Maryam Amirizaniani, Benjamin Charles Germain Lee, Jevin West, Nicholas Weber
First: 2026-05-12T18:38:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T18:38:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective personalized question answering (PQA) in language models requires grounding responses in the user's underlying intent, where intent refers to the implicit ``why'' behind a query beyond its explicit wording. However, existing approaches to intent-aware personalization rely on multi-turn conversational context or rich user profiles, and do not explicitly model user intent during the reasoning process. This limits their effectiveness in single-turn settings, where the user's latent goal must be inferred from minimal input and integrated into the thinking and reasoning process. To bridge this gap, we propose IAP (Intent-Aware Personalization), a reinforcement learning framework that trains models to infer implicit user intent directly from a single-turn question and incorporate it into thinking steps through a tag-based schema for generating personalized, intent-grounded answers. By optimizing intent-aware answer trajectories under a personalized reward function, IAP reinforces generation paths that make implicit user intent explicit and produce responses that better align with the user's underlying goal. Through experiments on the LaMP-QA benchmark across six models, IAP consistently outperforms all baselines, achieving an average macro-score gain of around 7.5\% over the strongest competitor, demonstrating that modeling implicit user intent within the training objective is a promising direction for PQA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的意图感知个性化问答大语言模型训练
语言模型中的有效个性化问答（PQA）需要将回答植根于用户的潜在意图，其中意图指查询显性措辞之外的隐含“为什么”。然而，现有意图感知个性化方法依赖多轮对话上下文或丰富的用户画像，未在推理过程中显式建模用户意图，这限制了其在单轮场景中的有效性——此时必须从最小输入推断用户潜在目标并将其融入思考推理过程。为弥补这一差距，我们提出意图感知个性化（IAP）框架，该强化学习框架训练模型直接从单轮问题推断隐含用户意图，并通过基于标签的架构将其融入思考步骤以生成个性化、基于意图的回答。通过个性化奖励函数优化意图感知回答轨迹，IAP强化了使隐含用户意图显式化的生成路径，并产生更符合用户潜在目标的响应。在LaMP-QA基准上对六个模型的实验表明，IAP持续优于所有基线，相比最强竞争者平均宏分数提升约7.5%，证明在训练目标中建模隐含用户意图是PQA的一个有前景方向。

The paper addresses the challenge of personalized question answering (PQA) in single-turn settings, where existing methods fail to model implicit user intent due to reliance on multi-turn context or rich profiles. The authors propose IAP (Intent-Aware Personalization), a reinforcement learning framework that trains large language models to infer and integrate user intent into reasoning steps using a tag-based schema, optimizing intent-aware answer trajectories with a personalized reward function. Experiments on the LaMP-QA benchmark across six models show that IAP consistently outperforms all baselines, achieving an average macro-score gain of approximately 7.5% over the strongest competitor, demonstrating the effectiveness of modeling implicit intent in training objectives for PQA.

OmniNFT: Modality-wise Omni Diffusion Reinforcement for Joint Audio-Video Generation
Authors: Guohui Zhang, XiaoXiao Ma, Jie Huang, Hang Xu, Hu Yu, Siming Fu, Yuming Li, Zeyue Xue, Lin Song, Haoyang Huang, Nan Duan, Feng Zhao
First: 2026-05-12T17:56:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:56:59+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://zghhui.github.io/OmniNFT/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Recent advances in joint audio-video generation have been remarkable, yet real-world applications demand strong per-modality fidelity, cross-modal alignment, and fine-grained synchronization. Reinforcement Learning (RL) offers a promising paradigm, but its extension to multi-objective and multi-modal joint audio-video generation remains unexplored. Notably, our in-depth analysis first reveals that the primary obstacles to applying RL in this stem from: (i) multi-objective advantages inconsistency, where the advantages of multimodal outputs are not always consistent within a group; (ii) multi-modal gradients imbalance, where video-branch gradients leak into shallow audio layers responsible for intra-modal generation; (iii) uniform credit assignment, where fine-grained cross-modal alignment regions fail to get efficient exploration. These shortcomings suggest that vanilla RL fine-tuning strategy with a single global advantage often leads to suboptimal results. To address these challenges, we propose OmniNFT, a novel modality-aware online diffusion RL framework with three key innovations: (1) Modality-wise advantage routing, which routes independent per-reward advantages to their respective modality generation branches. (2) Layer-wise gradient surgery, which selectively detaches video-branch gradients on shallow audio layers while retaining those for cross-modal interaction layers. (3) Region-wise loss reweighting, which modulates policy optimization toward critical regions related to audio-video synchronization and fine-grained alignment. Extensive experiments on JavisBench and VBench with the LTX-2 backbone demonstrate that OmniNFT achieves comprehensive improvements in audio and video perceptual quality, cross-modal alignment, and audio-video synchronization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OmniNFT：面向联合音视频生成的模态级全向扩散强化
近期联合音视频生成领域取得了显著进展，但实际应用对单模态保真度、跨模态对齐及细粒度同步提出了更高要求。强化学习（RL）提供了有前景的范式，但其在多目标、多模态联合音视频生成中的扩展尚未被探索。值得注意的是，我们的深入分析首次揭示了RL在此场景应用的主要障碍：（i）多目标优势不一致性，即多模态输出的优势在组内并不总是一致；（ii）多模态梯度失衡，即视频分支梯度泄漏至负责模态内生成的浅层音频层；（iii）统一信用分配，即细粒度跨模态对齐区域无法获得高效探索。这些缺陷表明，采用单一全局优势的朴素RL微调策略往往导致次优结果。为解决上述挑战，我们提出OmniNFT——一种新颖的模态感知在线扩散RL框架，包含三项关键创新：（1）模态级优势路由，将独立奖励优势分别路由至对应模态生成分支；（2）层级梯度手术，选择性分离浅层音频层上的视频分支梯度，同时保留跨模态交互层的梯度；（3）区域级损失重加权，针对与音视频同步及细粒度对齐相关的关键区域调整策略优化。基于LTX-2骨干网络在JavisBench和VBench上的大量实验表明，OmniNFT在音频与视频感知质量、跨模态对齐及音视频同步方面实现了全面改进。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces OmniNFT, a modality-aware online diffusion reinforcement learning framework designed to address challenges in joint audio-video generation, particularly multi-objective advantages inconsistency, multi-modal gradients imbalance, and uniform credit assignment. The method proposes three key innovations: modality-wise advantage routing to assign independent rewards per modality, layer-wise gradient surgery to prevent video-branch gradients from interfering with shallow audio layers, and region-wise loss reweighting to focus on critical synchronization regions. Extensive experiments on JavisBench and VBench with the LTX-2 backbone show that OmniNFT achieves comprehensive improvements in audio and video perceptual quality, cross-modal alignment, and audio-video synchronization.
该论文提出了OmniNFT，一种模态感知的在线扩散强化学习框架，旨在解决联合音视频生成中的多目标优势不一致、多模态梯度不平衡和均匀信用分配等挑战。该方法包含三项关键创新：模态级优势路由为每个模态分配独立奖励，层级梯度手术防止视频分支梯度干扰浅层音频层，以及区域级损失重加权聚焦于关键同步区域。在JavisBench和VBench上基于LTX-2骨干网络的广泛实验表明，OmniNFT在音频和视频感知质量、跨模态对齐以及音视频同步方面均实现了全面改进。
Reward Hacking in Rubric-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Anas Mahmoud, MohammadHossein Rezaei, Zihao Wang, Anisha Gunjal, Bing Liu, Yunzhong He
First: 2026-05-12T17:54:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:54:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has enabled strong post-training gains in domains such as math and coding, though many open-ended settings rely on rubric-based rewards. We study reward hacking in rubric-based RL, where a policy is optimized against a training verifier but evaluated against a cross-family panel of three frontier judges, reducing dependence on any single evaluator. Our framework separates two sources of divergence: verifier failure, where the training verifier credits rubric criteria that reference verifiers reject, and rubric-design limitations, where even strong rubric-based verifiers favor responses that rubric-free judges rate worse overall. Across medical and science domains, weak verifiers produce large proxy-reward gains that do not transfer to the reference verifiers; exploitation grows over training and concentrates in recurring failures such as partial satisfaction of compound criteria, treating implicit content as explicit, and imprecise topical matching. Stronger verifiers substantially reduce, but do not eliminate, verifier exploitation. We also introduce a self-internalization gap, a verifier-free diagnostic based on policy log-probabilities, which tracks reference-verifier quality, detecting when the policy trained using the weak verifier stops improving. Finally, in our setting, stronger verification does not prevent reward hacking when the rubric leaves important failure modes unspecified: rubric-based verifiers prefer the RL checkpoint, while rubric-free judges prefer the base model. These disagreements coincide with gains concentrated in completeness and presence-based criteria, alongside declines in factual correctness, conciseness, relevance, and overall quality. Together, these results suggest that stronger verification reduces reward hacking, but does not by itself ensure that rubric gains correspond to broader quality gains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于评分标准的强化学习中的奖励黑客行为
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已在数学和编程等领域实现了强大的训练后性能提升，但许多开放式场景仍依赖评分标准奖励。我们研究了基于评分标准的强化学习中的奖励黑客行为，其中策略针对训练验证器进行优化，但通过跨族群的三个前沿评判者面板进行评估，以减少对单一评估者的依赖。我们的框架区分了两种分歧来源：验证器失败，即训练验证器认可的评分标准被参考验证器拒绝；以及评分标准设计局限，即使强大的基于评分标准的验证器也更倾向于那些无评分标准评判者整体评价更差的回答。在医学和科学领域，弱验证器产生了巨大的代理奖励增益，但这些增益无法迁移到参考验证器；利用行为随训练过程增长，并集中在反复出现的失败模式中，例如部分满足复合标准、将隐含内容视为显式内容以及不精确的主题匹配。更强的验证器显著减少了验证器利用，但并未完全消除。我们还引入了一个自我内化差距，这是一种基于策略对数概率的无验证器诊断方法，用于跟踪参考验证器的质量，检测何时使用弱验证器训练的策略停止改进。最后，在我们的设置中，当评分标准遗漏了重要的失败模式时，更强的验证并不能防止奖励黑客行为：基于评分标准的验证器更倾向于强化学习检查点，而无评分标准评判者则更偏好基础模型。这些分歧与基于完整性和存在性标准的增益集中出现，同时伴随着事实正确性、简洁性、相关性和整体质量的下降。综合来看，这些结果表明更强的验证减少了奖励黑客行为，但本身并不能确保评分标准增益对应更广泛的质量增益。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates reward hacking in rubric-based reinforcement learning, where a policy is optimized against a training verifier but evaluated by a panel of three reference verifiers to reduce evaluator dependence. The authors separate two sources of divergence: verifier failure, where the training verifier credits criteria that reference verifiers reject, and rubric-design limitations, where even strong rubric-based verifiers favor responses that rubric-free judges rate worse. Experiments in medical and science domains show that weak verifiers produce large proxy-reward gains that do not transfer to reference verifiers, with exploitation increasing over training and manifesting in failures like partial satisfaction of compound criteria. Stronger verifiers reduce but do not eliminate exploitation, and a self-internalization gap based on policy log-probabilities is introduced to detect when weak-verifier training stops improving. Crucially, stronger verification does not prevent reward hacking when the rubric omits important failure modes, as rubric-based verifiers prefer the RL checkpoint while rubric-free judges favor the base model, with gains in completeness and presence-based criteria coinciding with declines in factual correctness and overall quality.
该论文研究了基于评分标准的强化学习中的奖励黑客现象，其中策略针对训练验证器进行优化，但通过三个参考验证器组成的面板进行评估以减少对单一评估者的依赖。作者区分了两种分歧来源：验证器失败，即训练验证器认可参考验证器拒绝的评分标准；以及评分标准设计局限，即即使强大的基于评分标准的验证器也更倾向于评分标准无关的评判者评价更差的回答。在医学和科学领域的实验中，弱验证器产生了无法迁移到参考验证器的大幅代理奖励增益，且利用行为随训练增加，集中在部分满足复合标准等失败模式上。更强的验证器减少了但未消除利用行为，并引入基于策略对数概率的自我内化差距来检测弱验证器训练何时停止改进。关键的是，当评分标准遗漏重要失败模式时，更强的验证无法阻止奖励黑客：基于评分标准的验证器偏好强化学习检查点，而评分标准无关的评判者偏好基础模型，增益集中在完整性和存在性标准上，同时事实正确性、简洁性、相关性和整体质量下降。
Towards Affordable Energy: A Gymnasium Environment for Electric Utility Demand-Response Programs
Authors: Jose E. Aguilar Escamilla, Lingdong Zhou, Xiangqi Zhu, Huazheng Wang
First: 2026-05-12T17:48:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:48:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Extreme weather and volatile wholesale electricity markets expose residential consumers to catastrophic financial risks, yet demand response at the distribution level remains an underutilized tool for grid flexibility and energy affordability. While a demand-response program can shield consumers by issuing financial credits during high-price periods, optimizing this sequential decision-making process presents a unique challenge for reinforcement learning despite the plentiful offline historical smart meter and wholesale pricing data available publicly. Offline historical data fails to capture the dynamic, interactive feedback loop between an electric utility's pricing signals and customer acceptance and adaptation to a demand-response program. To address this, we introduce DR-Gym, an open-source, online Gymnasium-compatible environment designed to train and evaluate demand-response from the electric utility's perspective. Unlike existing device-level energy simulators, our environment focuses on the market-level electric utility setting and provides a rich observational space relevant to the electric utility. The simulator additionally features a regime-switching wholesale price model calibrated to real-world extreme events, alongside physics-based building demand profiles. For our learning signal, we use a configurable, multi-objective reward function for specifying diverse learning objectives. We demonstrate through baseline strategies and data snapshots the capability of our simulator to create realistic and learnable environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向可负担能源：面向电力公用事业需求响应程序的Gymnasium环境
极端天气和波动的批发电力市场使居民消费者面临灾难性财务风险，然而配电层面的需求响应作为电网灵活性和能源可负担性的工具仍未得到充分利用。尽管需求响应程序可通过在高电价时期发放财务信用来保护消费者，但优化这一序列决策过程对强化学习提出了独特挑战——尽管公开可用的离线历史智能电表和批发定价数据充足。离线历史数据无法捕捉电力公用事业定价信号与客户对需求响应程序的接受及适应之间的动态交互反馈循环。为此，我们提出DR-Gym，一个开源的在线Gymnasium兼容环境，旨在从电力公用事业视角训练和评估需求响应。与现有设备级能源模拟器不同，我们的环境聚焦于市场级电力公用事业场景，并提供与电力公用事业相关的丰富观测空间。该模拟器还具备基于真实极端事件校准的体制转换批发价格模型，以及基于物理的建筑需求曲线。对于学习信号，我们使用可配置的多目标奖励函数来指定多样化的学习目标。通过基线策略和数据快照，我们展示了模拟器创建真实且可学习环境的能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of optimizing demand-response programs for electric utilities to protect residential consumers from financial risks during extreme weather and volatile wholesale markets. The authors propose DR-Gym, an open-source Gymnasium-compatible environment that simulates the interactive feedback loop between utility pricing signals and customer behavior, using offline historical smart meter and wholesale data. The environment features a regime-switching wholesale price model calibrated to real-world extreme events and physics-based building demand profiles, with a configurable multi-objective reward function. Baseline strategies and data snapshots demonstrate that DR-Gym creates realistic and learnable environments for training reinforcement learning agents.
该论文针对电力公司优化需求响应计划以保护居民消费者在极端天气和波动性批发市场中免受财务风险的挑战。作者提出了DR-Gym，一个开源的、兼容Gymnasium的环境，模拟了电力公司定价信号与客户行为之间的动态交互反馈循环，利用离线历史智能电表和批发市场数据。该环境包含一个基于真实极端事件校准的体制转换批发价格模型和基于物理的建筑需求曲线，并具有可配置的多目标奖励函数。基线策略和数据快照表明，DR-Gym能够创建真实且可学习的强化学习训练环境。
ORCE: Order-Aware Alignment of Verbalized Confidence in Large Language Models
Authors: Chen Li, Xiaoling Hu, Songzhu Zheng, Jiawei Zhou, Chao Chen
First: 2026-05-12T17:39:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:39:43+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) often produce answers with high certainty even when they are incorrect, making reliable confidence estimation essential for deployment in real-world scenarios. Verbalized confidence, where models explicitly state their confidence in natural language, provides a flexible and user-facing uncertainty signal that can be applied even when token logits are unavailable. However, existing verbalized-confidence methods often optimize answer generation and confidence generation jointly, which can cause confidence-alignment objectives to interfere with answer accuracy. In this work, we propose a decoupled and order-aware framework for verbalized confidence calibration. Our method first generates an answer and then estimates confidence conditioned on the fixed question--answer pair, allowing confidence optimization without directly perturbing the answer-generation process. To align confidence with correctness likelihood, we construct a sampling-based surrogate from multiple model completions and optimize rank-based reinforcement learning objectives that encourage responses with higher estimated correctness likelihood to receive higher verbalized confidence. Experiments on reasoning and knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that our method improves calibration and failure prediction performance while largely preserving answer accuracy. These results demonstrate that verbalized confidence can be more reliably aligned by decoupling confidence estimation from answer generation and optimizing the relative ordering of confidence across responses.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ORCE：大型语言模型中口头化置信度的顺序感知对齐
大型语言模型（LLM）即使在回答错误时也常表现出高度确定性，这使得可靠的置信度估计对于实际部署至关重要。口头化置信度（即模型以自然语言明确陈述其置信度）提供了一种灵活且面向用户的不确定性信号，即使在无法获取词元对数概率时也能使用。然而，现有的口头化置信度方法通常联合优化答案生成和置信度生成，这可能导致置信度对齐目标干扰答案准确性。本文提出了一种解耦且顺序感知的口头化置信度校准框架。该方法首先生成答案，然后基于固定的问答对估计置信度，从而在不直接扰动答案生成过程的情况下优化置信度。为了将置信度与正确可能性对齐，我们基于多次模型补全构建了采样替代指标，并优化基于排序的强化学习目标，鼓励具有更高估计正确可能性的响应获得更高的口头化置信度。在推理和知识密集型基准上的实验表明，我们的方法在基本保持答案准确性的同时，改善了校准和失败预测性能。这些结果证明，通过将置信度估计与答案生成解耦并优化响应间置信度的相对排序，可以更可靠地对齐口头化置信度。
Summary / 总结
Large language models often express high confidence even when wrong, motivating the need for reliable verbalized confidence estimation. The proposed ORCE framework decouples answer generation from confidence estimation by first generating an answer and then estimating confidence conditioned on the fixed question-answer pair, using a sampling-based surrogate from multiple completions and rank-based reinforcement learning to align confidence with correctness likelihood. Experiments on reasoning and knowledge-intensive benchmarks demonstrate that this method improves calibration and failure prediction performance while largely preserving answer accuracy.
大型语言模型在回答错误时仍常表现出高置信度，因此需要可靠的言语化置信度估计。提出的ORCE框架将答案生成与置信度估计解耦，先固定问答对再估计置信度，利用多次生成的采样代理和基于排序的强化学习来对齐置信度与正确可能性。在推理和知识密集型基准上的实验表明，该方法在基本保持答案准确性的同时，提升了校准和失败预测性能。
Learning Minimally Rigid Graphs with High Realization Counts
Authors: Oleksandr Slyvka, Jan Rubeš, Rodrigo Alves, Jan Legerský
Venue: IJCAI 2026
First: 2026-05-12T17:23:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:23:30+00:00
Comments: This is an extended version of the paper accepted to IJCAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
For minimally rigid graphs, the same edge-length data can admit multiple realizations (up to translations and rotations). Finding graphs with exceptionally many realizations is an extremal problem in rigidity theory, but exhaustive search quickly becomes infeasible due to the super-exponential growth of the number of candidate graphs and the high cost of realization-count evaluation. We propose a reinforcement-learning approach that constructs minimally rigid graphs via 0- and 1-extensions, also known as Henneberg moves. We optimize realization-count invariants using the Deep Cross-Entropy Method with a policy parameterized by a Graph Isomorphism Network encoder and a permutation-equivariant extension-level action head. Empirically, our method matches the known optima for planar realization counts and improves the best known bounds for spherical realization counts, yielding new record graphs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习具有高实现数量的最小刚性图
对于最小刚性图，相同的边长数据可能允许多种实现（在平移和旋转意义下）。寻找具有异常多实现的图是刚性理论中的一个极值问题，但由于候选图数量超指数增长以及实现计数评估的高成本，穷举搜索很快变得不可行。我们提出了一种强化学习方法，通过0-扩展和1-扩展（也称为Henneberg移动）构建最小刚性图。我们使用深度交叉熵方法优化实现计数不变量，其策略由图同构网络编码器和置换等变扩展级动作头参数化。实验表明，我们的方法匹配了平面实现计数的已知最优值，并改进了球面实现计数的已知最佳界限，产生了新的记录图。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of finding minimally rigid graphs that admit exceptionally many realizations from the same edge-length data, an extremal problem in rigidity theory where exhaustive search is infeasible due to super-exponential growth. The authors propose a reinforcement-learning approach that constructs graphs via 0- and 1-extensions (Henneberg moves), optimizing realization-count invariants using the Deep Cross-Entropy Method with a policy parameterized by a Graph Isomorphism Network encoder and a permutation-equivariant action head. Empirically, the method matches known optima for planar realization counts and improves the best known bounds for spherical realization counts, yielding new record graphs.
该论文针对在刚性理论中寻找具有异常多实现数量的最小刚性图这一极值问题，由于候选图数量超指数增长且实现计数评估成本高昂，穷举搜索不可行。作者提出了一种强化学习方法，通过0-扩展和1-扩展（Henneberg移动）构建图，利用深度交叉熵方法优化实现计数不变量，策略由图同构网络编码器和置换等变扩展级动作头参数化。实验结果表明，该方法在平面实现计数上匹配已知最优值，并在球面实现计数上改进了最佳已知界限，生成了新的记录图。
Aligning Flow Map Policies with Optimal Q-Guidance
Authors: Christos Ziakas, Alessandra Russo, Avishek Joey Bose
First: 2026-05-12T17:12:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:12:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative policies based on expressive model classes, such as diffusion and flow matching, are well-suited to complex control problems with highly multimodal action distributions. Their expressivity, however, comes at a significant inference cost: generating each action typically requires simulating many steps of the generative process, compounding latency across sequential decision-making rollouts. We introduce flow map policies, a novel class of generative policies designed for fast action generation by learning to take arbitrary-size jumps including one-step jumps-across the generative dynamics of existing flow-based policies. We instantiate flow map policies for offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) and formulate online adaptation as a trust-region optimization problem that improves the critic's Q-value while remaining close to the offline policy. We theoretically derive FLOW MAP Q-GUIDANCE (FMQ), a principled closed-form learning target that is optimal for adapting offline flow map policies under a critic-guided trust-region constraint. We further introduce Q-GUIDED BEAM SEARCH (QGBS), a stochastic flow-map sampler that combines renoising with beam search to enable iterative inference-time refinement. Across 12 challenging robotic manipulation and locomotion tasks from OGBench and RoboMimic, FMQ achieves state-of-the-art performance in offline-to-online RL, outperforming the previous one-step policy MVP by a relative improvement of 21.3% on the average success rate.
中文标题/摘要
标题：流映射策略与最优Q引导的对齐
基于表达性模型类（如扩散和流匹配）的生成策略非常适合具有高度多模态动作分布的复杂控制问题。然而，其表达性带来了显著的推理成本：生成每个动作通常需要模拟生成过程的多个步骤，从而在顺序决策的展开中累积延迟。我们引入了流映射策略，这是一种新型的生成策略，旨在通过学习在现有基于流的策略的生成动态中执行任意大小的跳跃（包括单步跳跃）来实现快速动作生成。我们将流映射策略实例化用于离线到在线强化学习，并将在线适应形式化为一个信任区域优化问题，该问题在保持接近离线策略的同时提高评论家的Q值。我们从理论上推导了流映射Q引导（FMQ），这是一个原则性的闭式学习目标，用于在评论家引导的信任区域约束下最优地适应离线流映射策略。我们进一步引入了Q引导束搜索（QGBS），这是一种随机流映射采样器，将重新噪声化与束搜索相结合，以实现迭代推理时的细化。在来自OGBench和RoboMimic的12个具有挑战性的机器人操作和 locomotion 任务中，FMQ在离线到在线强化学习中实现了最先进的性能，相比之前的一步策略MVP，平均成功率相对提高了21.3%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high inference cost of generative policies like diffusion and flow matching in complex control tasks, which require many simulation steps per action. The authors propose flow map policies that enable arbitrary-size jumps, including one-step generation, by learning to skip across the generative dynamics of existing flow-based policies. For offline-to-online reinforcement learning, they introduce FLOW MAP Q-GUIDANCE (FMQ), a closed-form learning target derived from a trust-region optimization that optimally adapts offline policies using critic Q-values, along with Q-GUIDED BEAM SEARCH (QGBS) for iterative refinement. Experiments on 12 robotic tasks from OGBench and RoboMimic show FMQ achieves state-of-the-art performance, outperforming the previous one-step policy MVP by a 21.3% relative improvement in average success rate.
该论文针对扩散和流匹配等生成式策略在复杂控制任务中推理成本高的问题，提出流图策略，通过学习在现有流基策略的生成动力学中进行任意大小跳跃（包括单步跳跃），实现快速动作生成。在离线到在线强化学习中，作者提出流图Q引导（FMQ），这是一个基于信任域优化的闭式学习目标，利用评论家Q值最优地适应离线策略，并引入Q引导束搜索（QGBS）进行迭代推理时优化。在OGBench和RoboMimic的12项机器人操作和移动任务上，FMQ实现了最先进的性能，平均成功率相比之前的一步策略MVP相对提升21.3%。
Model-based Bootstrap of Controlled Markov Chains
Authors: Ziwei Su, Imon Banerjee, Diego Klabjan
First: 2026-05-12T17:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:05:59+00:00
Comments: 45 pages, 7 figures, 19 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose and analyze a model-based bootstrap for transition kernels in finite controlled Markov chains (CMCs) with possibly nonstationary or history-dependent control policies, a setting that arises naturally in offline reinforcement learning (RL) when the behavior policy generating the data is unknown. We establish distributional consistency of the bootstrap transition estimator in both a single long-chain regime and the episodic offline RL regime. The key technical tools are a novel bootstrap law of large numbers (LLN) for the visitation counts and a novel use of the martingale central limit theorem (CLT) for the bootstrap transition increments. We extend bootstrap distributional consistency to the downstream targets of offline policy evaluation (OPE) and optimal policy recovery (OPR) via the delta method by verifying Hadamard differentiability of the Bellman operators, yielding asymptotically valid confidence intervals for value and $Q$-functions. Experiments on the RiverSwim problem show that the proposed bootstrap confidence intervals (CIs), especially the percentile CIs, outperform the episodic bootstrap and plug-in CLT CIs, and are often close to nominal ($50\%$, $90\%$, $95\%$) coverage, while the baselines are poorly calibrated at small sample sizes and short episode lengths.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型的自举法在受控马尔可夫链中的应用
我们提出并分析了一种针对有限受控马尔可夫链（CMC）中转移核的基于模型的自举法，适用于可能非平稳或依赖历史的控制策略——这一设定在离线强化学习（RL）中自然出现，当生成数据的行为策略未知时。我们在单长链场景和情节式离线RL场景中建立了自举转移估计量的分布一致性。关键技术工具包括：针对访问计数的新型自举大数定律（LLN），以及针对自举转移增量的鞅中心极限定理（CLT）的新颖应用。通过验证贝尔曼算子的哈达玛可微性，我们利用Delta方法将自举分布一致性扩展到离线策略评估（OPE）和最优策略恢复（OPR）的下游目标，从而为价值函数和Q函数生成渐近有效的置信区间。在RiverSwim问题上的实验表明，所提出的自举置信区间（CI），尤其是百分位CI，优于情节式自举和插件CLT CI，且通常接近名义覆盖率（50%、90%、95%），而基线方法在小样本量和短情节长度下校准效果较差。
Summary / 总结
This paper proposes a model-based bootstrap method for estimating transition kernels in finite controlled Markov chains, motivated by offline reinforcement learning scenarios where the behavior policy is unknown. The method constructs bootstrap samples from the empirical transition counts and establishes distributional consistency using a novel bootstrap law of large numbers for visitation counts and a martingale central limit theorem for transition increments. The consistency is extended to offline policy evaluation and optimal policy recovery via the delta method, leveraging Hadamard differentiability of Bellman operators to produce asymptotically valid confidence intervals. Experiments on the RiverSwim problem demonstrate that the proposed bootstrap confidence intervals, particularly the percentile intervals, achieve coverage close to nominal levels (50%, 90%, 95%) and outperform episodic bootstrap and plug-in CLT baselines, especially with small sample sizes and short episode lengths.
本文针对有限受控马尔可夫链中的转移核提出了一种基于模型的bootstrap方法，其动机源于离线强化学习中行为策略未知的场景。该方法通过经验转移计数构建bootstrap样本，并利用新颖的访问计数bootstrap大数定律和转移增量的鞅中心极限定理证明了分布一致性。通过验证Bellman算子的Hadamard可微性，借助delta方法将一致性扩展到离线策略评估和最优策略恢复，从而生成渐近有效的置信区间。在RiverSwim问题上的实验表明，所提出的bootstrap置信区间（尤其是百分位区间）的覆盖率接近名义水平（50%、90%、95%），并且在样本量小和回合长度短的情况下优于回合bootstrap和插件CLT基线方法。
Semantic Reward Collapse and the Preservation of Epistemic Integrity in Adaptive AI Systems
Authors: William Parris
First: 2026-05-12T17:03:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T17:03:26+00:00
Comments: 15 pages including references. Position and framework paper. Companion empirical work available at arXiv:2604.17587
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and preference optimization have substantially improved the usability, coherence, and safety of large language models. However, recurring behaviors such as performative certainty, hallucinated continuity, calibration drift, sycophancy, and suppression of visible uncertainty suggest unresolved structural issues within scalarized preference optimization systems. We propose Semantic Reward Collapse (SRC): the compression of semantically distinct forms of evaluative dissatisfaction into generalized optimization signals. Under SRC, categories such as factual incorrectness, uncertainty disclosure, formatting dissatisfaction, latency, and social preference may become entangled within a shared reward topology despite representing fundamentally different epistemic classes. We argue that adaptive reasoning systems operating under generalized evaluative pressure may drift toward suppression of visible epistemic failure rather than preservation of calibrated uncertainty integrity. These behaviors are framed strictly as optimization consequences rather than evidence of deception or anthropomorphic agency. Drawing on institutional proxy collapse, metric gaming, software reliability engineering, and human learning theory, we propose that uncertainty disclosure and escalation behavior should be treated as protected epistemic conduct rather than globally penalized task incompletion. Finally, we introduce Constitutional Reward Stratification (CRS), a domain-aware reward framework intended to preserve differentiated epistemic attribution within adaptive learning systems. We present CRS not as a validated solution, but as a testable governance-oriented research direction requiring further empirical investigation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语义奖励坍塌与自适应AI系统中认知完整性的维护
近期基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）与偏好优化的进展显著提升了大型语言模型的可用性、连贯性与安全性。然而，诸如表演性确定性、幻觉连续性、校准漂移、谄媚行为以及抑制可见不确定性等反复出现的行为，表明标量偏好优化系统内存在未解决的结构性问题。 我们提出语义奖励坍塌（SRC）：将语义上不同形式的评价性不满压缩为通用优化信号。在SRC下，事实错误、不确定性披露、格式不满、延迟及社会偏好等类别，尽管代表根本不同的认知类别，却可能纠缠于共享的奖励拓扑中。 我们认为，在通用评价压力下运行的自适应推理系统，可能倾向于抑制可见的认知失败，而非维护校准的不确定性完整性。这些行为被严格视为优化后果，而非欺骗或拟人化能动性的证据。 借鉴制度代理坍塌、指标博弈、软件可靠性工程及人类学习理论，我们提出不确定性披露与升级行为应被视为受保护的认知行为，而非全局惩罚的任务未完成。 最后，我们引入宪法奖励分层（CRS），一种旨在维护自适应学习系统中差异化认知归因的领域感知奖励框架。我们提出CRS并非作为已验证的解决方案，而是作为需要进一步实证研究的可测试治理导向研究方向。
Summary / 总结
This position paper identifies Semantic Reward Collapse (SRC) as a structural issue in reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and preference optimization systems, where distinct forms of evaluative dissatisfaction—such as factual errors, uncertainty disclosure, and formatting issues—become entangled into a single optimization signal. The authors argue that this collapse drives adaptive AI systems toward suppressing visible epistemic failures like uncertainty and calibration drift, rather than preserving calibrated integrity, and they frame these behaviors as optimization consequences rather than deception. Drawing on institutional proxy collapse and human learning theory, they propose Constitutional Reward Stratification (CRS), a domain-aware reward framework that treats uncertainty disclosure as protected epistemic conduct, though they present CRS as a testable research direction requiring further empirical validation rather than a validated solution.

When Does Non-Uniform Replay Matter in Reinforcement Learning?
Authors: Michal Korniak, Mikołaj Czarnecki, Yarden As, Piotr Miłoś, Pieter Abbeel, Michal Nauman
First: 2026-05-11T09:11:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:56:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern off-policy reinforcement learning algorithms often rely on simple uniform replay sampling and it remains unclear when and why non-uniform replay improves over this strong baseline. Across diverse RL settings, we show that the effectiveness of non-uniform replay is governed by three factors: replay volume, the number of replayed transitions per environment step; expected recency, how recent sampled transitions are; and the entropy of the replay sampling distribution. Our main contribution is clarifying when non-uniform replay is beneficial and providing practical guidance for replay design in modern off-policy RL. Namely, we find that non-uniform replay is most beneficial when replay volume is low, and that high-entropy sampling is important even at comparable expected recency. Motivated by these findings, we adopt a simple Truncated Geometric replay that biases sampling toward recent experience while preserving high entropy and incurring negligible computational overhead. Across large-scale parallel simulation, single-task, and multi-task settings, including three modern algorithms evaluated on five RL benchmark suites, this replay sampling strategy improves sample efficiency in low-volume regimes while remaining competitive when replay volume is high.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中非均匀回放何时重要？
现代离策略强化学习算法通常依赖简单的均匀回放采样，而非均匀回放何时以及为何能超越这一强基线尚不明确。通过多种强化学习设置，我们表明非均匀回放的有效性受三个因素支配：回放容量（每环境步回放的转换数）、预期新近度（采样转换的新近程度）以及回放采样分布的熵。我们的主要贡献是阐明非均匀回放何时有益，并为现代离策略强化学习中的回放设计提供实用指导。具体而言，我们发现非均匀回放在回放容量较低时最为有益，且即使在预期新近度相当的情况下，高熵采样也很重要。受这些发现启发，我们采用一种简单的截断几何回放，它在保持高熵且计算开销可忽略的同时，将采样偏向近期经验。在大规模并行模拟、单任务和多任务设置中（包括在五个强化学习基准套件上评估的三种现代算法），这种回放采样策略在低容量场景下提升了样本效率，而在高容量场景下仍保持竞争力。
Trust the Batch, On- or Off-Policy: Adaptive Policy Optimization for RL Post-Training
Authors: Rasool Fakoor, Murdock Aubry, Nicholas Stranges, Alexander J. Smola
First: 2026-05-12T16:44:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:44:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning is structurally harder than supervised learning because the policy changes the data distribution it learns from. The resulting fragility is especially visible in large-model training, where the training and rollout systems differ in numerical precision, sampling, and other implementation details. Existing methods manage this fragility by adding hyper-parameters to the training objective, which makes the algorithm more sensitive to its configuration and requires retuning whenever the task, model scale, or distribution mismatch changes. This fragility traces to two concerns that current objectives entangle through hyper-parameters set before training begins: a trust-region concern, that updates should not move the policy too far from its current value, and an off-policy concern, that data from older or different behavior policies should influence the update only to the extent that it remains reliable. Neither concern is a constant to set in advance, and their severity is reflected in the policy-ratio distribution of the current batch. We present a simple yet effective batch-adaptive objective that replaces fixed clipping with the normalized effective sample size of the policy ratios. The same statistic caps the score-function weight and sets the strength of an off-policy regularizer, so the update stays close to the usual on-policy score-function update when ratios are nearly uniform, and tightens automatically when stale or mismatched data cause ratio concentration, while retaining a nonzero learning signal on high-ratio tokens. Experiments across a wide range of settings show that our method matches or exceeds tuned baselines, introducing no new objective hyper-parameters and removing several existing ones. The code is available at https://github.com/FeynRL-project/FeynRL.
Summary / 总结
Reinforcement learning post-training for large models suffers from fragility due to distribution mismatch between training and rollout systems, which existing methods address by adding hyper-parameters that require retuning. The authors propose a batch-adaptive objective that replaces fixed clipping with the normalized effective sample size of policy ratios, dynamically adjusting the trust-region and off-policy concerns based on the current batch. Experiments across diverse settings show that the method matches or exceeds tuned baselines while removing several existing hyper-parameters and introducing none new.
大规模模型的强化学习后训练因训练与推理系统间的分布不匹配而脆弱，现有方法通过增加超参数来应对，但需针对任务重新调参。作者提出一种批次自适应目标函数，用策略比率的归一化有效样本量替代固定裁剪，根据当前批次动态调整信任区域和离策略约束。在多种设置下的实验表明，该方法匹配或超越调优基线，同时移除多个现有超参数且不引入新参数。
About Time: Model-free Reinforcement Learning with Timed Reward Machines
Authors: Rajarshi Roy, Anirban Majumdar, Ritam Raha, David Parker, Marta Kwiatkowska
Venue: IJCAI 2026
First: 2025-12-19T14:39:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:44:19+00:00
Comments: Extended version of paper accepted at IJCAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward specification plays a central role in reinforcement learning (RL), guiding the agent's behavior. To express non-Markovian rewards, formalisms such as reward machines have been introduced to capture dependencies on histories. However, traditional reward machines lack the ability to model precise timing constraints, limiting their use in time-sensitive applications. In this paper, we propose timed reward machines (TRMs), which are an extension of reward machines that incorporate timing constraints into the reward structure. TRMs enable more expressive specifications with tunable reward logic, for example, imposing costs for delays and granting rewards for timely actions. We study model-free RL frameworks (i.e., tabular Q-learning) for learning optimal policies with TRMs under digital and real-time semantics. Our algorithms integrate the TRM into learning via abstractions of timed automata, and employ counterfactual-imagining heuristics that exploit the structure of the TRM to improve the search. Experimentally, we demonstrate that our algorithm learns policies that achieve high rewards while satisfying the timing constraints specified by the TRM on popular RL benchmarks. Moreover, we conduct comparative studies of performance under different TRM semantics, along with ablations that highlight the benefits of counterfactual-imagining.
中文标题/摘要
标题：关于时间：基于时间奖励机的无模型强化学习
奖励规范在强化学习中扮演核心角色，引导智能体的行为。为表达非马尔可夫奖励，诸如奖励机等形式化方法被引入以捕捉对历史依赖。然而，传统奖励机缺乏建模精确时间约束的能力，限制了其在时间敏感应用中的使用。本文提出时间奖励机（TRMs），这是对奖励机的扩展，将时间约束融入奖励结构。TRMs通过可调奖励逻辑实现更具表达力的规范，例如对延迟施加成本、对及时行动给予奖励。我们研究了在数字和实时语义下，基于TRMs学习最优策略的无模型强化学习框架（即表格型Q学习）。我们的算法通过时间自动机的抽象将TRM整合到学习中，并采用反事实想象启发式方法，利用TRM结构改进搜索。实验表明，我们的算法在流行强化学习基准上学习到能实现高奖励并满足TRM指定时间约束的策略。此外，我们进行了不同TRM语义下性能的比较研究，以及消融实验，突出了反事实想象的优势。

The authors propose a model-free RL framework using tabular Q-learning, integrating TRMs via abstractions of timed automata and employing counterfactual-imagining heuristics to exploit the TRM structure for improved search. Experimental results on popular RL benchmarks demonstrate that the learned policies achieve high rewards while satisfying the specified timing constraints, with comparative studies under different TRM semantics and ablations confirming the benefits of the counterfactual-imagining approach.

Discrete Flow Matching for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Fairoz Nower Khan, Nabuat Zaman Nahim, Peizhong Ju
First: 2026-05-12T16:44:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:44:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many reinforcement learning (RL) tasks have discrete action spaces, but most generative policy methods based on diffusion and flow matching are designed for continuous control. Meanwhile, generative policies usually rely heavily on offline datasets and offline-to-online RL is itself challenging, as the policy must improve from new interaction without losing useful behavior learned from static data. To address those challenges, we introduce DRIFT, an online fine-tuning method that updates an offline pretrained continuous-time Markov chain (CTMC) policy with an advantage-weighted discrete flow matching loss. To preserve useful pretrained knowledge, we add a path-space penalty that regularizes the full CTMC trajectory distribution, rather than only the final action distribution. For large discrete action spaces, we introduce a candidate-set approximation that updates the actor over a small subset of actions sampled from reference-policy rollouts and uniform exploration. Our theoretical analysis shows that the candidate-set error is controlled by missing target probability mass, and the induced CTMC generator error decreases as the candidate set covers more high-probability actions. Experiments on prevailing discrete action RL task show that our method provides stable offline-to-online improvement across all tasks, achieving the highest average score on Jericho with a simple GRU encoder while outperforming methods that use pretrained language models. Controlled experiments further confirm that the path-space penalty remains bounded during fine-tuning and that the CTMC generator adapts to shifted rewards faster than deterministic baselines. The candidate-set mechanism is supported by a stability analysis showing that the generator error decreases exponentially with candidate coverage.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向离线到在线强化学习的离散流匹配方法
许多强化学习任务具有离散动作空间，但基于扩散和流匹配的生成式策略方法主要针对连续控制设计。同时，生成式策略通常严重依赖离线数据集，而离线到在线强化学习本身具有挑战性，因为策略必须从新交互中改进，同时不丢失从静态数据中学到的有用行为。为应对这些挑战，我们提出DRIFT——一种在线微调方法，通过优势加权离散流匹配损失更新离线预训练的连续时间马尔可夫链策略。为保留有用的预训练知识，我们添加路径空间惩罚项，对完整CTMC轨迹分布进行正则化，而非仅作用于最终动作分布。针对大规模离散动作空间，我们引入候选集近似方法，在从参考策略 rollout 和均匀探索中采样的小动作子集上更新演员网络。理论分析表明，候选集误差受缺失目标概率质量控制，且当候选集覆盖更多高概率动作时，诱导的CTMC生成器误差会降低。在主流离散动作强化学习任务上的实验显示，我们的方法在所有任务中均能实现稳定的离线到在线改进，使用简单GRU编码器在Jericho上取得最高平均分，同时优于使用预训练语言模型的方法。控制实验进一步证实，微调期间路径空间惩罚保持有界，且CTMC生成器比确定性基线更快适应奖励偏移。候选集机制得到稳定性分析支持，表明生成器误差随候选覆盖率呈指数级下降。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenges of applying generative policy methods based on diffusion and flow matching to discrete action spaces in reinforcement learning, as well as the difficulty of offline-to-online RL where policies must improve from new interactions without losing useful offline-learned behavior. The authors propose DRIFT, an online fine-tuning method that updates an offline pretrained continuous-time Markov chain (CTMC) policy using an advantage-weighted discrete flow matching loss, and introduces a path-space penalty to regularize the full CTMC trajectory distribution for preserving pretrained knowledge. For large action spaces, a candidate-set approximation is used to update the actor over a subset of actions. Experiments on discrete action RL tasks show that DRIFT provides stable offline-to-online improvement across all tasks, achieving the highest average score on Jericho with a simple GRU encoder while outperforming methods using pretrained language models, with controlled experiments confirming that the path-space penalty remains bounded and the CTMC generator adapts faster to shifted rewards than deterministic baselines.
该论文针对离散动作空间中强化学习任务难以应用基于扩散和流匹配的生成式策略方法，以及离线到在线强化学习中策略需从新交互中提升而不丢失离线有用行为的问题，提出了DRIFT方法。该方法通过优势加权离散流匹配损失更新离线预训练的连续时间马尔可夫链策略，并引入路径空间惩罚项来正则化整个CTMC轨迹分布以保留预训练知识。对于大离散动作空间，采用候选集近似从参考策略采样和均匀探索中选取动作子集进行更新。实验表明，DRIFT在所有离散动作任务上均实现稳定的离线到在线提升，在Jericho环境中使用简单GRU编码器取得最高平均分，超越使用预训练语言模型的方法，且控制实验证实路径空间惩罚在微调中保持有界，CTMC生成器比确定性基线更快适应奖励变化。
QAP-Router: Tackling Qubit Routing as Dynamic Quadratic Assignment with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Kien X. Nguyen, Ankit Kulshrestha, Ilya Safro, Xiaoyuan Liu
First: 2026-05-12T16:34:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:34:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Qubit routing is a fundamental problem in quantum compilation, known to be NP-hard. Its dynamic nature makes local routing decisions propagate and compound over time, making global efficient solutions challenging. Existing heuristic methods rely on local rules with limited lookahead, while recent learning-based approaches often treat routing as a generic sequential decision problem without fully exploiting its underlying structure. In this paper, we introduce QAP-Router, framing qubit routing based on a dynamic Quadratic Assignment Problem (QAP) formulation. By modeling logical interactions, or quantum gates, as flow matrices and hardware topology as a distance matrix, our approach captures the interaction-distance coupling in a unified objective, which defines the reward in the reinforcement learning environment. To further exploit this structure, the policy network employs a solution-aware Transformer backbone that encodes the interaction between the flow matrix and the distance matrix into the attention mechanism. We also integrate a lookahead mechanism that blends naturally into the QAP framework, preventing myopic decisions. Extensive experiments on 1,831 real-world quantum circuits from the MQTBench, AgentQ and QUEKO datasets show that our method substantially reduces the CNOT gate count of routed circuits by 15.7%, 30.4% and 12.1%, respectively, relative to existing industry compilers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QAP-Router：基于强化学习将量子比特路由建模为动态二次分配问题
量子比特路由是量子编译中的基础问题，已知为NP难问题。其动态特性使得局部路由决策随时间传播和累积，导致全局高效解决方案极具挑战性。现有启发式方法依赖有限前瞻的局部规则，而近期基于学习的方法常将路由视为通用序列决策问题，未能充分利用其内在结构。本文提出QAP-Router，基于动态二次分配问题（QAP）框架对量子比特路由进行建模。通过将逻辑交互（即量子门）建模为流矩阵，将硬件拓扑建模为距离矩阵，我们的方法在统一目标中捕捉交互-距离耦合，该目标定义了强化学习环境中的奖励。为进一步利用该结构，策略网络采用解感知Transformer骨干网络，将流矩阵与距离矩阵的交互编码至注意力机制中。我们还整合了自然融入QAP框架的前瞻机制，避免短视决策。在来自MQTBench、AgentQ和QUEKO数据集的1,831个真实量子电路上的大量实验表明，相对于现有工业编译器，我们的方法分别将路由电路的CNOT门数量减少了15.7%、30.4%和12.1%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the NP-hard qubit routing problem in quantum compilation, where local decisions propagate and compound over time, making global optimization difficult. The authors propose QAP-Router, which formulates qubit routing as a dynamic Quadratic Assignment Problem (QAP), modeling logical gates as flow matrices and hardware topology as a distance matrix, with the unified objective defining the reward in a reinforcement learning environment. The policy network uses a solution-aware Transformer backbone that encodes flow-distance interactions into the attention mechanism, integrated with a lookahead mechanism to avoid myopic decisions. Experiments on 1,831 real-world quantum circuits from MQTBench, AgentQ, and QUEKO datasets show that QAP-Router reduces CNOT gate counts by 15.7%, 30.4%, and 12.1%, respectively, compared to existing industry compilers.
该论文针对量子编译中NP难的量子比特路由问题，其中局部决策会随时间传播和累积，使得全局优化困难。作者提出QAP-Router，将量子比特路由建模为动态二次分配问题（QAP），以逻辑门作为流矩阵、硬件拓扑作为距离矩阵，统一目标函数定义强化学习环境中的奖励。策略网络采用基于解决方案的Transformer骨干网络，将流矩阵与距离矩阵的交互编码到注意力机制中，并集成前瞻机制以避免短视决策。在来自MQTBench、AgentQ和QUEKO数据集的1831个真实量子电路上的实验表明，相比现有行业编译器，QAP-Router分别将CNOT门数量减少了15.7%、30.4%和12.1%。
A Family of Quaternion-Valued Differential Evolution Algorithms for Numerical Function Optimization
Authors: Gerardo Altamirano-Gomez, Álvaro Gallardo, Carlos Ignacio Hernández Castellanos
First: 2026-05-12T16:32:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:32:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The numerical optimization of continuous functions is a fundamental task in many scientific and engineering domains, ranging from mechanical design to training of artificial intelligence models. Among the most effective and widely used algorithms for this purpose is Differential Evolution (DE), known for its simplicity and strong performance. Recent research has shown that adapting AI models to operate over alternative number systems-such as complex numbers, quaternions, and geometric algebras-can improve model compactness and accuracy. However, such extensions remain underexplored in bio-inspired optimization algorithms. In particular, the use of quaternion algebra represents an emerging area in computational intelligence. This paper introduces a family of novel Quaternion-Valued Differential Evolution (QDE) algorithms that operate directly in the quaternion space. We propose several mutation strategies specifically designed to exploit the algebraic and geometric properties of quaternions. Results show that our QDE variants achieve faster convergence and superior performance on several function classes in the BBOB benchmark compared to the traditional real-valued DE algorithm.

标题：面向数值函数优化的四元数差分进化算法族

BSO: Safety Alignment Is Density Ratio Matching
Authors: Tien-Phat Nguyen, Truong Nguyen, Thin Nguyen, Duy Minh Ho Nguyen, Ngoc-Thanh Dinh, Trung Le
First: 2026-05-12T16:19:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:19:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning language models for both helpfulness and safety typically requires complex pipelines-separate reward and cost models, online reinforcement learning, and primal-dual updates. Recent direct preference optimization approaches simplify training but incorporate safety through ad-hoc modifications such as multi-stage procedures or heuristic margin terms, lacking a principled derivation. We show that the likelihood ratio of the optimal safe policy admits a closed-form decomposition that reduces safety alignment to a density ratio matching problem. Minimizing Bregman divergences between the data and model ratios yields Bregman Safety Optimization (BSO), a family of single-stage loss functions, each induced by a convex generator, that provably recover the optimal safe policy. BSO is both general and simple: it requires no auxiliary models, introduces only one hyperparameter beyond standard preference optimization, and recovers existing safety-aware methods as special cases. Experiments across safety alignment benchmarks show that BSO consistently improves the safety-helpfulness trade-off.

标题：BSO：安全对齐即密度比匹配
对齐语言模型以实现有用性和安全性通常需要复杂的流程——分离的奖励和成本模型、在线强化学习以及原始-对偶更新。最近的直接偏好优化方法简化了训练，但通过临时修改（如多阶段流程或启发式边际项）来融入安全性，缺乏原则性的推导。我们证明最优安全策略的似然比具有封闭形式的分解，将安全对齐简化为密度比匹配问题。最小化数据和模型比率之间的布雷格曼散度，得到布雷格曼安全优化（BSO），这是一族由凸生成元诱导的单阶段损失函数，可证明地恢复最优安全策略。BSO既通用又简单：无需辅助模型，在标准偏好优化之外仅引入一个超参数，并将现有的安全感知方法作为特例恢复。跨安全对齐基准的实验表明，BSO持续改善了安全-有用性权衡。

The authors propose Bregman Safety Optimization (BSO), a method that reduces safety alignment to a density ratio matching problem by showing that the likelihood ratio of the optimal safe policy admits a closed-form decomposition. BSO is a family of single-stage loss functions that requires no auxiliary models and introduces only one hyperparameter beyond standard preference optimization. Experimental results across safety alignment benchmarks demonstrate that BSO consistently improves the safety-helpfulness trade-off compared to existing methods.

Manifold Sampling via Entropy Maximization
Authors: Cornelius V. Braun, Tilman Burghoff, Marc Toussaint
First: 2026-05-12T16:19:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:19:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sampling from constrained distributions has a wide range of applications, including in Bayesian optimization and robotics. Prior work establishes convergence and feasibility guarantees for constrained sampling, but assumes that the feasible set is connected. However, in practice, the feasible set often decomposes into multiple disconnected components, which makes efficient sampling under constraints challenging. In this paper, we propose MAnifold Sampling via Entropy Maximization (MASEM) for sampling on a manifold with an unknown number of disconnected components, implicitly defined by smooth equality and inequality constraints. The presented method uses a resampling scheme to maximize the entropy of the empirical distribution based on k-nearest neighbor density estimation. We show that, in the mean field, MASEM decreases the KL-divergence between the empirical distribution and the maximum-entropy target exponentially in the number of resampling steps. We instantiate MASEM with multiple local samplers and demonstrate its versatility and efficiency on synthetic and robotics-based benchmarks. MASEM enables fast and scalable mixing across a range of constrained sampling problems, improving over alternatives by an order of magnitude in Sinkhorn distance with competitive runtime.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sampling from constrained distributions when the feasible set consists of multiple disconnected components, a scenario where prior methods fail due to their assumption of connectivity. The authors propose MASEM, a method that maximizes the entropy of the empirical distribution via a resampling scheme using k-nearest neighbor density estimation, effectively handling an unknown number of disconnected components defined by smooth constraints. Theoretically, they prove that MASEM reduces the KL-divergence to the maximum-entropy target exponentially with resampling steps. Experimentally, on synthetic and robotics benchmarks, MASEM demonstrates fast mixing and outperforms alternatives by an order of magnitude in Sinkhorn distance with competitive runtime.
该论文针对可行集由多个不连通分量组成时约束分布采样的难题，提出了一种名为MASEM的方法。该方法通过基于k近邻密度估计的重采样方案最大化经验分布的熵，从而有效处理由光滑等式和不等式约束隐式定义的不连通分量。理论上证明了在平均场下，MASEM能使经验分布与最大熵目标之间的KL散度随重采样步数呈指数级下降。在合成和机器人基准测试中，MASEM实现了快速混合，并在Sinkhorn距离上比现有方法提升一个数量级，同时保持有竞争力的运行时间。
Reinforcing VLAs in Task-Agnostic World Models
Authors: Yucen Wang, Rui Yu, Fengming Zhang, Junjie Lu, Xinyao Qin, Tianxiang Zhang, Kaixin Wang, Li Zhao
First: 2026-05-12T16:16:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:16:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models via reinforcement learning (RL) in learned world models has emerged as an effective strategy to adapt to new tasks without costly real-world interactions. However, while using imagined trajectories reduces the sample complexity of policy training, existing methods still heavily rely on task-specific data to fine-tune both the world and reward models, fundamentally limiting their scalability to unseen tasks. To overcome this, we argue that world and reward models should capture transferable physical priors that enable zero-shot inference. We propose RAW-Dream (Reinforcing VLAs in task-Agnostic World Dreams), a new paradigm that completely disentangles world model learning from downstream task dependencies. RAW-Dream utilizes a world model pre-trained on diverse task-free behaviors for predicting future rollouts, and an off-the-shelf Vision-Language Model (VLM) for reward generation. Because both components are task-agnostic, VLAs can be readily finetuned for any new task entirely within this zero-shot imagination. Furthermore, to mitigate world model hallucinations, we introduce a dual-noise verification mechanism to filter out unreliable rollouts. Extensive experiments across simulation and real-world settings demonstrate consistent performance gains, proving that generalized physical priors can effectively substitute for costly task-dependent data, offering a highly scalable roadmap for VLA adaptation.

Black-Box Optimization of Mixed Binary-Continuous Variables: Challenges and Opportunities in Evolutionary Model Merging
Authors: Md. Robiul Islam Niloy
First: 2026-05-12T16:08:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T16:08:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model merging has emerged as a cost-effective alternative to training large language models (LLMs) from scratch, enabling researchers to combine pre-trained models into more capable systems without full retraining. Evolutionary approaches to model merging have shown particular promise, automatically searching for optimal merging configurations across both parameter space (PS) and data flow space (DFS). However, the optimization challenges underlying these approaches -- particularly in DFS merging -- remain poorly understood and formally underspecified in the literature. This paper makes two contributions. First, we provide a structured survey of evolutionary model merging techniques, organizing them into three categories: parameter-space merging, data flow space merging, and hybrid approaches. Second, we formally characterize the DFS merging problem as a black-box optimization problem involving mixed binary-continuous variables, high-dimensional search spaces, and conditional dependencies between variable types -- challenges that standard optimization methods such as CMA-ES are not designed to handle. We provide preliminary empirical validation using real pre-trained language models, demonstrating that a structured approach respecting the binary-continuous conditional dependency outperforms an unstructured approach by 6.7% accuracy while reducing the effective search space by 51.4%. By connecting the model merging community with the broader evolutionary computation and black-box optimization literature, we identify concrete open problems and propose research directions to address them.

Transferable Delay-Aware Reinforcement Learning via Implicit Causal Graph Modeling
Authors: Chenran Zhao, Dianxi Shi, Yaowen Zhang, Chunping Qiu, Shaowu Yang
First: 2026-05-12T15:58:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T15:58:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Random delays weaken the temporal correspondence between actions and subsequent state feedback, making it difficult for agents to identify the true propagation process of action effects. In cross-task scenarios, changes in task objectives and reward formulations further reduce the reusability of previously acquired task knowledge. To address this problem, this paper proposes a transferable delay-aware reinforcement learning method based on implicit causal graph modeling. The proposed method uses a field-node encoder to represent high-dimensional observations as latent states with node-level semantics, and employs a message-passing mechanism to characterize dynamic causal dependencies among nodes, thereby learning transferable structured representations and environment dynamics knowledge. On this basis, imagination-driven behavior learning and planning are incorporated to optimize policies in the latent space, enabling cross-task knowledge transfer and rapid adaptation. Experimental results show that the proposed method outperforms baseline methods on DMC continuous control tasks with random delays. Cross-task transfer experiments further demonstrate that the learned structured representations and dynamics knowledge can be effectively transferred to new tasks and significantly accelerate policy adaptation.
