PriorZero: Bridging Language Priors and World Models for Decision Making
Authors: Junyu Xiong, Yuan Pu, Jia Tang, Yazhe Niu
First: 2026-05-12T15:47:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T15:47:18+00:00
Comments: 30 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Leveraging the rich world knowledge of Large Language Models (LLMs) to enhance Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents offers a promising path toward general intelligence. However, a fundamental prior-dynamics mismatch hinders existing approaches: static LLM knowledge cannot directly adapt to the complex transition dynamics of long-horizon tasks. Using LLM priors as fixed policies limits exploration diversity, as the prior is blind to environment-specific dynamics; while end-to-end fine-tuning suffers from optimization instability and credit assignment issues. To bridge this gap, we propose PriorZero, a unified framework that integrates LLM-derived conceptual priors into world-model-based planning through a decoupled rollout-training design. During rollout, a novel root-prior injection mechanism incorporates LLM priors exclusively at the root node of Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS), focusing search on semantically promising actions while preserving the world model's deep lookahead capability. During training, PriorZero decouples world-model learning from LLM adaptation: the world model is continuously refined on interaction data to jointly improve its dynamics, policy, and value predictions, its value estimates are then leveraged to provide fine-grained credit assignment signals for stable LLM fine-tuning via alternating optimization. Experiments across diverse benchmarks, including text-based adventure games in Jericho and instruction-following gridworld tasks in BabyAI, demonstrate that PriorZero consistently improves both exploration efficiency and asymptotic performance, establishing a promising framework for LLM-empowered decision-making. Our code is available at https://github.com/opendilab/LightZero.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PriorZero：弥合语言先验与世界模型在决策中的鸿沟
利用大型语言模型（LLM）丰富的世界知识来增强强化学习（RL）智能体，为实现通用智能提供了一条有前景的路径。然而，根本性的先验-动态不匹配阻碍了现有方法：静态的LLM知识无法直接适应长时域任务的复杂转移动态。将LLM先验用作固定策略会限制探索多样性，因为先验对环境特定的动态视而不见；而端到端微调则面临优化不稳定和信用分配问题。为弥合这一差距，我们提出PriorZero，一个通过解耦的推演-训练设计将LLM衍生的概念先验整合到基于世界模型的规划中的统一框架。在推演过程中，一种新颖的根节点先验注入机制仅在蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的根节点处融入LLM先验，将搜索聚焦于语义上有希望的动作，同时保留世界模型的深度前瞻能力。在训练过程中，PriorZero将世界模型学习与LLM适应解耦：世界模型在交互数据上持续精炼，以联合改进其动态、策略和值预测，然后利用其值估计通过交替优化为稳定的LLM微调提供细粒度的信用分配信号。在包括Jericho中基于文本的冒险游戏和BabyAI中指令跟随网格世界任务在内的多种基准测试中的实验表明，PriorZero持续提高了探索效率和渐近性能，为LLM赋能的决策制定建立了一个有前景的框架。我们的代码可在https://github.com/opendilab/LightZero获取。
Summary / 总结
PriorZero addresses the prior-dynamics mismatch between Large Language Models (LLMs) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents, where static LLM knowledge fails to adapt to complex long-horizon tasks. The method introduces a decoupled rollout-training design: during rollout, a root-prior injection mechanism integrates LLM priors only at the root node of Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) to guide search toward semantically promising actions while preserving the world model's lookahead capability; during training, the world model is refined on interaction data, and its value estimates provide credit assignment signals for stable LLM fine-tuning via alternating optimization. Experiments on Jericho text-based games and BabyAI gridworld tasks show that PriorZero consistently improves both exploration efficiency and asymptotic performance.
PriorZero旨在解决大语言模型（LLM）与强化学习（RL）智能体之间的先验-动态不匹配问题，即静态的LLM知识无法适应复杂的长时域任务动态。该方法采用解耦的展开-训练设计：在展开阶段，通过根节点先验注入机制仅在蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的根节点融入LLM先验，引导搜索聚焦于语义上有希望的动作，同时保留世界模型的深度前瞻能力；在训练阶段，世界模型基于交互数据持续优化，其价值估计为LLM的稳定微调提供细粒度信用分配信号。在Jericho文本冒险游戏和BabyAI指令跟随网格世界任务上的实验表明，PriorZero在探索效率和渐近性能上均取得一致提升。
Self-Consolidating Language Models: Continual Knowledge Incorporation from Context
Authors: Zekun Wang, Anant Gupta, Zihan Dong, Christopher J. MacLellan
First: 2026-05-08T00:50:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T15:47:00+00:00
Comments: 9 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) increasingly receive information as streams of passages, conversations, and long-context workflows. While longer context windows expose more evidence, they do not ensure that useful information is preserved and reused. We study continual context consolidation: writing current context into model weights while limiting interference with previously consolidated information. We propose \textbf{S}elf-\textbf{Co}nsolidating \textbf{L}anguage Models (SCoL), a post-training framework in which, given current context, an LLM learns to generate textual update instructions specifying which of its own Transformer layers should be updated. Because committed updates change the model that later generates future selections, we train SCoL with meta-reinforcement learning over an evolving model state. We instantiate SCoL with supervised QA rewards on SQuAD knowledge incorporation and intrinsic likelihood-based rewards for LongBench v2 long-context consolidation. Across both settings, SCoL improves acquisition and retention over prompting, summarization, batch test-time training, and sequential finetuning baselines. Analysis of learned selection patterns shows that SCoL encourages the LLM to generate sparse update locations that align with layers of high Fisher information, suggesting that the model learns to route plasticity toward loss-sensitive regions while limiting interference. Moreover, SCoL transfers from shorter meta-training streams to longer LongBench v2 streams at evaluation, suggesting that our framework supports scalable streaming consolidation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自巩固语言模型：从上下文中持续整合知识
大型语言模型（LLMs）日益以段落、对话和长上下文工作流的形式接收信息。虽然更长的上下文窗口能暴露更多证据，但并不能确保有用信息被保留和重用。我们研究持续上下文巩固：将当前上下文写入模型权重，同时限制与先前巩固信息的干扰。我们提出自巩固语言模型（SCoL），这是一种后训练框架，其中给定当前上下文，LLM学习生成文本更新指令，指定应更新其自身的哪些Transformer层。由于已提交的更新会改变后续生成未来选择的模型，我们通过元强化学习在演化模型状态上训练SCoL。我们在SQuAD知识整合上使用监督式问答奖励，在LongBench v2长上下文巩固上使用基于内在似然的奖励来实例化SCoL。在这两种设置下，SCoL在获取和保留方面均优于提示、摘要、批量测试时训练和顺序微调基线。对学习选择模式的分析表明，SCoL鼓励LLM生成稀疏的更新位置，这些位置与高Fisher信息的层对齐，表明模型学会将可塑性引导至损失敏感区域，同时限制干扰。此外，SCoL从较短的元训练流迁移到评估时更长的LongBench v2流，表明我们的框架支持可扩展的流式巩固。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of enabling large language models to continually consolidate knowledge from context into their weights without catastrophic interference. The authors propose Self-Consolidating Language Models (SCoL), a post-training framework where the LLM learns to generate textual update instructions that specify which Transformer layers to modify, using meta-reinforcement learning to handle the evolving model state. Experiments on SQuAD and LongBench v2 show that SCoL outperforms baselines like prompting and sequential finetuning in both knowledge acquisition and retention, with learned update patterns aligning with layers of high Fisher information, and it successfully transfers from shorter to longer streams.
该论文针对大型语言模型在持续从上下文中整合知识到模型权重时避免灾难性干扰的问题。作者提出了自我巩固语言模型（SCoL），这是一个后训练框架，其中LLM学习生成文本更新指令，指定要修改的Transformer层，并通过元强化学习处理不断变化的模型状态。在SQuAD和LongBench v2上的实验表明，SCoL在知识获取和保留方面优于提示、摘要和顺序微调等基线方法，学习到的更新模式与高Fisher信息层对齐，并且能够从较短的元训练流成功迁移到较长的评估流。
Delay-Empowered Causal Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chenran Zhao, Dianxi Shi, Haotian Wang, Mengzhu Wang, Yaowen Zhang, Chunping Qiu, Shaowu Yang
First: 2026-05-12T15:28:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T15:28:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many real-world tasks involve delayed effects, where the outcomes of actions emerge after varying time lags. Existing delay-aware reinforcement learning methods often rely on state augmentation, prior knowledge of delay distributions, or access to non-delayed data, limiting their generalization. Hierarchical reinforcement learning, by contrast, inherently offers advantages in handling delays due to its hierarchical structure, yet existing methods are restricted to fixed delays. To address these limitations, we propose Delay-Empowered Causal Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (DECHRL). DECHRL explicitly models both the causal structure of state transitions and their associated stochastic delay distributions. These are then incorporated into a delay-aware empowerment objective that drives proactive exploration toward highly controllable states, thereby improving performance under temporal uncertainty. We evaluate DECHRL in modified 2D-Minecraft and MiniGrid environments featuring stochastic delays. Experimental results show that DECHRL effectively models temporal delays and significantly outperforms baselines in decision-making under temporal uncertainty.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of delayed effects in reinforcement learning, where existing methods struggle due to reliance on state augmentation or prior delay knowledge. The authors propose Delay-Empowered Causal Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (DECHRL), which explicitly models causal state transitions and stochastic delay distributions, integrating them into a delay-aware empowerment objective to encourage proactive exploration of controllable states. Experiments in modified 2D-Minecraft and MiniGrid environments with stochastic delays show that DECHRL effectively captures temporal delays and significantly outperforms baseline methods in decision-making under temporal uncertainty.
该论文针对强化学习中动作结果存在随机延迟的问题，现有方法依赖状态增强或延迟分布先验知识，泛化能力有限。作者提出延迟赋能因果分层强化学习（DECHRL），通过显式建模状态转移的因果结构及其随机延迟分布，并将其融入延迟感知的赋能目标，驱动智能体主动探索高可控状态。在具有随机延迟的改进版2D-Minecraft和MiniGrid环境中的实验表明，DECHRL能有效建模时间延迟，并在时间不确定性下的决策任务中显著优于基线方法。
TMRL: Diffusion Timestep-Modulated Pretraining Enables Exploration for Efficient Policy Finetuning
Authors: Matthew M. Hong, Jesse Zhang, Anusha Nagabandi, Abhishek Gupta
First: 2026-05-12T15:07:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T15:07:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Fine-tuning pre-trained robot policies with reinforcement learning (RL) often inherits the bottlenecks introduced by pre-training with behavioral cloning (BC), which produces narrow action distributions that lack the coverage necessary for downstream exploration. We present a unified framework that enables the exploration necessary to enable efficient robot policy finetuning by bridging BC pre-training and RL fine-tuning. Our pre-training method, Context-Smoothed Pre-training (CSP), injects forward-diffusion noise into policy inputs, creating a continuum between precise imitation and broad action coverage. We then fine-tune pre-trained policies via Timestep-Modulated Reinforcement Learning (TMRL), which trains the agent to dynamically adjust this conditioning during fine-tuning by modulating the diffusion timestep, granting explicit control over exploration. Integrating seamlessly with arbitrary policy inputs, e.g., states, 3D point clouds, or image-based VLA policies, we show that TMRL improves RL fine-tuning sample efficiency. Notably, TMRL enables successful real-world fine-tuning on complex manipulation tasks in under one hour. Videos and code available at https://weirdlabuw.github.io/tmrl/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TMRL：扩散时间步调制预训练助力高效策略微调中的探索
使用强化学习（RL）微调预训练机器人策略通常会继承行为克隆（BC）预训练引入的瓶颈，即产生狭窄的动作分布，缺乏下游探索所需的覆盖范围。我们提出一个统一框架，通过桥接BC预训练和RL微调，实现高效机器人策略微调所需的探索。我们的预训练方法——上下文平滑预训练（CSP）——将前向扩散噪声注入策略输入，在精确模仿与广泛动作覆盖之间创建连续体。随后，我们通过时间步调制强化学习（TMRL）微调预训练策略，该方法训练智能体在微调期间通过调制扩散时间步动态调整此条件，从而实现对探索的显式控制。TMRL与任意策略输入（如状态、3D点云或基于图像的VLA策略）无缝集成，我们证明TMRL能提升RL微调的样本效率。值得注意的是，TMRL可在不到一小时内实现复杂操作任务的真实世界微调。视频和代码见https://weirdlabuw.github.io/tmrl/。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces TMRL, a framework designed to address the exploration bottleneck in fine-tuning robot policies pre-trained with behavioral cloning, which typically results in narrow action distributions. The method proposes Context-Smoothed Pre-training (CSP) that adds forward-diffusion noise to policy inputs, creating a spectrum from precise imitation to broad action coverage, and then uses Timestep-Modulated Reinforcement Learning (TMRL) to dynamically adjust the diffusion timestep during fine-tuning for controlled exploration. Experimental results demonstrate that TMRL improves sample efficiency across various policy inputs, including states, 3D point clouds, and image-based VLA policies, and enables successful real-world fine-tuning on complex manipulation tasks in under one hour.
该论文提出了TMRL框架，旨在解决通过行为克隆预训练的机器人策略在微调时因动作分布狭窄而导致的探索瓶颈问题。方法包括上下文平滑预训练（CSP），通过向策略输入添加前向扩散噪声，在精确模仿和广泛动作覆盖之间建立连续谱，然后使用时序调制强化学习（TMRL）在微调过程中动态调整扩散时间步，以实现可控探索。实验结果表明，TMRL在状态、3D点云和基于图像的VLA策略等多种输入上提高了微调样本效率，并能在不到一小时内完成复杂操作任务的真实世界微调。
